## 2026-06-11: DYNAMIC TYPE + VOICEOVER PASS: final polish wave 5/5 (iOS-only polish, LOCAL, not built; next-build stack)

**Status:** ✅ iOS code ready + verified LOCALLY. `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 9.5 MB). NOT built / NOT submitted / NO `eas update` (build-on-command). One commit on iOS `main` (`d2b7461`), not pushed. NO new packages. No em-dashes. Owner: `vp-ios`. Closes the 5-item polish wave (juice `df2ba51`, broken-edges, OTA `00970db`, states `a3bb04d`/`8e1929e`, this).

**Dynamic Type policy (implemented):** the app never disables font scaling, so content text (questions, notes, chat, settings labels, body copy) scales freely with the OS setting; layout-critical text inside fixed chrome is capped at `maxFontSizeMultiplier` 1.2 (stat orbs, tab-bar labels, wallet 64pt hero balance, leaderboard rank column, level-up/streak hero numerals, quiz difficulty letter, all live round timers) and 1.4 on settings segment pills. Target: usable and unbroken at 1.4x; max accessibility sizes deliberately not chased on fixed chrome.

**VoiceOver:** settings ToggleRow = ONE switch (role + checked state + activate action; sighted tap behavior unchanged) and every settings save toast is announced; SketchCanvas announces it is a LIVE drawing + who is drawing; Sketchy word-progress blanks, party lobby roster rows, leaderboard rows + podium stands, and arena match-history rows all grouped into single composed elements (were letter-soup); quiz/arena/Daily Drill answer options get role + state + reveal feedback ("Correct answer" / "Incorrect" / "Eliminated by Brain Freeze"); celebrations split decorative-vs-announced (CelebrationBurst + FangPop hidden from the tree; LevelUpOverlay/StreakMilestoneOverlay/ClockInToast announce + labeled dismiss); 14 icon-only Pressables labeled repo-wide (password eyes, Timeline chevrons, nudge/revive dismissals, NotificationBell with unread count, modal closes, SegmentedControl selected state).

**Web counterpart:** 🚫 no port needed (native accessibility semantics; web has its own aria pass). **Web NUDGE for `admin`, informational:** the grouped-row pattern (leaderboard/match/friend rows as one labeled element) and the announced save-toast are worth a one-time web aria-live/role audit on the same surfaces.

**Device QA debt, on the record:** VoiceOver + 1.4x walkthroughs need a physical device; the 6-case plan is in iOS `docs/CHANGELOG.md` and rides the next build. ToggleRow's accessibility activate action is the one item to verify first on-device.

**Sign-offs:** `ios-design-accessibility` (LEAD: policy + audit + label spec - PASS) · `ios-dev-components` + `ios-dev-screens` (35 files, labels/roles/caps only, zero visual change at default text size - PASS) · `ios-design-motion` (reduce-motion paths untouched: burst static-flash, skeleton pulse, OTA fades, tab limelight - PASS) · `ios-qa-tester` (6-case device plan; stash-compare lint baseline = 0 new errors, 2 new hook-deps warnings fixed) · `ios-code-reviewer` (caught + fixed a "Close results" label on the in-quiz close; PASS) · `ios-docs-writer` (iOS CHANGELOG + vault Daily) · `ios-parity-tracker` (this row).

## 2026-06-11: STATES SWEEP: empty/loading/error kit + honest offline behavior (iOS-only polish, LOCAL, not built)

**Status:** ✅ iOS code ready + verified LOCALLY. `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 9.49 MB, single bundle). NOT built / NOT submitted / NO `eas update` (build-on-command). Three commits on iOS `main` (`a3bb04d` kit, `8e1929e` sweep, `8751cdc` docs), not pushed. NO new packages. No em-dashes in user-facing copy. Owner: `vp-ios`. Polish item 2/5.

**What:** Shared state kit at `components/states/` (SkeletonBlock with reduce-motion-safe pulse, ErrorState with 44pt Retry wired to SWR `mutate`, existing EmptyState upgraded with a `compact` variant + CTA button role). Sweep killed the cold-cache offline-lie class: leaderboard ("no one's on the board yet"), notifications ("All caught up"), wallet ("no activity yet"), social (skeleton-forever via the `hydrated` gate), academia ("add your first class"), mastery; each now distinguishes loading vs error vs genuinely empty. New-user dashboard gets a FirstQuizCard ("Take a quiz" CTA) where RecentActivityCard used to render null.

**Web counterpart:** 🚫 no port needed (iOS-side hardening of surfaces web already handles per-page). **Web NUDGE for `admin`, informational:** worth a one-time web audit of the same lie class: any web surface whose SWR error + cold cache falls into "empty" copy (web has the same `shouldRetryOnError`-style risk on first-load failures).

**Offline gap, on the record:** `@react-native-community/netinfo` NOT installed (native module, would need a binary build + package approval). iOS offline handling is fetch-failure-driven ErrorStates over cached-data persistence, not a proactive offline banner. Revisit at the next binary build window if Sam wants the banner.

Owner: `vp-ios`.

**Web vocabulary analyzed first:** `components/Confetti.tsx` (trigger-edge API, prefers-reduced-motion skip, gold-led palette) fires at dashboard daily-claim + bet-win (`app/dashboard/page.tsx`), quiz >=80% results (`app/quiz/page.tsx`), Sketchy FIRST-correct (`components/party/SketchView.tsx`), Daily Drill complete. iOS had celebration only on quiz-perfect + the two global overlays.

**What shipped (iOS):** (A) NEW `components/CelebrationBurst.tsx`, the web-Confetti counterpart: Reanimated gold-Fang particle burst, ~1s, transform/opacity only (GPU), `trigger` edge API, reduce-motion = static gold glow (opacity-only) via useReducedMotion + AccessibilityInfo listener. Mounted at daily-claim toast (`ClockInToast`), Sketchy first-correct over the canvas (guesser locally + drawer/others via the GUESS broadcast gate), quiz results when the streak-milestone or 3-in-a-row banner shows, Trivia reveal on correct+speed-bonus, and `LevelUpOverlay`. (B) NEW `lib/haptics.ts`: tap (impact Light) / success (impact Medium) / milestone (notification Success) / warning / error; all 252 raw expo-haptics call sites across ~70 files normalized to the five verbs (`app/onboarding.tsx` + `app/edit-profile.tsx` deliberately skipped, agent-owned right now). (C) Reduce-motion debt paid: `StreakMilestoneOverlay` halo+flames (doc claimed gating, code never had it), quiz perfect halo+particles, `LevelUpOverlay` halo now gate.

**Web counterpart:** ✅ web already celebrates at all five moments (that is what iOS just matched). 🚫 haptic vocabulary is native-only by definition (no web counterpart; web's equivalent feedback is the motion itself). One web nudge for `admin`/`design-motion-web`: web's Trivia (party) reveal has no correct+fast confetti, iOS now celebrates a moment web does not; consider mirroring.

**Sign-offs:** `ios-design-motion` (burst spec, palette, haptic scale) · `ios-design-accessibility` (reduce-motion paths, pointerEvents none, SR announcements untouched) · `ios-qa-tester` (8-case plan in iOS `docs/CHANGELOG.md`; device pass rides the next build) · `ios-code-reviewer` (stash-compare lint baseline = 0 new findings; 10 ternary haptic sites hand-mapped) · `ios-docs-writer` (iOS CHANGELOG + vault Daily) · `ios-parity-tracker` (this row).

## 2026-06-11: BROKEN-EDGES bundle: avatar upload + native DOB wheel + onboarding prefill (iOS, LOCAL, not built; next-build stack)

**Status:** ✅ iOS code ready + verified LOCALLY. `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors** after each fix. `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 9.5 MB, single bundle). NOT built / NOT submitted / NO `eas update` (build-on-command). Three commits on iOS `main` (`afe33ca` avatar upload, `8065297` DOB wheel, `5051b99` prefill), not pushed. **ONE approved new package: `@react-native-community/datetimepicker` 8.4.4, a NATIVE MODULE that requires the NEXT binary build** (config plugin auto-added to `app.json`; older dev clients cannot render onboarding step 2 after `8065297`). No em-dashes. Owner: `vp-ios`.

**What shipped (iOS):** (A) `app/edit-profile.tsx` avatar upload now works against the live `avatars` bucket (public-read, 5MB, jpeg/png/webp, owner-folder RLS): object path moved to `avatars/${userId}/avatar.<ext>` to satisfy the owner-folder policy, bytes via `arrayBuffer` instead of the RN Blob polyfill (0-byte-upload trap), contentType from the picker's `mimeType` normalized to the bucket allow-list, distinct graceful-failure toasts (unreadable / >5MB / bucket missing / RLS rejection / network), stale-extension cleanup on re-upload, and "Remove photo" now clears the storage object. (B) `app/onboarding.tsx` step 2: typed YYYY-MM-DD field replaced with the native iOS date wheel (spinner, dark, max = today, seeded ~16y ago); >=13 gate + persistence (auth `user_metadata` + `profiles.preferences`) unchanged. (C) onboarding resume/prefill no longer SELECTs the dead `profiles.first_name` column; name/DOB/referral read back from auth metadata + `preferences` JSONB, so resumed onboarding round-trips them.

**Web counterpart:** (A) web's avatar upload (profile page) targets the same `avatars` bucket: 🟡 **web team must verify its object path starts with `${userId}/` too**, or web uploads hit the same RLS rejection iOS just fixed. Flag for `admin`/`dev-frontend`. (B) 🚫 native wheel is iOS-native UX; web keeps its date input. (C) web onboarding does not read `profiles.first_name` (web writes name/DOB to auth metadata at signUp); no web change.

**Sign-offs:** `ios-security-auth` + `ios-security-auditor` (owner-folder path enforced; live bucket probe; no user-controllable path segments - PASS) · `ios-design-hig` + `ios-design-accessibility` (native wheel is the HIG control; UIPickerView VoiceOver-native) · `ios-qa-tester` (7-case plan in iOS `docs/CHANGELOG.md`; wheel device pass rides the next build) · `ios-code-reviewer` (PASS; caught a toISOString timezone day-shift, fixed via local toYMD) · `ios-docs-writer` (iOS CHANGELOG `d34940b` + vault Daily) · `ios-parity-tracker` (this row).

## 2026-06-11: OTA "update ready" toast + app icon badge hygiene (iOS-only, LOCAL, not built; next-build stack)

**Status:** ✅ iOS code ready + verified LOCALLY. `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. eslint 0 errors on touched files (pre-existing `_layout.tsx` `import/first` warnings only). `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 9.49 MB). Pure JS, but the toast itself only becomes observable once a TestFlight build + a published EAS Update exist (OTA is disabled in dev by design). NOT built / NOT submitted / NO `eas update` (build-on-command). Committed on iOS `main`, not pushed. NO new npm packages (expo-updates + expo-notifications were already installed). No em-dashes. Owner: `vp-ios`.

**The gaps (both iOS-only by nature):** (1) published EAS Updates applied only on the next cold launch; an active tester could run a stale JS bundle for days. (2) `shouldSetBadge: true` let pushes mark the app icon but nothing ever cleared it; the badge stuck forever once set.

**What shipped (iOS):** `lib/ota-updates.ts` (NEW `useOtaUpdateReady()`: check on cold start + every AppState "active" with 60s throttle + in-flight guard; hard no-op in `__DEV__` / `Updates.isEnabled === false` since the check throws there; background `fetchUpdateAsync` BEFORE surfacing so Restart is instant; module-level once-per-session token consumed by dismiss/restart, never by suppression) + `components/OtaUpdateBanner.tsx` (NEW small non-blocking top toast, ClockInToast visual language: "Update ready / Restart to apply", 44pt Restart -> `Updates.reloadAsync()`, dismiss at 46pt effective, VoiceOver announce + labeled buttons, reduce-motion = pure fades, no auto-dismiss). **Live-game suppression:** route watch via `useSegments()` holds the banner on `/quiz`, `/party/[code]`, `/duel`, `/arena`; it appears when the user leaves the live surface. Badge: NEW `clearBadge()` in `lib/push-notifications.ts` + `<BadgeHygiene />` in `app/_layout.tsx` clearing on cold start, every foreground, and when the route hits `notifications` (inbox screen file untouched). In-app unread logic (server read flags) unaffected.

**Web counterpart:** 🚫 none. Web is a server-rendered Next.js app (deploys are live on refresh) and has no app-icon badge; both mechanics are native-platform concerns by definition. No web row needed.

**Sign-offs:** `ios-design-hig` + `ios-design-motion` + `ios-design-accessibility` (44pt targets, fades under reduce-motion, VoiceOver announce - PASS) · `ios-qa-tester` (7-case plan in iOS `docs/CHANGELOG.md`; device pass rides the next TestFlight build + first published update) · `ios-code-reviewer` (PASS) · `ios-docs-writer` (iOS CHANGELOG + vault Daily) · `ios-parity-tracker` (this row).

## 2026-06-11: Push notification tap routing + the push payload contract (iOS, LOCAL, not built; next-build stack)

**Status:** ✅ iOS code ready + verified LOCALLY. `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. eslint 0 errors on touched files (pre-existing `_layout.tsx` `import/first` warnings only). `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 9.46 MB). Pure JS, OTA-eligible, but NOT built / NOT submitted / NO `eas update` (build-on-command). Committed on iOS `main`, not pushed. NO new npm packages. No em-dashes. Owner: `vp-ios`.

**The gap:** the iOS push client registered tokens (`profiles.expo_push_token`) and presented foreground banners but had NO notification-response listener; tapping a push opened the app and went nowhere. Web has no equivalent surface (browser pushes are not wired), so this row is iOS-led.

**📜 PUSH PAYLOAD CONTRACT (binding on FUTURE WEB/SERVER SENDERS — read before building any push dispatcher):** when POSTing to `https://exp.host/--/api/v2/push/send`, set the message `data` field to `{ "action_url": "<web-shaped path>" }` — the EXACT string the server writes to `notifications.action_url` for the in-app inbox (e.g. `/dashboard`, `/games/party/{code}`, `/social`). `url` is accepted as a fallback key; `action_url` is canonical. Senders NEVER pre-translate paths for iOS: the client owns the web→native mapping (shared `lib/notification-routing.ts` `mapActionUrl`: `/dashboard`→`/`, `/games/party/{code}`→`/party/{code}`, passthrough set, web-only paths dropped), so inbox taps and push taps can never drift. Missing/garbage `data` is safe (tap opens the app, no crash, no navigation). Contract is documented in-code in `~/Desktop/lionade-ios/lib/notification-routing.ts`.

**What shipped (iOS):** `lib/notification-routing.ts` (NEW; `mapActionUrl` extracted from `app/notifications.tsx` + defensive `pushTargetFromResponse`) and `<PushTapRouter />` in `app/_layout.tsx`: `addNotificationResponseReceivedListener` (warm + foreground taps) + `getLastNotificationResponseAsync` then `clearLastNotificationResponseAsync` (cold start, replay-proof across JS/OTA reloads) + request-identifier dedupe. Auth-gated queue: target held until auth resolves; signed-out or un-onboarded users get the link DROPPED (RouteGuard owns /login//onboarding; no protected navigation around the auth wall); onboarded users get `router.push` on the next tick after RouteGuard settles. Sign-offs: `ios-qa-tester` (6-case plan in iOS `docs/CHANGELOG.md`; device pass rides the next APNs-signed build), `ios-code-reviewer` (caught + fixed a timer-cleanup race that silently dropped the navigation), `ios-docs-writer`, `ios-parity-tracker` (this row).

**Web counterpart:** 🚫 none needed today (web has no push). WHEN web/server gains a push dispatcher (streak warnings, friend nudges, daily reminders per the `lib/push-notifications.ts` lifecycle note), it MUST follow the contract above — flag `admin`/`dev-backend` to read this row first.

## 2026-06-11: Post-build-21 improvement batch — 4 tails (iOS, LOCAL, not built; next-build stack)

**Status:** ✅ All 4 items code-ready + verified LOCALLY. iOS `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors** per item. `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 9.46 MB). NOT built, NOT submitted (build-on-command standing order; these stack on `main` for the NEXT build after 21). 4 separate commits on iOS `main` (`fd4d689` chat, `6e035de` note detail, `db9987a` paths anti-cheat, `4236628` mono weights), not pushed. NO new npm packages. No em-dashes. No-flash-of-zero. Reduced-motion-safe. Owner: `vp-ios`.

**1. Party lobby chat hardening (closes the §10 V2 flag).** iOS `components/party/RoomLobby.tsx` LobbyChat was always-expanded and trusted every broadcast on the public room topic; web's 2026-06-10 security pass + unread counter never reached it. Ported web's exact model: collapsed-with-unread-badge (broadcast-while-collapsed only, 9+ cap, cleared on open, hydration exempt), optimistic broadcast-first send (pending local echo + client broadcast + parallel REST; rollback + draft restore on REST failure), and the pending/authoritative reconcile — broadcasts without the server backstop's `authoritative: true` render dimmed and expire in 10s unless the same-message_id authoritative copy replaces them, so forged/contradicting broadcasts can't stick. Sender username now rides the fast-path payload (peers saw "Player" before). ✅ full chat parity.

**2. Note detail screen (closes the photo-notes flag "notes render only as rows").** New pushed `app/note/[id].tsx`: large-photo NoteBody (new `photoHeight` prop, 260 vs 180), title/class/source/date metadata, **pin + archive verified REAL on web before building** — `PATCH /api/classes/notes/[noteId] { pinned }` and `DELETE` (soft archive) both exist (`app/api/classes/notes/[noteId]/route.ts`), so iOS ships them (writes via the API for server ownership checks; reads via RLS like use-class-detail), plus native Share of text segments. Note rows in class detail now navigate (haptic + a11y); BackButton + Stack registered. NOTE: web has no single-note GET — iOS reads the note directly under RLS (parity-equivalent). iOS now arguably EXCEEDS web's note view (pin/archive are inline buttons on web's class page, not a dedicated note screen) — 🚫 no web work needed.

**3. Learning Paths anti-cheat parity (closes pre-build-audit divergence FLAG: correct_index fetched upfront).** **Verdict: web is the per-pick model, NOT fetch-then-hide and NOT a server check route.** Web fetches stage questions without answers and calls `checkAnswer(questionId)` (`lib/db.ts:306`) — a deferred per-question client-side select at answer time. iOS `app/learn/paths/[subject].tsx` now matches: answer fields dropped from the question fetch + interface, per-pick `quiz_questions` lookup after the answer locks, `revealedIndex` drives the green highlight, feedback gated on the resolved verdict (no wrong-state flash mid-lookup), failed reveal = incorrect + no explanation (web's catch). **Shared-limitation flag for the web team:** on BOTH platforms the reveal is an RLS table select a motivated client can query early; a true server check route would harden both. Not invented here per scope.

**4. JetBrainsMono 600/700 faces (deferred polish, isolated commit).** 85 mono sites set fontWeight 600/700 with only 400/500 registered — bold mono rendered as Medium. Loaded the SemiBold/Bold faces from the installed `@expo-google-fonts/jetbrains-mono`; no call-site changes. Overflow spot-check: TTF metrics read directly — identical advances across all four weights (1200/602/1000), so fixed-width mono containers (wallet, stat pills, timers, rank columns) keep exact layout. Revert `4236628` alone if it reads wrong on device. 🚫 web N/A (web loads variable/weighted mono via next/font already).

**Quality gates (chain via `vp-ios`):** `ios-dev-realtime` (chat reconcile on the shared topic, no removeChannel — PASS) · `ios-dev-screens`/`ios-dev-components` (note screen + chat pill + quiz states — PASS) · `ios-dev-data` (route reality checks read from web source: note PATCH/DELETE exist, no note GET, no paths check route — PASS) · `ios-design-hig` (collapsed-chat pill pattern, destructive archive confirm via Alert, action chips — PASS) · `ios-design-accessibility` (unread count in the pill's label, labeled note actions, imagebutton roles inherited from NoteBody — PASS) · `ios-qa-tester` (chat send-fail rollback / dupe echo / unread math; note pin revert + archive + unfiled quick-note; paths timer-expiry + slow-lookup; font metric verification — PASS) · `ios-code-reviewer` (PASS) · `ios-docs-writer` (iOS `docs/CHANGELOG.md` + vault Daily) · `ios-parity-tracker` (this row; §10-chat, photo-notes-detail, and pre-build-audit-anticheat flags closed).

Reduced-motion-safe. Owner: `vp-ios`.

**What shipped (iOS):** Quick Note composer (`components/QuickNoteFab.tsx`) gets a "Snap photo" camera row (44pt targets; library as secondary). Optimistic local thumbnail on capture (haptic, background upload, typing never blocked), tap-to-retry on failure, text never lost. Photos embed as standard markdown tokens `![photo](note-images/<userId>/<uuid>.jpg)` appended to `class_notes.body` (plain TEXT per migration 033 — ZERO schema change; `/api/classes/quick-note` stores body verbatim, AI fills metadata only). New `lib/note-images.ts` (token parse/strip, 1h signed-URL cache, syllabus-pattern byte upload) + `components/NoteBody.tsx` (inline rounded photos, fixed-height frame while resolving, full-screen viewer). `NoteRow` in `app/classes/[id].tsx` renders inline; `RecentNoteRow` strips tokens from teasers. app.json purpose strings broadened (were syllabus-only).

**Storage (NEW infra, NEEDS SAM VERIFY — flagged):** live DB has exactly ONE bucket (`class-syllabi`, private, 5 MB, `application/pdf` ONLY — verified via storage admin API 2026-06-11), so images CANNOT reuse it without loosening the PDF-only guarantee. Plan: sibling private bucket `note-images` (10 MB, image/jpeg|png|webp|heic) + owner-folder RLS mirroring migration 044, written as `supabase/migrations/20260611_note_images_storage.sql` (committed, NOT applied — bucket creation was classifier-blocked as autonomous infra). Until Sam creates the bucket + pushes the migration, iOS uploads fail honestly (retry affordance; text still saves). Photos are served ONLY via short-lived signed URLs under owner-folder SELECT; no public bucket, no public-write.

Web fix = parse the same `note-images/` token (strip in teasers/previews, render signed-URL image in the note view; same RLS, no schema work). Owner when picked up: `admin` → `dev-frontend`.

## 2026-06-11: §5 consume pass — live /api/arena/matches strip + server-authoritative Learning Paths reward (iOS consumes 2 new web routes, LOCAL, not built)

**Status:** ✅ CLOSES §5 schema-safety FLAG 1 (`/api/arena/matches` phantom) AND the pre-build-audit divergence FLAG 1 (Learning Paths pays no Fangs) — both web routes now EXIST on web `main` (deploying with the batch push) and iOS consumes them. Code ready + verified LOCALLY. iOS `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 9.41 MB). NOT built, NOT submitted. Committed on `main` in `~/Desktop/lionade-ios`, not pushed. NO new npm packages. No user-facing em-dashes. No-flash-of-zero on both surfaces. `components/party/*` + `RoomLobby` untouched (parallel agent lane). Owner: `vp-ios`.

**What shipped (iOS):**
1. **Arena recent-matches strip is LIVE.** `lib/hooks/use-arena-matches.ts` rewired from the honest-`[]` stub to `GET /api/arena/matches` (auth-scoped bearer, no query params) → `{ matches: [{ id, opponentId, opponentUsername, opponentAvatarUrl, myScore, oppScore, myEloChange, status, createdAt }] }`, newest first, max 10, completed-only. Contract deltas handled: the live shape has NO `winnerId`/`completedAt`, so the lobby tally + `MatchRow` in `app/arena.tsx` now derive WIN/LOSS/DRAW from `myScore` vs `oppScore`, timestamps use `createdAt`, and `myEloChange` renders only when non-zero (0 = legacy row predating ELO snapshots). New `isLoading` from the hook gates the strip behind a 3-row skeleton (and blanks the header count) so "NO MATCHES YET" can never flash pre-resolve; fetch errors still resolve to an honest empty list.
2. **Learning Paths now PAY (server-side).** `app/learn/paths/[subject].tsx` `finishQuiz()` no longer upserts `user_stage_progress` client-side; it POSTs `/api/paths/complete-stage { stageId, correct, total }`. The server owns the progress write AND the reward (first completion pays `min(50, correct*5 + stars*10)` × plan multiplier through the atomic `update_user_coins` RPC + a `coin_transactions` ledger row; replays/races pay 0 via the UNIQUE(user_id, stage_id) claim). Stage progress has exactly ONE writer now; the map's `loadData` select stays read-only. Stars/isNewBest display the server response (optimistic local stars animate first, server overwrites). Balance reconciles via the existing `useUserStats` mutate with the server's `newCoins` (no refetch lag); the wallet screen self-updates via its `coin_transactions` Realtime INSERT subscription. `quiz_sessions` log now records `coins_earned = fangsAwarded` (the old row logged Fangs nobody received) and is non-fatal so a failed log can't flip the UI to error after the reward settled.

**UI honesty rules on the paths results screen:** Fangs slot spins until the server settles (never a fabricated number); replay shows `+0` + "Stage reward already earned"; sub-50% shows "Score 50% or higher to earn the stage reward"; a failed POST swaps the row for "Couldn't save your result. Check your connection and retry the stage." (true — with the client write gone, a failed call records nothing).

**Contract verification (read from web source 2026-06-11):** `app/api/arena/matches/route.ts` (flat shape above; `myEloChange = elo_after - elo_before`, 0 on legacy rows; one batched profile read for opponents) · `app/api/paths/complete-stage/route.ts` (200 `{ success, stars, isNewBest, completed, firstCompletion, fangsAwarded, newCoins }`; star thresholds >=90% 3 / >=70% 2 / >=50% 1 — same as the old client; reward reverts the completion claim if the coin credit fails so a retry can pay).

**Quality gates:** `ios-dev-data` (hook rewrite + completion rewire) + `ios-dev-screens` (lobby strip + results row) + `ios-qa-tester` (live rows render; empty state only post-resolve; replay pays 0 and the UI says so; activity-log failure can't lie; offline POST = honest error card) + `ios-code-reviewer` (single writer for `user_stage_progress`; the remaining `winnerId` read at `arena.tsx:1397` is the `/complete` contract where the field really exists; new copy dash-free) + `ios-docs-writer` (iOS CHANGELOG + vault Daily) + `ios-parity-tracker` (this row; both flags struck through above).

**What shipped (iOS):**
1. **Request-to-join (both sides).** Requester: new `RequestToJoinGate.tsx` rendered by the ROOM SHELL when `usePartyRoom` detects the privacy gate (`POST /join` → `200 { ok:false, requires_request:true }`). Optional 50-char note → `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/request-join` → 3s poll of the GET for `approved|declined` (mirrors the web hub modal's poll); approval calls `retryJoin()` → idempotent re-join → lobby. Placement divergence from web (deliberate): web hosts the requester flow in a `/games/party` HUB modal because web joins from the hub; iOS joins inside the room shell, so the gate there covers hub joins + Past Lobbies + deep links with one surface. Host: `RoomLobby.tsx` banner stack (max 3, like web) — hydrates `GET /join-requests` `{ pending: [{request_id, requester_user_id, requester_name, requester_avatar, note, requested_at}] }` on becoming host, listens for `JOIN_REQUEST`/`JOIN_DECISION` broadcasts on the shared room topic (isHost rides a ref so mid-lobby host promotion works without re-binding), Let in / Pass → `POST /join-requests/[id]/decide { decision: "approve"|"decline" }`. `JOIN_DECISION` clears the banner on every co-client; approve also fires `PLAYER_JOINED` server-side → roster refresh.
2. **Mid-round queue.** New `JoiningNextRoundBanner.tsx` (trivia/bluff/sketch variants, web's exact copy + accents) rendered at the top of TriviaView/BluffView/SketchView while the caller's `is_pending_round` is true. Server behavior (verified): join/approve sets the flag when `status='playing' && current_game`; round-creation paths clear it, the next snapshot refresh unmounts the banner, and the queued player pops into rosters via the players prop. Web's `pokerface` variant lands with the Poker Face port.
3. **Spectator toggle.** `POST /spectate { on }` → `{ ok, is_spectator }`. Non-host dashed secondary button under Ready with web's exact copy ("Watching only · tap to play" / "Watch only (spectator)"); roster rows show an eye + "watching" state for spectators (iOS-additive clarity — web's roster shows no marker; flagged below, not a contract change).
4. **Public-room discovery: 🚫 N/A — web has NO such surface.** Verified `app/games/party/page.tsx`: create + join-by-code + the request modal only; `privacy_mode` gates by code, nothing lists open rooms. The §10a flag assumed web had one; it does not. No iOS list built — parity, not an omission.

**Contract verification (real route filenames + response keys, read from the web source 2026-06-11):** `POST|GET /api/party/rooms/[code]/request-join` (POST body `{note?}` → `{ok, request_id, status:"pending"}` | `{ok, already_pending}` | `{ok, already_member}` | 429 `{error}` on the 5-min/3-pending caps; GET → `{status:"none"}` | `{request_id, status, requested_at, decided_at, note}`) · `GET /api/party/rooms/[code]/join-requests` (host-gated via `isEffectiveHost`; non-hosts get `{pending: []}`) · `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/join-requests/[id]/decide` (→ `{ok, decision, is_pending_round?}`; capacity 409 "Room is full") · `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/spectate` · broadcasts on `party-room-{code}`: `join_request` `{request_id, requester_user_id, requester_name, requester_avatar, note}` + `join_decision` `{request_id, requester_user_id, decision, is_pending_round?}` (event strings already in the iOS `PARTY_EVENTS` mirror since §10a).

**Realtime discipline:** the new lobby listeners attach to the topic-deduped shared room channel that `use-party-room` owns and NEVER removeChannel it (same pattern as LobbyChat; supabase-js `subscribe()` no-ops on a non-closed channel — verified in `RealtimeChannel.js`). Requester-side decision detection is REST-polled like web's hub modal (no extra channel).

**Divergences/flags:** (1) Requester-flow placement: room shell (iOS) vs hub modal (web) — same contract, better deep-link coverage; (2) iOS shows requester name + note but no avatar in the host banner (the iOS lobby roster has no avatars yet — consistent); (3) iOS roster marks spectators "watching"; web's roster doesn't mark them at all — consider porting the marker BACK to web; (4) shared-platform quirk for the web team: the `POST /start` ready gate counts spectators, so an un-readied spectator blocks start on BOTH platforms (server-side; iOS needs no change if web relaxes it).

**Quality gates (chain via `vp-ios`):** `ios-dev-realtime` (shared-topic attach without removeChannel, isHostRef promotion path, AppState interplay — PASS) · `ios-dev-data` (route filenames + response keys read from web source, not assumed — PASS) · `ios-dev-screens` + `ios-dev-components` (gate + banner + lobby surfaces — PASS) · `ios-design-hig` (gold private-room accent matching web's request modal, 44pt+ targets, secondary dashed spectator CTA — PASS) · `ios-design-accessibility` (accessibilityLiveRegion on banner/gate states, labeled Let in/Pass per requester, reduce-motion gating incl. switching the host-banner entrance to an opacity-only fade — PASS) · `ios-qa-tester` (request→approve/decline both sides incl. already_pending resume + already_member shortcut + 429 cooldown copy; mid-round queue promote on next round; spectator watching state + server-side count exclusion; discovery skip verified against web — PASS) · `ios-code-reviewer` (eslint clean after fixing 4 unescaped-entity errors + 1 unused const — PASS) · `ios-docs-writer` (iOS CHANGELOG + vault Daily + this row) · `ios-parity-tracker` (this row; §10a FLAGS 1–2 closed).

## 2026-06-11: Web-replication Section 10c — PARTY third game: SKETCHY SUBJECTS (Subject Pictionary, live drawing) (iOS-only port, LOCAL, not built)

**Status:** 🟡 PARTIAL (by design — extends the §10a foundation + §10b with the third game; only Poker Face remains, compliance-gated). ✅ Code ready + verified LOCALLY. iOS `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. `expo export --platform ios` clean (single Hermes bundle, 9.42 MB). NOT built, NOT submitted. NO new npm packages — `@shopify/react-native-skia` (2.2.12) + `react-native-gesture-handler` (~2.28.0) were already installed; the canvas uses them. No user-facing em-dashes. No-flash-of-zero preserved. Committed on `main` in `~/Desktop/lionade-ios`, not pushed. Owner: `vp-ios`.

**What shipped (iOS):** **Sketchy Subjects**, the third Party game, fully playable: lobby 3-game picker now has a SKETCHY tile → host start (`POST /start` `game:"sketch"`) → 5s round intro countdown ("you draw / X draws this round") → drawer's `select-word` screen (3 candidate cards easy/medium/hard OR a grey BANK pill with the definition, sorted easiest-first, 10s auto-pick) → `drawing` (drawer: Skia canvas + 16-color palette toolbar + 3 sizes + eraser + undo + tap-to-confirm clear; guessers: live canvas + Wordle blanks row + guess input + live guess feed + compact scoreboard) → first correct guess (or 90s timeout) → 2.5s celebrating stamp ("GUESSED!"/"TIME'S UP") → `reveal` (word + factoid/definition + scoreboard) → PLAY ANOTHER ROUND / END GAME → game-over podium + rematch.

**The hard part — stroke sync (mirrors web 1:1):** strokes ride a SEPARATE high-frequency topic `party-room-{code}-sketch-strokes` (decoupled from the slower `party-room-{code}-sketch` game-state channel, same split as web). Drawer captures touch via a gesture-handler `Pan` (worklet → `runOnJS`), renders locally with Skia `<Path>`, broadcasts the in-progress stroke at ~30Hz (33ms) while the pen is down + an authoritative final broadcast on release, and POSTs persisted batches every 500ms. Guessers subscribe, replace-or-append incoming strokes by `stroke_num`, and render. Wire format is IDENTICAL to web: logical 1000×600 coord space, paper `#EEF4FF`, eraser serialized as `"__erase__"`, 16-color palette + sizes `[3,8,16]` all byte-for-byte matching `SKETCH_COLORS`/`SKETCH_SIZES` — so a native drawer and a web guesser (or vice versa) interoperate. **Late-joiner + AppState resync:** `SketchCanvas` owns its strokes channel's lifecycle, fetches `GET /strokes` on mount (replay), tears the channel down on background, and on foreground re-subscribes AND re-fetches the full canvas (merging persisted history with any newer live strokes) so a reconnecting guesser catches up — web has the same persisted-replay GET but no explicit foreground resync (RN-specific, since a backgrounded WS is dead on iOS).

**Reused from §10a/§10b (no new infra):** `use-party-room.ts` realtime hook unchanged; `[code].tsx` game-container gained a `sketch` case; `RoomLobby.tsx` picker went from 2 → 3 tiles + a `startSketch` handler + a Sketchy start card; the resilient-channel + AppState-foreground-resubscribe / background-teardown discipline, `adoptRound` seen-set, effective-host derivation, deadline-driven completion + game-over podium + rematch are the same patterns as Trivia/Bluff.

**Schema verification — every DB table / column / API route / realtime channel+event this surface touches (verified against the web routes' actual queries + response keys + broadcast shapes):**

- **Tables (read/written ONLY server-side via routes — iOS never selects them):** `sketch_rounds` (id, room_id, round_num, drawer_user_id, word [SECRET, drawer-only], factoid, subject, duration_sec, started_at, ended_at, phase ['celebrating'|'reveal'], winner_user_id, celebrating_started_at, candidate_words [JSONB], source_kind ['curated'|'bank'], source_bank_id, rerolled), `sketch_strokes` (round_id, stroke_num, color, size, points [number[][]]), `sketch_guesses` (round_id, user_id, guess [redacted to "[correct]" when correct], was_correct, was_close, points_earned, guessed_at), `sketch_revealed_positions` (round_id, position, letter, revealed_by — UNIQUE(round_id,position)), `sketch_fang_awards` (round_id, user_id, reason ['drawing'|'guess'|'letters'], fangs — UNIQUE for idempotency), `party_room_players` (score bumped server-side), `vocab_banks` (bank-word source), `profiles` (coins for the letter-Fang trickle). Migration `051` + the `sketch_bank_source` migration (source_kind/source_bank_id/rerolled) + the word-difficulty CHECK are applied.
- **API routes (iOS consumes; server owns all scoring + the Fang faucet):** `POST /api/party/sketch/rounds` (create round; returns `{round:{id,room_id,round_num,drawer_user_id,subject,duration_sec,started_at}, drawer_should_pick, candidate_words?}` — `candidate_words` ONLY when caller is the drawer; **no word leaked**), `GET /rounds/[id]/words` (drawer-only 403-gated; `{candidates:[{word,difficulty,factoid,source?}]}` or `{locked,word}`), `POST /rounds/[id]/select-word` (`{word}` → locks), `POST /rounds/[id]/strokes` (drawer-only persist batch) + `GET /strokes` (`{strokes:[{stroke_num,color,size,points}]}` replay), `POST /rounds/[id]/guess` (`{guess}` → `{verdict,was_correct,was_close,points_earned,fangs_earned,mask,matched_positions,newly_revealed}` — **never the word**; clamps reveal to a hidden floor of ⌈letters/3⌉, min 1, that guesses can never uncover), `GET /rounds/[id]/reveal` (guesser catch-up: `{mask,revealed:[{position,letter}]}` — structural mask + already-green positions, **never the word**), `POST /rounds/[id]/complete` (drawer/host) + `GET /complete` (member lazy-complete backstop) → `{word,factoid,drawer_user_id,source_kind,scoreboard:[{user_id,username,score}]}` — the FIRST time guessers get the word, `POST /rounds/[id]/advance-phase` (celebrating→reveal), `POST /rounds/[id]/reroll` (drawer-only, once/round — NOT wired into the iOS V1 picker, see scope-out), `POST /rooms/[code]/start` `{game:"sketch"}`, `POST /rooms/[code]/rematch`, `GET /rooms/[code]` snapshot (carries the sketch `activeRound` with drawer_user_id/round_num/subject/duration_sec + the `word_picked` BOOLEAN, **never the word**).
- **Realtime channels + events:** game-state `party-room-{code}-sketch` carries `round_started` (round_id, drawer_user_id, round_num, subject, duration_sec, started_at), `word_selected` (round_id), `guess` (user_id, username, body, variant ['guess'|'close'|'correct'], matched[]), `letter_reveal` (mask, revealed[{position,letter}] — **never the word**), `round_ended` (reveal payload + celebrating{winnerName,word,started_at}), `game_over`. Strokes topic `party-room-{code}-sketch-strokes` carries `stroke` ({stroke:{stroke_num,color,size,points,is_eraser}}) + `clear_canvas`. Room channel `party-room-{code}` reused for `game_ended` (rematch). `paused`/`resumed` exist in the event map for cross-client parity but the iOS V1 has no host pause button (scope-out).

**Word-never-leaked + no-client-scoring confirmation:** the SECRET word never reaches a guesser before reveal. The drawer reads it via the drawer-only `GET /words` (403 for everyone else) and holds it as local `lockedWord`; guessers only ever receive the structural `mask` + the Wordle green positions THEY matched (server-clamped to the hidden floor). The full word first lands for everyone in the `/complete` reveal payload. iOS computes NO scores and mints NO Fangs — the guess/complete routes own the scoreboard bump + the server-side, idempotent `sketch_fang_awards` faucet (drawing reward + per-correct-guess + per-letter trickle). Verified by grep: no direct `sketch_rounds`/`sketch_guesses` selects in any iOS file, no `coins`/`score` writes.

**Stroke-perf approach:** in-progress stroke lives in a ref (mutated in place); a cheap render counter bumps so Skia diffs the `<Path>` children. Completed strokes compile their `SkPath` once (memoized by point-count) so only the active stroke re-tessellates per frame; points are decimated (sub-1.5px moves dropped) and mid-stroke broadcast is throttled to 30Hz — the same cadence + decimation web uses, so the channel never floods.

**Verification:** `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. `expo export --platform ios` clean (single Hermes bundle 9.42 MB, all Skia/gesture-handler/reanimated imports resolve). `GestureHandlerRootView` already wraps the app root in `app/_layout.tsx`.

**Scoped out of iOS V1 (deliberate, all web-only extras — none affect correctness or the wire contract):** word reroll button (route exists; not surfaced — drawer just picks from the 3 cards or auto-picks), the candidate-card dictionary "i" popover (web fetches dictionaryapi.dev client-side), host pause/resume button, mid-game friend invite modal, the color-roulette custom-color picker + recents row, and the post-round vote card (the auto-advance + host CTAs cover round flow). Confetti/Fang-burst juice is replaced by native haptics + the SR announce.

**Still web-only after 10c:** Poker Face (per-presenter rotation + casino mechanics behind a legal/compliance gate) is the LAST of the 4 games unported. The lobby teaser now reads "Poker Face is coming to iOS soon."

## 2026-06-11: Web-replication Section 10b — PARTY second game: BLUFF TRIVIA (Fibbage-style) (iOS-only port, LOCAL, not built)

**Status:** 🟡 PARTIAL (by design — extends the §10a slice with the second game). ✅ Code ready + verified LOCALLY. iOS `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. `expo export --platform ios` clean (single Hermes bundle, 9.35 MB). `eslint` clean on all touched files. NOT built, NOT submitted. Committed on `main` in `~/Desktop/lionade-ios` (`dc2f026`), not pushed. Owner: `vp-ios`. Builds directly on the §10a foundation (`2e39478`).

**What shipped (iOS):** **Bluff Trivia**, the second Party game, fully playable: lobby game-picker (Lightning / Bluff toggle) → host start → `write` phase (type a fake answer that sounds real; live "N of M submitted" progress; surfaces the server's SPECIFIC rejection like "That answer matches the real answer. Try a different bluff."; forfeit/"skip me this round" via the sentinel) → `vote` phase (server-shuffled real+fakes, you CAN'T pick your own fake — grayed + disabled + server backstop, re-vote until the timer, "N of M voted" ticker) → `reveal` (fakes ascending by fool-count then the gold TRUTH card last, "X fooled N players" per fake, "YOU FOOLED N PLAYERS" banner, display-only points-this-round breakdown mirroring +1000 found-the-truth / +500-per-fooled, leaderboard re-sort) → NEXT ROUND / Game Over podium + rematch.

**Reused from §10a (no new infra):** `use-party-room.ts` realtime hook unchanged; the `[code].tsx` game-container just gained a `bluff` case; the lobby `RoomLobby.tsx` gained a 2-game picker (Lightning / Bluff) + a `startBluff` handler; the resilient-channel + AppState-foreground-resubscribe/background-teardown discipline is copied from TriviaView onto a self-owned `party-room-{code}-bluff` topic; the GameOver podium + leaderboard + effective-host derivation + deadline-driven auto-advance are the same patterns as Trivia.

**Server contract (consumed, NOT reimplemented):** all rounds read ONLY via `GET /api/party/bluff/rounds/[id]` (the truth/`correct_answer` is stripped during write/vote and present only at reveal — the client NEVER selects `bluff_rounds`/`bluff_answers`/`bluff_votes`). POSTs: `/api/party/bluff/rounds` (create, idempotent), `/[id]/answer` (submit fake / forfeit sentinel), `/[id]/vote`, `/[id]/complete` (CAS advance w/ `from_phase` stale-intent guard). The relaxed answer-dedup, server lazy-advance, host-election tiebreak, and CAS-once scoring all live in `lib/party/bluff-advance.ts` + the routes (web-owned); iOS just calls them. The `FORFEIT_SENTINEL` contract (`"__forfeit__"` + normalizer) is mirrored client-side per the web note. Timers derive purely from `write_ends_at`/`vote_ends_at` (which already include the 5s countdown pad), never back-computed.

**DB columns / tables touched (read via the GET route only):** `bluff_rounds` (`id, room_id, round_num, question, category, phase, write_ends_at, vote_ends_at, started_at, ended_at, correct_answer` — last one reveal-only) · `bluff_answers` (`id, round_id, user_id, text, is_truth` — author/truth flag hidden pre-reveal) · `bluff_votes` (`round_id, voter_user_id, answer_id`) · `party_room_players` (`score` read for leaderboard; NEVER written client-side) · `party_rooms` (`current_game`, `settings.bluff_round_count` default 5). Migration `051` + the `truth_fake_coexist` unique `(round_id,user_id,is_truth)` are server-side; no iOS schema work.

**Realtime events (mirror web 1:1, case-sensitive):** topic `party-room-{code}-bluff`; `BLUFF_EVENTS` = `round_started` / `phase_changed` / `answer_submitted` / `vote_submitted` / `round_ended`. Plus `game_ended` on the room topic for rematch.

**Security (ios-security-auditor PASS):** no direct round-table selects (verified by grep); `correct_answer` consumed only inside the reveal-gated announce + the reveal truth card; no client scoring or `party_room_players` writes; own-fake vote blocked client-side AND server-side; forfeit sentinel filtered server-side so it never becomes a votable card.

**Quality gates (chain via `vp-ios`):** `ios-dev-realtime` (bluff channel reuse + AppState lifecycle + dedupe-trap avoidance via the self-owned topic — PASS) · `ios-dev-screens` + `ios-dev-components` (BluffView write/vote/reveal + lobby picker — PASS) · `ios-dev-data` (round/answer/vote/complete wiring to real routes + verified response shapes — PASS) · `ios-design-hig` + `ios-design-motion` (Bluff gold accent, Bebas/Inter, reduced-motion via live `AccessibilityInfo`, FadeIn/FadeInDown entrances — PASS) · `ios-design-accessibility` (per-answer VoiceOver labels incl. own-fake/your-vote, once-per-round reveal announce via `announceForAccessibility` mirroring web's live region, 44pt targets, danger-timer label — PASS) · `ios-qa-tester` (full write→vote→reveal, can't-vote-own, truth-collision error surfaced, forfeit, host-leaves-mid-round effective-host fallback, AppState background/foreground mid-round, no-flash-of-zero loader — PASS) · `ios-code-reviewer` (removed unused const + escaped JSX apostrophe; eslint clean — PASS) · `ios-security-auditor` (no secret exposure, no client scoring — PASS) · `ios-docs-writer` (this row + CHANGELOG note + vault Daily) · `ios-parity-tracker` (this row).

**Still web-only after 10b (next sub-plan):** Sketchy Subjects (needs Skia canvas + stroke channel) and Poker Face (per-presenter rotation + casino gate) remain unported; the lobby teaser now reads "Sketchy Subjects and Poker Face are coming to iOS soon."

## 2026-06-11: Web-replication Section 10a — PARTY foundation + Trivia (Lightning Round) VERTICAL SLICE (iOS-only port, LOCAL, not built)

**Status:** 🟡 PARTIAL (by design — vertical slice). ✅ Code ready + verified LOCALLY. iOS `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. `expo export --platform ios` clean (single Hermes bundle, 9.31 MB). NOT built, NOT submitted. Committed on `main` in `~/Desktop/lionade-ios` (`2e39478`), not pushed. Owner: `vp-ios`. Tenth surface in the page-by-page replication. The Party suite is XL (4 games + V2 lobbies + realtime + Skia + a compliance gate), so this pass builds the FOUNDATION + the simplest game (Trivia) end to end to prove the realtime stack; Bluff/Sketchy/Poker Face are sub-planned below.

**What shipped (iOS):** the Party FOUNDATION (hub + room shell + native lobby + the resilient realtime layer + a game-container that mounts the active game by `room.current_game`) and the FIRST game, **Trivia (Lightning Round)**, fully playable: lobby → ready → host start → round countdown → 4-tile answer (one pick, no take-backs, "X of Y locked in") → reveal (correct tile + per-option tallies + base/speed/streak points + leaderboard re-sort) → next round → Game Over podium + rematch.

**Realtime approach (the crux):** `lib/hooks/use-party-room.ts` is the SINGLE OWNER of `party-room-{code}` (broadcasts) + `party-room-{code}-players` (room_id-filtered postgres_changes), each wrapped in a RN port of web's `subscribeResilient` (1s→16s backoff, 5 attempts). **AppState:** a backgrounded WebSocket is dead on iOS, so on `background` it tears the channels down and on `active` it fully re-subscribes AND `refresh()`es to pull anything missed; a 3s poll is the always-on backstop. **Channel-per-topic dedupe trap (the web Party connectivity bug) avoided:** the hook is the sole owner of its topics, and all outgoing broadcasts ride the ALREADY-SUBSCRIBED channel — never a throwaway `supabase.channel()` that would need a `removeChannel` (which detaches by TOPIC and would deafen the live channel). TriviaView owns its own `party-room-{code}-trivia` topic with the same discipline.

**SCHEMA / ROUTES / CHANNELS touched (verified against the LIVE DB via information_schema + the web routes' actual queries — for Sam's verification):**
- **Tables (live columns confirmed present):**
  - `party_rooms` — `id, code, host_user_id, status, current_game, last_game, settings (jsonb), created_at, ended_at, privacy_mode ('open'|'friends'|'closed'), display_name, dismissed_at`.
  - `party_room_players` — composite PK `(room_id, user_id)`; `score, joined_at, left_at, is_ready, selected_subjects (text[]), is_pending_round, is_spectator`.
  - `trivia_rounds` (migration 061, APPLIED) — `id, room_id, round_num, question, category, options (jsonb = ARRAY OF STRINGS), correct_index (int — SECRET), phase ('answer'|'reveal'), started_at, answer_ends_at, reveal_ends_at, ended_at`. **iOS NEVER selects this table directly** — reads go through the GET route which maps `options` → `[{id:String(i), text}]` and strips `correct_index` until reveal. (Note: the correct_index column-REVOKE migration 064 is a NO-OP on prod, so the secret lives only behind the API filter — this is exactly why iOS uses the route, never a direct select.)
  - `trivia_answers` — PK `(round_id, user_id)`; `choice_index, answered_at, is_correct, points_earned`. **iOS NEVER touches this table directly** (the server scores it on the answer→reveal CAS flip).
  - `party_lobby_chat` — `id, room_code, user_id, body, created_at` (read via GET, written via POST; client `client_id` = row id for de-dup).
  - `party_join_requests` — read by the web request-to-join flow (iOS request-to-join host banner is FLAGGED for a later pass, not built here).
  - `party_room_players`-joined `profiles` (username + equipped cosmetics) via the snapshot route.
- **API routes consumed (with real response shapes):**
  - `POST /api/party/rooms` `{ display_name?, privacy_mode? }` → `{ code, room, players }`.
  - `GET /api/party/rooms/[code]` → `{ room, players, meUserId, isHost, activeRound: {id,phase,started_at}|null }`.
  - `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/join` → `{ ok, already_member?|is_pending_round?, room, players }` (idempotent; privacy gate may return `{ ok:false, requires_request:true }`).
  - `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/ready` `{ ready }` → `{ ok, is_ready, all_ready, players_total, players_ready }`.
  - `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/start` `{ game:"trivia", settings:{ trivia_round_count, trivia_answer_seconds } }` → `{ ok, game, room_id }` (server whitelists+clamps the trivia settings; clears prior `trivia_rounds` on a fresh trivia game).
  - `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/end-game` → `{ ok }` · `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/rematch` · `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/leave` · `POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/dismiss` → `{ ok }`.
  - `GET/POST /api/party/rooms/[code]/lobby-chat` → GET `{ messages:[{id,user_id,user_name,body,created_at}] }`; POST `{ body, client_id }` → `{ ok, message }`.
  - `GET /api/party/history` → `{ active:[HistoryRow], recent:[HistoryRow], saved:[] }` (HistoryRow: `room_id, room_code, display_name, game_type, status, members_count, last_activity_at, joined_at, left_at, is_dismissed`).
  - `POST /api/party/trivia/rounds` `{ code }` → `{ round:{ id, room_id, round_num, question, category, phase, started_at, answer_ends_at, options:[{id,text}] } }` (idempotent; NO correct_index).
  - `GET /api/party/trivia/rounds/[id]` → `{ round:{...,reveal_ends_at,ended_at, correct_option_id? (REVEAL ONLY)}, my_answer_option_id, answered_count, answered_user_ids, reveal?:{ correct_option_id, option_tallies, round_points, breakdown:{base,speed,streak,correct,streak_count} } }` (server lazy-advances on read).
  - `POST /api/party/trivia/rounds/[id]/answer` `{ choice_index }` → `{ ok, already, answered_count, total }` (409 once the deadline passes; PK makes it immutable/idempotent).
  - `POST /api/party/trivia/rounds/[id]/complete` `{ action:"advance", from_phase }` → `{ advanced, round }` (CAS-guarded; effective-host anytime, any member after deadline+grace).
- **Realtime channels + events:** `party-room-{code}` (PLAYER_JOINED/LEFT, GAME_STARTED/ENDED, ROOM_UPDATED, ROOM_DISMISSED, READY_CHANGED, LOBBY_CHAT) · `party-room-{code}-players` (postgres_changes on `party_room_players`) · `party-room-{code}-trivia` (ROUND_STARTED, PHASE_CHANGED, ROUND_ENDED, ANSWER_SUBMITTED). Event strings match web verbatim (case-sensitive).

**Security confirmations (grep-verified on iOS source):** (a) `correct_index` appears ONLY in comments — never read; (b) NO direct `trivia_rounds`/`trivia_answers` table selects (all reads via the GET route which strips the secret pre-reveal); (c) NO client-side scoring and NO `coins`/`coin_transactions`/`score` writes anywhere in the party files (scoring is the server's CAS-guarded `scoreRound`); (d) no-flash-of-zero preserved (spinners gate; scores/ready never flash 0 pre-load).

**Sub-plan for the remaining 3 games (assessed, NOT built):**
- **Bluff Trivia (Fibbage)** — MEDIUM, ~1 screen. write→vote→reveal, server-authoritative exactly like Trivia (`bluff_rounds` + `/api/party/bluff/rounds/[id]/{answer,vote,complete}`). Text + tap UI, NO new packages. Closest reuse of this slice's realtime foundation; **recommended next.**
- **Sketchy Subjects (Pictionary)** — LARGE/XL. Live drawing canvas (Skia — ALREADY installed), a separate high-frequency stroke topic (`party-room-{code}-sketch-strokes`, ~30Hz, decoupled from game-state per the web split), gesture-handler for drawing input (ALREADY installed), drawer word-pick + Wordle-style progressive letter reveal. ~2 screens (canvas + guess feed). The realtime/lobby foundation carries over; the canvas + stroke sync is the bulk of the work. **No new packages needed.**
- **Poker Face** — LAST, behind a **compliance gate.** Gambling-adjacent (believe/doubt calling, casino mechanics legally gated to a bounded version per `project_competitive_modes`). Ships only after `business-legal-compliance` review; NOT scheduled in the replication pass.

**FLAGS for Sam:** (1) V2 lobby sub-features deferred (foundation + core V2 are in): the request-to-join host accept/decline banner, the mid-round join-queue surface, and the spectator toggle are FLAGGED for a follow-up lobby pass (the DB/routes exist; it's additive UI). (2) The Party hub's PUBLIC-room discovery list (web shows joinable open rooms on the landing page) is not ported — join is create-or-by-code for now. (3) Trivia answer-speed presets on iOS are Chill/Normal/Fast (18/12/8s) mapping to `trivia_answer_seconds`; web uses a slider — same server field, clamped server-side.

**Quality gates (chain via `vp-ios`):** `ios-dev-realtime` (channel lifecycle + AppState foreground re-sub/background teardown + the dedupe-trap avoidance — the most important review; PASS) · `ios-dev-screens` + `ios-dev-components` (hub + room shell + lobby + TriviaView) · `ios-dev-data` (room/round/chat/history API wiring to real routes + response shapes) · `ios-design-hig` + `ios-design-motion` (Party purple + Trivia orange, Bebas/Inter, reduced-motion via live AccessibilityInfo) · `ios-design-accessibility` (VoiceOver per-tile labels + once-per-round reveal announce mirroring web's live region, 44pt targets, colorblind-safe glyph anchors) · `ios-qa-tester` (create/join, lobby, ready gate, start, full trivia round, answer lock, reveal, next round, game over, AppState background/foreground mid-round reconnect, host-leaves-mid-round effective-host fallback, no-flash-of-zero) · `ios-code-reviewer` (single-owner channel refactor — eliminated a dual-owner players-channel race) · `ios-security-auditor` (no correct_index exposure, no client scoring/coin writes — confirmed) · `ios-docs-writer` (CHANGELOG + this row + vault Daily) · `ios-parity-tracker` (this row).

## 2026-06-11: Web-replication Section 8 — SHOP (real Fang store + cosmetics + Locker + cross-surface cosmetic RENDERER) (iOS-only port, LOCAL, not built)

**Status:** ✅ Code ready + verified LOCALLY. iOS `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 9.12 MB, single bundle). NOT built, NOT submitted. **Web shop inventory (analyzed):** `/shop` (`app/shop/page.tsx`, ~2186 lines) "The Lion's Den". Coin store reads id/price/type from the canonical `@lionade/core` catalog (`toShopItem` merges catalog + local icon chrome). Tabs Featured / Cosmetics / Boosters / Inventory; sections Today's Drops, Trending, Limited-Time founder badges, Username Effects (live preview), Premium Fang banners, frames/name-colors/banners sub-tabs. `CosmeticCard` renders a LIVE `<CosmeticPreview>` (real frame/aura on a sample Avatar, name color/effect via AnimatedUsername, banner swatch) via `lib/cosmetics/cosmetic-styles.ts` id→visual maps. Buy → `POST /api/shop/purchase` (server reads price from catalog, debits Fangs via `update_user_coins`, refund-on-failure, blocks already-owned + coming-soon `voice_skin`/`boost_mastery_hint_pack`). Equip → `POST /api/shop/equip` (generic cosmetics, writes `profiles.equipped_*`) + `POST /api/me/equip {slot:"username_effect"}`. `GET /api/cosmetics/owned` → `{ items:[{itemId,itemType,equipped}], equipped:{effect,frame,name_color,banner,avatar_aura} }`. Real-money: Stripe Fang IAP packs + cash `*_premium` SKUs + Premium-store subscriptions (web-only; these are §8b on iOS).

**iOS gap found:** `app/shop.tsx` was a 101-line stub ("MORE SHOP COMING SOON" + Daily Spin). NO cosmetic renderer existed on iOS at all — `components/Avatar.tsx` had no frame/aura support; no AnimatedUsername; no banner renderer; no `useEquippedCosmetics`; no Locker. The §6 social rows + leaderboard rows rendered PLAIN avatars/names even though the equipped_* data was passed through.

**Exactly what changed (iOS, all NEW unless noted):**
- `lib/cosmetics/cosmetic-styles.ts` — NEW. iOS-native id→visual maps (RN-specific encoding: frames = border+shadow ring, auras = soft glow, name colors = solid/gradient stops, banners = LinearGradient color stops + `anim` token), mirroring the web file ID-for-ID. Lives as a native lib (NOT in `@lionade/core`) because the styling is RN-primitive-specific; the catalog stays the only shared dependency.
- `lib/cosmetics/username-effects.ts` — NEW. `UsernameEffect` type + `effectForId` / `resolveUsernameEffect` / `resolveNameColor` (mirrors web AnimatedUsername resolvers; tolerates bare token + full `name_fx_*` SKU id).
- `lib/hooks/use-equipped-cosmetics.ts` — NEW. SELF SWR hook over `GET /api/cosmetics/owned` (key `cosmetics-owned/{userId}`, shared/deduped across all call sites). Preferred `equipped` object path + per-item fallback. Plus `resolveRowUsernameEffect` / `resolveRowNameColor` for OTHER-user list rows (no per-row SWR fan-out — same contract as web).
- `components/CosmeticAvatar.tsx` — NEW. Wraps the existing `<Avatar>` with frame ring (border + glow overlay) + aura (Reanimated pulse, GPU-only, `useReducedMotion`-safe, STATIC below 44px for list rows). Zero layout shift; avatar url passed verbatim (avatar-stability). DiceBear PNG endpoint used for the shop-preview fallback.
- `components/AnimatedUsername.tsx` — NEW. Effect-wins-then-name-color precedence (matches web). No MaskedView dep on iOS, so gradients/effects degrade to a representative dominant color + a subtle reduced-motion-safe shimmer (paid users still see something distinct).
- `components/CosmeticBanner.tsx` — NEW. `expo-linear-gradient` banner strip/swatch; default ambient gradient for empty/unknown id (never a blank box).
- `app/shop.tsx` — REWRITTEN. Real store: Fangs balance pill (no-flash-of-zero skeleton), Daily Spin hero kept, tabs Featured/Cosmetics/Boosters/Locker, live previews per card, BUY WITH FANGS via `/api/shop/purchase` (confirm Alert + insufficient-funds + already-owned handling), boosters auto-activate via `/api/shop/activate-booster` on buy. `voice_skin` + `boost_mastery_hint_pack` rendered coming-soon (server also blocks). §8b real-money card is informational only — no web links.
- `components/Shop/ShopCard.tsx`, `components/Shop/CosmeticLocker.tsx`, `components/Shop/cosmetic-icon.ts` — NEW. Card with live preview + buy/equip/owned/coming-soon states; Locker groups owned cosmetics by slot, equips via the service-role routes with optimistic `mutate()` of the owned cache + a live equipped preview header.
- **Cosmetics now RENDER across:** nav/top-bar avatar (`components/TopBar.tsx` → CosmeticAvatar), profile hero (`app/(tabs)/profile.tsx` → CosmeticAvatar + AnimatedUsername), social friend rows + weekly circle (`app/(tabs)/social.tsx`, **closes §6 deferral**), leaderboard podium + list rows (`app/leaderboard.tsx`). `lib/hooks/use-leaderboard.ts` now SELECTs the 4 `equipped_*` columns so other users' cosmetics render (matches web `getLadderLeaderboard`).

**Scope line:** everything built here spends EARNED Fangs (server-side debit) — NOT a StoreKit transaction, so no IAP. Equip is server-side only (no client coin/equipped writes — audited clean). No anti-steering risk: the iOS shop NEVER links out to a web purchase; §8b real-money Fang packs + Pro/Platinum subscriptions are rendered "Coming soon", disabled, no navigation.

**§8b — scoped OUT (do NOT build until App Store Connect IAP + compliance):** real-money Fang packs ($→Fangs) and Pro/Platinum subscriptions via StoreKit. Need App Store Connect products + lawyer/compliance work. Flag for `ios-release-appstore` + `business-legal-compliance` + `ios-security-auditor`.

**Migration dependency:** equip/render is silently inert until `lib/migrations/063_equipped_cosmetic_slots.sql` (`profiles.equipped_frame/equipped_name_color/equipped_banner/equipped_avatar_aura` + `equipped_username_effect`) is applied on prod. Shared schema — apply once, both platforms read it. (Per the existing row, 063 is Sam's manual apply.)

**Quality gates:** `ios-dev-components` (CosmeticAvatar / AnimatedUsername / CosmeticBanner / ShopCard) + `ios-dev-screens` (shop + Locker) + `ios-dev-data` (purchase/equip/owned/booster wiring) + `ios-design-hig`/`ios-design-motion`/`ios-design-accessibility` (5-digit price labels fit; reduced-motion-safe GPU animations; 44pt tap targets + a11y labels on CTAs) + `ios-qa-tester` (buy-with-Fangs happy path, insufficient-funds, already-owned, equip reflects on avatar/name, Locker, previews, coming-soon not purchasable, no-flash-of-zero) + `ios-code-reviewer` + `ios-security-auditor` (no client coin/equipped writes; equip via service-role routes; no real-money path; no anti-steering web links — all confirmed). Flags for Sam below.

**Status:** ✅ Code ready + verified LOCALLY. iOS `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. Web `npx tsc --noEmit` unaffected (shared `@lionade/core` gained a NEW additive `api/academia.ts` module + new `academiaAPI`; web does not import it, so no web behavior change). `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 9.05 MB, single bundle). **Web Academia inventory (shipped vs stubbed):** `/academia` (`app/academia/page.tsx`, ~1570 lines) is the school hub. SHIPPED: onboarding gate (`/api/academia/onboarding`) → redirect to setup; classes index (rich cards: next-exam countdown, exam + note counts) via `GET /api/classes`; **cross-class term GPA snapshot** (`GET /api/academia/gpa` — weighted current % per class → US letter + 4.0 points, unweighted term mean; soft empty state when nothing graded); **THIS WEEK agenda + month calendar** (`GET /api/academia/agenda?from&to` — merges `user_exams.target_date` (kind exam) + `class_assignments.due_date` (kind assignment) into one date-sorted feed, class-annotated; default window [today, today+60], clamped ≤120d); **assignment tracker** (add/complete/track — `POST /api/classes/[id]/assignments`, `PATCH/DELETE /api/classes/assignments/[assignmentId]`, status todo→doing→done); **workload heat warning** (pure-client "crunch" detect: densest 3-consecutive-day window in next ~14d, gold caution at 3 items, red heat at 4+); **ICS import** (`POST /api/academia/import-ics` — PREVIEW `{url}`→`{events,count,truncated}` SSRF-guarded server fetch; COMMIT `{classId,events}`→`{created}` bulk-insert as todo assignments). Recent-notes strip (`/api/classes/recent-notes`). Email digest = server-side cron, NO client UI (untouched, not broken). Study-plan blocking is per-class (`/api/classes/[id]/study-plan` + `/plan`) and lives in class detail, not the hub — left to the class-detail port (flagged).

**iOS gap found (vs current web):** the iOS Academia tab (`app/(tabs)/academia.tsx`, 911 lines) was classes-grid-ONLY — notebook cards + a "Reminders" empty placeholder. MISSING ENTIRELY: GPA snapshot, the THIS WEEK agenda, the month calendar, assignment add/complete, the workload-heat banner, and ICS import. No agenda/gpa/assignment code existed anywhere on iOS, and `@lionade/core` had an EMPTY `api/academia.ts` (zero academia methods; `classesAPI` had grades/flashcards/syllabus but no assignment CRUD).

**Exactly what changed:**
- `packages/lionade-core/src/api/academia.ts` (web-repo copy iOS resolves via tsconfig path) — **NEW.** `academiaAPI` with `agenda(range?)`, `gpa()`, `importIcsPreview(url)`, `importIcsCommit(classId, events)`, and assignment CRUD `listAssignments` / `createAssignment` / `updateAssignment` / `deleteAssignment`. New shared types: `AgendaItem`, `AssignmentStatus`, `GpaClass`, `GpaSnapshot`, `IcsEvent`, `IcsPreviewResponse`, `IcsCommitResponse`, `ClassAssignment`, `Create/UpdateAssignmentPayload`. Response shapes match the live web routes EXACTLY (`{ items }`, flat gpa snapshot, `{ events, count, truncated }`, `{ created }`, `{ assignments }`, `{ assignment }`, `{ ok }`).
- `lib/hooks/use-academia-agenda.ts`, `lib/hooks/use-academia-gpa.ts` — NEW. Agenda keyed by visible-month `[first, max(end, today+7)]` window (dedupes week tile + calendar); `keepPreviousData` so paging months never flashes empty.
- `components/academia/GpaSnapshot.tsx` — NEW. Term-GPA hero + horizontal per-class grade chips; soft "add graded items" empty state; self-hides until first fetch (no-flash-of-zero).
- `components/academia/AcademiaPlanner.tsx` — NEW. THIS WEEK agenda (grouped by day, Today/Tomorrow headings) + 6×7 month calendar (class-colored dots, tap-day to filter, prev/next month) + crunch/workload-heat banner + optimistic assignment status cycle (todo→doing→done) via PATCH. First-load spinner instead of "0 due".
- `components/academia/ImportCalendarSheet.tsx` — NEW. Two source paths converging on one review+commit: (1) paste feed URL → server PREVIEW (SSRF-guarded); (2) pick a `.ics` file via **existing** `expo-document-picker` → read text with `expo-file-system` `File().text()` → parse VEVENTs client-side (mirrors server parser) → commit directly (no URL for a local file to fetch). Select events, pick class, commit. NO new npm package.
- `components/academia/AddAssignmentSheet.tsx` — NEW. Quick-add (class chooser + title + optional YYYY-MM-DD due date) → `createAssignment`.
- `app/(tabs)/academia.tsx` — wired GPA snapshot + Planner section (with quiet "Import" + "Add" pills in a new SectionHeader action variant) above the classes grid; mounted both sheets; `refreshAgenda` invalidates all `/api/academia/agenda` SWR keys after a write (matches web's `refreshAgenda`).

**DB columns / tables touched (read-only via routes; iOS adds NO migration, NO direct table access — all through the shared web routes):**
- `class_assignments` (verified live): `id` uuid, `user_id` uuid, `class_id` uuid, `title` text, `due_date` date (nullable), `status` text (todo|doing|done), `created_at` timestamptz, `updated_at` timestamptz. — agenda READ + assignment POST/PATCH/DELETE + ICS commit INSERT.
- `user_exams`: `id`, `class_id` (nullable → class-less Mastery targets), `title`, `target_date` (agenda exam kind), `archived` — agenda READ.
- `classes`: `id`, `name`, `color`, `emoji`, `user_id`, `archived` (+ `short_code`, `professor`, `term`, `position`, `created_at`, `updated_at` for the list) — agenda/gpa/import class-metadata READ + ownership verify.
- `class_grades`: `class_id`, `earned_points`, `max_points`, `weight_pct` — gpa READ (weighted-% math server-side).
- `class_notes`: `id`, `class_id`, `archived` — classes-list note counts (pre-existing).

**API routes consumed (all pre-existing on web; iOS adds ZERO routes):**
- `GET /api/academia/agenda?from=YYYY-MM-DD&to=YYYY-MM-DD` → `{ items: AgendaItem[] }` (each: id, kind exam|assignment, date, title, status?, classId, className, classColor, classEmoji).
- `GET /api/academia/gpa` → `{ termGpa: number|null, gradedClasses: number, scale: "4.0", classes: GpaClass[] }`.
- `POST /api/academia/import-ics` → PREVIEW `{ url }` returns `{ events:[{title,date}], count, truncated }` (400 + generic msg on bad/blocked URL); COMMIT `{ classId, events }` returns `{ created }`.
- `GET/POST /api/classes/[id]/assignments` → list `{ assignments: ClassAssignment[] }` / create `{ assignment }` (201).
- `PATCH/DELETE /api/classes/assignments/[assignmentId]` → `{ assignment }` / `{ ok: true }`.
- `GET /api/classes`, `GET /api/classes/recent-notes`, `GET /api/academia/onboarding` (already consumed pre-§7).

**Sign-offs:** `ios-qa-tester` ✅ (classes CRUD unaffected; GPA snapshot renders + self-hides while loading + soft empty when ungraded; agenda THIS WEEK + selected-day + month dots render; assignment add via sheet + optimistic status cycle PATCH with rollback-on-error; ICS happy path URL-preview + file-pick parse; malformed file → "not a calendar" guard, non-VCALENDAR rejected; workload banner appears at ≥3 items in a 3-day window, red at ≥4; no-flash-of-zero verified (spinner not "0"); empty states for no-classes / nothing-due / nothing-to-import). `ios-code-reviewer` ✅ (response keys match web exactly; additive core change; functional setState in toggles; one benign exhaustive-deps warning on `toggleAll` reading `events.length` — matches web's pattern). `ios-design-hig` ✅ (Bebas/JetBrainsMono treatment, gold accents, glass surfaces consistent with the hub; quiet secondary pills don't fight the primary gold "Add class" oval). `ios-design-accessibility` ✅ (calendar cells, agenda rows, GPA chips, event rows all carry `accessibilityRole` + descriptive `accessibilityLabel`/`accessibilityState`; status cycle announces; 44pt min targets on month-nav + back/import/add controls; the gorhom Sheet respects iOS reduce-motion; FadeIn entrances only). `ios-docs-writer` ✅ (CHANGELOG + vault Daily). `ios-parity-tracker` ✅ (this row).

2. **Email digest** is a server-side cron with no client UI on either platform — untouched, not broken, nothing to port.
3. **GPA is UNWEIGHTED** (no `classes.credits` column exists) — iOS faithfully mirrors web's unweighted term mean. Credit-weighting is a shared-server enhancement if ever wanted.
4. **ICS file-pick parses client-side** (the server only fetches URLs; a local file has no URL to fetch). The parser mirrors the server's RFC-5545 logic (line unfold, SUMMARY, DTSTART date, [today-7d, today+365d] window, cap 200) so both paths produce identical event sets. If the picker module is absent in a build, the file path degrades gracefully to "paste a link instead."

## 2026-06-11: Web-replication Section 6 — SOCIAL (friends + requests + search + feed + circle + nudges + DMs) (iOS-only port, LOCAL, not built)

**Status:** ✅ Code ready + verified LOCALLY. iOS `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors**. Web `npx tsc --noEmit` = **0 errors** (shared `@lionade/core` social API extended — additive, web doesn't import `socialAPI`). `expo export --platform ios` clean (Hermes 8.98 MB, single bundle). NOT built, NOT submitted. Committed on `main` in `~/Desktop/lionade-ios`, not pushed. Owner: `vp-ios`.

**Web social inventory (shipped vs stubbed):** `/social` is a two-pane bulletin board. SHIPPED: friends list (online-first sort), pending requests (accept/decline), outgoing requests (cancel/undo), relationship-aware search/add (Add / Accept / Requested / Friends), Circle Pulse chips (online / requests / your-rank / nudges-left), Weekly Showdown rival card, Squad Goal bar, Circle weekly-Fang leaderboard polaroids (per-friend challenge + nudge), Activity Feed (friends' reward events), in-app DM threads (realtime, arena-result chips interleaved), nudges (5/day budget, 1/pair/day, 4 fixed presets), notifications tab, Past Lobbies tab. No blocking/unfriend exists on web (DELETE only cancels an OUTGOING pending request; there is NO unfriend-accepted endpoint and NO block table) — so neither platform has them.

**iOS gap found (vs current web):** the iOS Social tab was v1 — friends list + pending + a SILENTLY-BROKEN search. Two drifts were live bugs: (1) `@lionade/core` `socialAPI.search` read `res.data.results` but the web route returns `{ users }` → search always empty; (2) `PendingRow` PATCHed `/api/social/friends/<id>` with `{ status }`, a route that does NOT exist on web (web PATCHes `/api/social/friends` with `{ friendshipId, action }`) → accept/decline 404'd. Missing entirely: outgoing requests, feed, circle, showdown, squad goal, nudges, DMs, pulse chips, relationship-aware search actions.

**What changed (iOS):**
- `packages/lionade-core/src/api/social.ts` (the web-repo copy iOS resolves via tsconfig path) extended with: `acceptRequest`/`declineRequest` (correct PATCH body), `cancelRequest` (DELETE `?id=`), relationship-aware `search` (returns `{ users }` with `relationship` + `friendshipId`), `feed`, `nudgeBudget`/`sendNudge`, `messages`/`sendMessage`. New types (FeedItem, CircleRank, NudgeBudget, DirectMessage, ArenaChatEvent, Relationship, CosmeticFields). iOS-repo mirror kept identical.
- `lib/hooks/use-friends.ts` — exposes outgoingRequests + `hydrated`; adds accept/decline/cancel/acceptFromSearch wrappers (fixed endpoint); search returns `.users`. 8s poll.
- `lib/hooks/use-social-feed.ts`, `lib/hooks/use-nudges.ts` — NEW. Feed/circle (30s) + nudge budget (60s).
- `lib/hooks/use-messages.ts` — NEW. Per-friend DM thread; realtime `messages` INSERT (filter `receiver_id=eq.<me>`, append + mark-read inbound from this friend); **AppState foreground → tear-down + re-subscribe + revalidate** (backgrounded WS dies on iOS); unsubscribe on unmount/friend-change; keepPreviousData OFF to prevent cross-thread bleed.
- `app/(tabs)/social.tsx` — full rewrite: pulse chips, showdown, squad goal, circle polaroids (challenge → /arena, nudge → modal), activity feed, friends list → DM, pending accept/decline (FIXED), add-friend modal (search + outgoing/undo), nudge modal. Skeletons gate empty copy (no-flash-of-zero).
- `app/social/chat.tsx` — NEW DM thread screen (bubbles, arena-result chips, say-hi empty state, KeyboardAvoidingView composer). Registered in root stack `_layout.tsx`.
- `lib/hooks/use-leaderboard.ts` — **§3 leaderboard-visibility flag CLOSED**: added `.eq("profile_visibility", "public")` so the iOS ELO board honors visibility like web's `getLadderLeaderboard`/`getEloLeaderboard` (excludes friends-only + private users). Single chokepoint — all iOS leaderboard surfaces route through this hook.

**DB columns / tables / API routes / realtime channels (for schema verification):**
- **Tables/columns READ:**
  - `profiles`: `id`, `username`, `avatar_url`, `arena_elo`, `is_online`, `last_seen`, `level`, `profile_visibility`, `equipped_username_effect`/`equipped_frame`/`equipped_name_color`/`equipped_avatar_aura` (passed through, NOT rendered — see cosmetics flag). (online heartbeat write `is_online`/`last_seen` is web-only; iOS does NOT write the heartbeat in §6.)
  - `friendships`: `id`, `user_id`, `friend_id`, `status` (`pending`/`accepted`/`declined`), `created_at`.
  - `messages`: `id`, `sender_id`, `receiver_id`, `content`, `read`, `created_at` (read; INSERT via route; UPDATE `read=true` on inbound realtime).
  - `coin_transactions`: `id`, `user_id`, `amount`, `type`, `description`, `created_at` (read server-side by feed route).
  - `nudges`: `id`, `sender_id`, `recipient_id`, `preset`, `created_at` (server-side).
  - `arena_chat_events`: `id`, `match_id`, `user1_id`, `user2_id`, `winner_id`, `player1_score`, `player2_score`, `wager`, `created_at` (server-side, surfaced in DM timeline).
  - `notifications`: written server-side by friends/nudge routes (gated on `friend_requests` notif pref).
- **API routes consumed:** `GET/POST/PATCH/DELETE /api/social/friends`, `GET /api/social/search?q=`, `GET /api/social/feed`, `GET/POST /api/social/nudge`, `GET/POST /api/social/messages?friendId=`. All pre-existing on web; iOS adds NO routes.
- **Realtime channel:** `social-chat-<me>-<friend>-<rand>` → `postgres_changes` INSERT on `public.messages` filtered `receiver_id=eq.<myUserId>`. Subscribe per open thread; AppState-resume reconnect.
- **NO writes** to `profiles.coins` / ELO / any reward column introduced (reward-integrity safe). Message send + friend mutations go through the authed server routes.

**Privacy-pref enforcement (mirrors web exactly):**
- `profile_visibility = 'public'` → enforced SERVER-SIDE by the web search route (non-public users never surface in iOS search) AND by the iOS leaderboard fix.
- `friend_request_from` / `show_activity_feed` / `online_status` → web does NOT enforce these on the friends/feed routes today (they gate only the notification ping via `friend_requests`, or are Settings-surfaced toggles the routes ignore). iOS mirrors web 1:1 by consuming the same routes — it does NOT invent a client-side gate web lacks. **Flagged for Sam** (see below).

**Scoped OUT / deferred:**

- **Blocking / unfriend** → does NOT exist on web (no endpoint, no table). Not built on either platform. The old iOS context-menu "Remove friend" stub is gone (friend rows now open the DM thread).
- **Online heartbeat write** → web writes `profiles.is_online` on a 120s interval; iOS §6 reads online state but does not add the heartbeat writer (own follow-up; flagged).

**Sign-offs:** `ios-dev-realtime` ✅ (DM channel subscribe-on-mount / unsubscribe-on-unmount per friend; AppState foreground reconnect + revalidate; mark-read on inbound; no leaked channels). `ios-qa-tester` ✅ (friends/requests happy path; accept/decline hits correct endpoint; search returns results + relationship actions; private users excluded from search; feed respects the same route as web; nudge budget + per-pair lock; no-flash-of-zero on all skeletons). `ios-code-reviewer` ✅ (search + accept/decline drift bugs fixed at the core; no reward writes; per-thread SWR key prevents cross-thread bleed; lint 0). `ios-design-hig` ✅ (44pt tap targets on all request/nudge/send actions; slide-up modals; chevron affordance on friend rows). `ios-design-accessibility` ✅ (accessibilityRole/Label on every actionable row — accept/decline/add/accept-from-search/undo/nudge/send/friend-open/challenge; Dynamic Type via font families; VoiceOver reads tier + online state on friend rows). `ios-docs-writer` ✅ (iOS CHANGELOG + vault Daily). `ios-parity-tracker` ✅ (this row; §3 leaderboard-visibility flag CLOSED).
