## 2026-06-05 — Bluff Trivia host vote-save failure (web-only, no iOS row)

**Status:** 🚫 N/A (deliberate no-row decision — Lionade Party is web-only V1 per project memory; iOS Party has not shipped, so there is no equivalent flow to fix today).

Root cause: `app/api/party/bluff/rounds/route.ts` inserts the round's truth as a `bluff_answers` row with `user_id = creator` as an FK placeholder. The table has `UNIQUE (round_id, user_id)`. When the host (creator) tried to submit their own fake, `app/api/party/bluff/rounds/[id]/answer/route.ts` looked for an existing fake row (`is_truth=false`) found none, ran a fresh INSERT that collided with the truth row's `(round_id, user_id)` and returned 500 "Couldn't save answer". The host's fake never landed, write phase advanced to vote, and the stale write-phase error stayed on screen because `castVote` didn't clear `error` state on click (and there was no phase-transition cleanup). The vote itself was technically savable; the pink "Couldn't save answer" Sam saw was the bleed-through from write phase.

Fix:
1. New migration `supabase/migrations/20260605230000_bluff_answers_truth_fake_coexist.sql` drops the legacy 2-column UNIQUE and replaces it with `UNIQUE (round_id, user_id, is_truth)` so a single user can own both the truth-row placeholder and their fake in the same round.
2. Round-create endpoint now picks a non-creator room member as the truth-row's FK placeholder when one exists, so the host's fake insert no longer collides even on un-migrated databases (Sam's live game).
3. Answer endpoint self-heals: if the user's only existing row is the truth (host case), re-point that truth row's `user_id` to another room member before inserting the fake. Belt-and-suspenders for the deployed-before-migration window.
4. `components/party/BluffView.tsx` clears stale `error` on phase change and at start of `castVote`, gates vote buttons behind a `voting` in-flight flag so a fail re-enables for retry without losing state.

iOS stance: Lionade Party iOS port is paused. When it ships, the same UNIQUE invariant + answer-route logic + write→vote error clearing must be mirrored. **No iOS row required today.**

**Files touched (web):** `supabase/migrations/20260605230000_bluff_answers_truth_fake_coexist.sql` (new), `app/api/party/bluff/rounds/route.ts` (truth-owner picks non-creator member), `app/api/party/bluff/rounds/[id]/answer/route.ts` (self-heal collision), `components/party/BluffView.tsx` (clear stale error on phase change + voting in-flight flag).

---

## 2026-06-05 — Sketchy round-end deadlock unstick (web-only, no iOS row)

**Status:** 🚫 N/A (deliberate no-row decision — Lionade Party is web-only V1 per project memory; iOS Party has not shipped, so there is no equivalent reveal screen to unstick).

Root cause: the reveal-phase "PLAY ANOTHER ROUND" / "BACK TO LOBBY" CTAs in `components/party/SketchView.tsx` were gated on `isHost`, which is derived from `room.host_user_id === me`. If the original host disconnected (or their tab dropped the realtime WS before the `/leave` `pagehide` handler fired), `host_user_id` kept pointing at the no-longer-active user. Every remaining player saw "Waiting for host" with no way out — the round-end state had no auto-advance, the vote card only fires `onAutoPlayAgain` once 75% have voted AND that callback was also `isHost`-gated, and the next-round POST endpoint actually only requires room membership.

Fix:
1. Derived `effectiveHostUserId` from the players list — if the real `host_user_id` is not in active players, promote the longest-connected active player (deterministic across clients).
2. Added a visible 12s auto-advance countdown on the reveal phase ("Next round in 8s") that triggers `startRound()` from the effective host's client when it hits 0.
3. After 6s on reveal, non-effective-host clients also see a "START NEXT ROUND" fallback button as belt-and-suspenders.
4. Re-pointed the vote auto-decide callbacks at `isEffectiveHost` so the threshold path works the moment a stale host pointer is detected.
5. Real-host-only Rematch button stays gated on the original `isHost` (server `/rematch` requires real host).

iOS stance: Lionade Party iOS port is paused per `~/Desktop/lionade-vault/lionade/Features/Party.md` and current memory. When the iOS port resumes, mirror the same instinct: derive `effectiveHostUserId` client-side from the same player list, run a visible reveal-phase countdown, fall back to a non-host advance button after a short delay. The server-side contract is unchanged — `POST /api/party/sketch/rounds` only requires `isMember`. **No iOS row required today.**

**Files touched (web):** `components/party/SketchView.tsx` (effective-host derivation, reveal auto-advance + fallback unlock, render branch swap).

---

## 2026-06-05 — Vocab AddWordForm "Lock it in" save fix (web-only, no iOS row)

**Status:** 🚫 N/A (deliberate no-row decision — web client bug; iOS Vocab Add flow has not shipped, so there is no equivalent client payload to fix today).

Root cause: `components/Vocab/AddWordForm.tsx` `handleSave` for general banks built a payload with `term`, `term_definition`, and `user_definition`, but never included `definition_source`. The server validator (`app/api/vocab/words/route.ts`) requires `wikipedia | ai | manual` and 400s otherwise, surfaced to the user as the red toast "definition_source must be wikipedia, ai, or manual". Two adjacent bugs fell out of the same trace:

1. Language-bank save was also missing `source_lang` / `target_lang` in the payload, which the route validates against the bank row — silently broken for any user who tried to save a translation.
2. The success toast typed the response as `{ ok: true; fangs: number }` but the route returns `{ coinsAwarded }`, so the toast read "+undefined Fangs!" even on success.

Fix: pass `definition_source` (state's `defineSource`, falling back to `"manual"` when the user typed their own without a Wikipedia/AI fetch), pass `source_lang` + `target_lang` on the language path, and read `coinsAwarded` from the response. Failure path already preserves user input — `resetForm` runs only on success.

iOS stance: iOS Vocab Add flow is not yet implemented (`lionade-ios/` has Vocab read surfaces but no add-word screen). When `vp-ios` ports the Add flow, mirror the payload contract: general banks send `{ bank_id, term, term_definition, definition_source, user_definition? }`; language banks send `{ bank_id, word, translation, source_lang, target_lang, user_definition? }`. **No iOS row** — no iOS surface to port to yet; instinct documented for the future port.

**Files touched (web):** `components/Vocab/AddWordForm.tsx` (handleSave passes `definition_source`, `source_lang`, `target_lang`; reads `coinsAwarded` from response).

---

## 2026-06-05 — Mastery Session Report pill moved out of FAB collision (web-only, no iOS row)

**Status:** 🚫 N/A (deliberate no-row decision — web-side layout collision between two web-only floating widgets; iOS Mastery does not have the equivalent collision).

The Session Report pill (`components/Mastery/StudySheetButton.tsx`, mounted on `app/learn/mastery/[examId]/page.tsx`) was a `fixed bottom-right` element at `bottom-[56px] md:bottom-[118px]` showing either "🔒 X / 33%" while locked or "Session Report" once unlocked. It overlapped vertically with the global `LaunchDock` ("+" launcher) at `right-4 md:right-6 bottom-[88px] md:bottom-[24px]`, which clipped the right side of the pill and hid the denominator in the locked progress label. Sam reported he couldn't see his quota at a glance.

Fix: added a `placement` prop ("header" | "floating") to `SessionReportFab`. The Mastery session page now mounts it inline in the top header row, alongside the elapsed-time chip, where it is content-anchored and never collides with floating chrome. The `floating` variant is retained for future surfaces with no header slot, with its `bottom` offset bumped (`md:bottom-[96px]` desktop / `bottom-[158px]` mobile) so even that variant clears the global LaunchDock if reused.

iOS stance: iOS Mastery (`lionade-ios/src/screens/mastery/...`) renders the equivalent Session Report affordance inline within its own header / toolbar — there is no iOS counterpart to the web `LaunchDock` global "+" button (iOS uses the tab bar + native modals for the equivalent quick-launch surfaces). The collision physically cannot occur on iOS. **No iOS row required.**

**Files touched (web):** `components/Mastery/StudySheetButton.tsx` (added `placement` prop + sized variant; floating bottom values bumped to clear LaunchDock as a safety net), `app/learn/mastery/[examId]/page.tsx` (moved the SessionReportFab call from the bottom of the page into the header row next to the elapsed-time chip; removed the old fixed mount).

## 2026-06-05 — Stale Resume banner root-cause fix (web-only, no iOS row)

**Status:** 🚫 N/A (deliberate no-row decision — web-side data-flow bug; iOS reads `profiles.active_session` through `@lionade/core` but does not call `/api/daily-drill` on every dashboard mount, so the same loop does not exist there).

Root cause of Sam's perpetually-showing "ACTIVE — Resume your daily drill. Click to rejoin" banner: `app/api/daily-drill/route.ts` GET unconditionally called `setActiveSession(userId, "daily_drill", today, "player")` whenever it returned questions. That GET fires from `components/DailyDrillWidget.tsx` on every dashboard mount + SWR revalidation, so the active_session pointer was being re-pinned (with a fresh `joined_at`) every time the user merely loaded the dashboard — even if they never opened the drill modal. Both prior fixes (8a90ed7 client staleness + 13240e2 auto-reap) were correct as far as they went, but the re-pin happened FASTER than the 2h staleness threshold could fire, so the banner came back instantly on the next dashboard load.

Fix: removed the GET-side pin entirely; moved `setActiveSession` to `app/api/daily-drill/state/route.ts` GET, which the `DrillModal` calls exactly once on mount (the real "user actually started drilling" signal). The 60s server-side AFK reaper + the existing `/api/daily-drill/complete` clear path handle teardown for genuine drill sessions.

iOS stance: iOS reads `profiles.active_session` via `@lionade/core` but the iOS daily-drill flow does not have the equivalent dashboard-mount fetch loop (the iOS dashboard surfaces drill via a different hook that does not call the pin-side-effect route). No iOS port required. When iOS Daily Drill ships its modal-open flow, it should call the same `/api/daily-drill/state` GET to set the pointer — that's the canonical "start a drill" signal cross-platform.

**Files touched (web):** `app/api/daily-drill/route.ts` (removed `setActiveSession` import + call), `app/api/daily-drill/state/route.ts` (added `setActiveSession` import + call on GET).

---

## 2026-06-05 — SWR provider hydration fix (web-only, no iOS row)

**Status:** 🚫 N/A (deliberate no-row decision — web-only race condition in the SWR provider boot sequence; iOS has no analogous bug).

`components/SwrProvider.tsx` was mounting `swrConfigNoPersist` on first render then swapping to `swrConfig` (the persisted variant) in a post-mount `useEffect`. The swap discarded the SWR cache mid-handshake and raced with auth state flipping null→object, so `/social` painted blank on cold load and cross-nav felt like a full reload. Fix: mount `swrConfig` from the very first render — `getProvider()` returns an empty `Map` synchronously (DOM matches the server) and `readyPromise` resolves on a microtask after the first commit, so there's no hydration mismatch.

iOS already gates splash-screen dismissal on `readyPromise` per the Phase B shared `createPersistedSwrProvider` contract (the iOS adapter wraps AsyncStorage, which is genuinely async — so the iOS app waits explicitly rather than rendering an empty cache on first frame). No analogous race exists on iOS, no port required.

---

## 2026-06-04 — Lionade-Pardy V1 (web)

**Status:** Web ships. iOS port: ❌ missing.

Lionade-Pardy on web. iOS port: same deck schema (`lib/pardy/decks.ts` is pure TS with no DOM/Next deps — copy verbatim into `@lionade/core` or `lionade-ios/src/pardy/decks.ts`), same `/api/games/pardy/submit` endpoint (no client-side amount; server reads `tile.value` and applies the Fang multiplier server-side). Render the 5×5 board with a `FlatList` of 25 tiles in row-major order or a custom grid; modal flow is identical. Reuse the same `lib/pardy/match.ts` normalizer client-side only if you want optimistic hints — the server is the source of truth.

**New files (web):**
- `lib/pardy/decks.ts` — `PardyDeck` / `PardyCategory` / `PardyTile` types + 3 starter decks + `getDeck` / `tileId` / `parseTileId` / `getTile`.
- `lib/pardy/match.ts` — `normalizePardyAnswer` (lowercase + diacritic-strip + prefix-strip + punctuation-strip + whitespace-collapse) + `matchPardyAnswer` (exact-equality on normalized form, NO fuzzy/Levenshtein in V1).
- `app/api/games/pardy/submit/route.ts` — POST { tileId, answer } → { correct, correct_answer, awarded?, newCoins? }. Server-side validation + Fang grant; client never tells the server how many Fangs to award.
- `app/games/pardy/page.tsx` — Deck picker → board → modal → Game Over. Solo V1; multiplayer + Final Pardy queued.

**Modified files (web):**
- `app/api/games/reward/route.ts` — added `pardy_correct` to MAX_REWARD_BY_GAME (cap 200, the top-tile value). Not currently used by the Pardy submit flow but kept for future client-side bulk grants if needed.
- `app/games/page.tsx` — added 5th ticket "PARDY" routing to `/games/pardy` (gold-themed, MicrophoneStage icon, mini 3×3 gold-grid animation, gold ambient orb).

**Multiplayer:** intentionally **skipped V1**. Solo is the must-ship and ships. The party room infra is reusable for V2 (host picks a tile, locks the buzz-in window, tracks per-player scores) but the V1 footprint is already large enough.

**Final Pardy round:** V2. V1 ends on a Game Over screen showing the total earned.

**Answer matching:** exact equality after a normalization pipeline (lowercase + Jeopardy-prefix strip + diacritic strip + article strip + period strip + non-alphanumeric-to-space + whitespace collapse). NO Levenshtein in V1 — Jeopardy rewards correctness, and authors can add explicit `alternateAnswers` to cover synonyms. The `damerau-levenshtein` package is already in node_modules so V2 can opt in per-deck.

**Anti-cheat:** the client never tells the server how many Fangs to award. Server reads the authored `tile.value` and applies the user's Fang multiplier. Multi-claim on the same tile within a session is suppressed client-side (V1); V2 will persist per-user-per-deck progress in Supabase and refuse double-claims server-side.

**`npx tsc --noEmit` clean.** No commit per directive. Owner: dev-frontend.

Shop daily-rotation polish on web. iOS port mirrors: same deterministic-by-UTC-date `todaysDrops()` algorithm (seed = `YYYYMMDD` integer, stable shuffle by `hash(seed + sku.id)`, slice 5), same `/api/shop/trending` endpoint (top 3 SKU ids by `purchase_history` count over last 7 days, empty-fallback so client picks 3 from `FEATURED_ITEMS`), same FOMO cap-countdown UI for the Limited Time strip when ported. ## 2026-06-04 — Solo mode resume on web (Phase 2 Tier 3)

**Status:** Web ships. iOS port: ❌ missing.

Refresh-resumable state for the six solo experiences: Mastery, Daily Drill, Quiz (/quiz), Blitz (/compete/blitz), Roardle (/games), Timeline (/games). Each game autosaves its in-flight state (debounced 500ms) to a server-side row, and hydrates on mount. Mastery restores the partial socratic textarea draft + question pointer. Daily Drill records each answered question_id so refresh skips past already-answered questions. Quiz, Roardle, and Timeline present a "Resume your last X? [Resume] [Start fresh]" banner because the user might want a clean slate. Blitz mid-run resume is intentionally NOT implemented — the timer/score/streak live inside the BlitzMode component's hooks/refs (too coupled to live React refs); page just clears the state row on mount as a breadcrumb. Heartbeats are now wired across all solo game pages so the AFK reaper sees them as active.

**Files shipped (web):** `app/api/mastery/sessions/[id]/state/route.ts` (new, GET + POST, upserts mastery_session_state, rate-limited 60/min as `mastery-state`). `app/api/daily-drill/state/route.ts` (new, GET + POST, idempotent question-id union into answered_question_ids, rate-limited 30/min as `daily-drill-state`). `app/api/quiz/state/route.ts` (new, GET ?game_type=X + POST { game_type, state }, deletes row on `state: null`, rate-limited 60/min as `quiz-state`, allowed game_types: quiz | blitz | roardle | timeline). `middleware.ts` (modified — three new rate-limit rules above presence-heartbeat). `components/Mastery/MasteryActionArea.tsx` (modified — SocraticInput accepts `initialValue` + `onChange` so partial text can be re-hydrated + persisted from the parent page). `app/learn/mastery/[examId]/page.tsx` (modified — GET state on mount, debounced POST on every keystroke, clear partial_answer on socratic submit, useHeartbeat already in place). `components/DailyDrillWidget.tsx` (modified — modal hydrates today's answered_question_ids on open + filters out already-answered, POSTs each answer to /state, useHeartbeat fires while modal mounted). `app/quiz/page.tsx` (modified — resume banner on select screen, debounced autosave during quiz phase, clear on finish, useHeartbeat during quiz phase). `app/compete/blitz/page.tsx` (modified — clear state row on mount, useHeartbeat during blitz phase). `app/games/page.tsx` (modified — autosave + resume prompts for Roardle and Timeline, clear on game-over, useHeartbeat during roardle/timeline).

**iOS port should mirror via the same APIs.** The three endpoints (`/api/mastery/sessions/:id/state`, `/api/daily-drill/state`, `/api/quiz/state`) are platform-agnostic and accept the same JSON shapes. Recommended iOS implementation: AsyncStorage cache for offline-resilient writes (debounce server writes 500ms, optimistic local restore on mount). On reconnect, replay the pending write. Server response wins on timestamp tie-break. Use `partial_answer = null` on Mastery socratic submit (matches web). For Daily Drill iOS, call POST `/api/daily-drill/state` { questionId, wasCorrect } after each answer and skip already-answered ids on mount. Blitz mid-run resume is also out-of-scope on iOS V1 for the same reason (timer state coupling).

**State shape per game (jsonb in quiz_session_state):**
- quiz: `{ subject, activeTopic, difficulty, blitzMode, questions[], currentIndex, answers[] }`
- blitz: `null` (V1 — not persisted)
- roardle: `{ wordLength, targetWord, guesses[], won }`
- timeline: `{ events[], order[], correctlyPlacedCount }`

Mastery state-row shape: `{ current_question_id, partial_answer, answered_count, correct_count }` (columns on the dedicated table, not jsonb).

`npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No commits per directive. Owner: dev-frontend.

## 2026-06-04 — Party Phase 2 Tier 2 (web ships; iOS port should mirror)

Phase 2 Tier 2 features layered on top of the Phase 1 session-lifecycle backbone. Web ships all six concerns in one pass; iOS port should mirror.

**Files shipped on web:** `components/party/PostRoundVoteCard.tsx` (new — shared voting card surfaced on every post-round screen for Sketchy / Bluff / Poker Face; polls `/api/party/rounds/[id]/votes?round_kind=...` every 3s, exposes Play Another / Back To Lobby buttons to non-hosts, dual-progress-bar tally for both kinds, fires `onAutoPlayAgain` / `onAutoBackToLobby` exactly once when the server first reports a winner). `components/party/MidGameInviteModal.tsx` (new — host-surface modal showing the full invite URL + copy button + the room code in big type for verbal sharing; Escape closes, backdrop-blur, SSR-safe origin capture). `components/party/SketchView.tsx` (modified — replaced the V1 stub thumbs-up with the real PostRoundVoteCard wired to roundKind="sketch"; added client-derived spectator detection comparing `me.joined_at` against `round.started_at`; added host pause/resume corner buttons with broadcast-only V1 — PAUSE / RESUME events added to SKETCH_EVENTS; round timer freezes while `pausedAt !== null`; paused overlay over canvas; pausedOffsetMsRef banks elapsed pause time across multiple pause cycles; spectator notice replaces guess input for mid-round joiners; host invite button corner-pinned next to pause; invite modal mounted at view root). `components/party/BluffView.tsx` (modified — migrated `ch.subscribe()` -> `subscribeResilient(ch, { label })`; added PostRoundVoteCard on reveal phase; forfeit-this-round button on write phase submits sentinel "__forfeit__" via existing /answer endpoint, local `forfeited` flag flips the submit button to "FORFEITED THIS ROUND"; fixed-position host invite button + modal). `components/party/PokerFaceView.tsx` (modified — migrated `ch.subscribe()` -> `subscribeResilient(ch, { label })`; PostRoundVoteCard on mid-game reveal only — final game-over screen keeps its existing "BACK TO LOBBY · RUN IT BACK" flow; fixed-position host invite button + modal). `components/party/PartyScoreboard.tsx` (modified — accepts optional `spectatorUserIds: Set<string>` prop; renders a small "SPECTATING" badge next to non-drawer spectators). `app/games/party/[code]/page.tsx` (modified — migrated room-state channel `ch.subscribe()` -> `subscribeResilient(ch, { label, silentOnGiveUp: true })`; silent so it doesn't double-toast on top of the game channel's own connection-loss toast). `lib/party/realtime-channels.ts` (modified — added `PAUSED` and `RESUMED` to `SKETCH_EVENTS`).

**Pause/resume scope decision:** shipped as REAL broadcast-only V1, NOT a no-op placeholder. The host pause button is functional today — clicks fire a PAUSED broadcast, every client freezes their local round timer + disables canvas input, the paused overlay shows for everyone. Resume bumps a local `pausedOffsetMsRef` so the remaining seconds are preserved across multiple pause cycles. The deliberate V1 limitation: no DB persistence (`sketch_rounds.paused_at` would have required a migration + two new endpoints, which would have exploded scope per spec). Refresh-mid-pause means the new tab won't see the paused overlay until the next PAUSE broadcast lands; their local timer will keep counting against `round.started_at`. The next round resets all pause state cleanly. The persistent-pause path (DB column + /pause + /resume routes + server-arbitrated remaining duration) is V3 work.

**Spectator-detection approach:** CLIENT-DERIVED, NOT server-flagged. The spec called both options OK for V1; client-derived ships without a `party_room_players.joined_mid_round` column or backend change. The derivation: a player whose `joined_at` > current round's `started_at` is spectating THIS round (drawer always excluded — they were already in the room). Computed via `useMemo` in SketchView; the room-wide set is passed to PartyScoreboard for the "SPECTATING" badge, and the per-self flag replaces the guess input with a "You joined mid-round" notice. Resets naturally on next round because the new `round.started_at` is fresh. The server-flag path would handle the edge case of a player who joined just before round-start and gets misclassified — fine for V1; V3 may upgrade.

**Vote auto-decide wiring:** PostRoundVoteCard polls `/api/party/rounds/[id]/votes` every 3s (spec floor is 2s; 3s matches the rest of the room-state polling cadence). When the server first reports `winner: "play_again" | "back_to_lobby"`, the card's `winnerFiredRef` gate fires the appropriate callback exactly once. Both host and non-host receive the broadcast — only the host's callback advances the round (non-host gets the next round/lobby via the room channel broadcast anyway). 3s polling on the votes GET is well under the 10/min/IP rate limit (20 polls/min per active reveal screen at most, and the limit is per-user not per-route — see `middleware.ts` party-vote rule).

**Bluff forfeit-this-round:** the simple sentinel-answer path. The user taps "I'm out — skip me this round" -> the existing `/api/party/bluff/rounds/[id]/answer` route accepts a literal `__forfeit__` string. The vote phase will surface that sentinel like any other fake; the existing scoring naturally excludes it from "you fooled N people" credit because no one will vote for `__forfeit__` once they see it (and if they do, the fooled-points still flow normally — the worst case is the forfeiter accidentally fools someone, which is fine). A cleaner separate /forfeit endpoint that filters the sentinel out of the vote pool is V3. Local `forfeited` flag also disables the submit button so the user can't accidentally double-submit.

**Mid-game friend invite:** purely client-side. The join flow already handles late joiners (they fall into spectator mode via the new derivation). The modal exposes the full URL + a copy button + the room code in big type. ~20 minutes of work, no server change required. Resume Banner picks them up on landing because their `active_session` pointer is set the moment they hit `/api/party/rooms/[code]/join` (Phase 1 wiring).

**iOS bearing:** identical pattern shape. PostRoundVoteCard ports cleanly to `components/party/PostRoundVoteCard.tsx` in lionade-ios with the same SWR/poll cadence (use a 3s setInterval inside a useEffect, or React Native's `useInterval` equivalent — both work). MidGameInviteModal ports to a `react-native-modal` or `@gorhom/bottom-sheet` bottom sheet, with `Share.share({ url })` as the native invite primitive INSTEAD of the clipboard-copy approach (better UX on phone — invokes iMessage / WhatsApp / etc. directly). subscribeResilient should move to `@lionade/core/realtime` if iOS doesn't already have its own copy. Spectator detection is platform-agnostic — same `useMemo` shape ports identically. Host pause/resume on iOS needs the same broadcast-only V1 (PAUSED / RESUMED events) plus a `pausedOffsetMsRef` equivalent; the corner button placement should respect iOS safe-area insets (Expo's `useSafeAreaInsets`). Bluff forfeit-this-round is a simple button + sentinel send, ports 1:1. **Watch out on iOS:** the 3s vote-poll inside a useEffect needs to be paused when the app goes to background (use `AppState` listener) to avoid burning the 10/min rate limit when the player is in another app — web doesn't hit this because the heartbeat hook already manages the visibility transition.

`npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No commits per CEO directive. Owner: `dev-frontend`.

---

## 2026-06-04 — Session lifecycle backend wiring (server-side, no iOS row)

Deliberate no-row decision. Server-side wiring of the Phase 1 session-lifecycle plumbing. The schema + RPCs (shipping in parallel via dev-database) define the canonical contract; iOS hits the same `/api/presence/heartbeat`, `/api/cron/reap-afk-presence`, join/leave routes, vote routes, and the new sketchy `advance-phase` route once iOS gets its corresponding screen ports. NO iOS code change required — RN clients inherit the lifecycle behavior the moment they hit the same routes.

**Files shipped on web (backend):** `lib/presence.ts` (new — fire-and-forget `setActiveSession(userId, type, id, role)` + `clearActiveSession(userId)` wrappers around the `set_active_session` / `clear_active_session` RPCs; both swallow errors so presence bookkeeping never blocks a user-facing response). `lib/party/round-votes.ts` (new — shared `computeTally(supabase, roundId, roomId)` + `resolveRoundRoom(supabase, roundId, roundKind)` helpers; threshold rule >=75% of eligible voters OR everyone-voted with tie-break to play_again). `app/api/presence/heartbeat/route.ts` (new — POST, accepts optional `{ type, id }`, calls `ping_presence` RPC, 30/min/IP rate limit). `app/api/cron/reap-afk-presence/route.ts` (new — GET, auth via `Authorization: Bearer $CRON_SECRET` OR `?key=` query param, calls `reap_afk_presence` RPC, returns reaped row count). `app/api/party/sketch/rounds/[id]/advance-phase/route.ts` (new — POST, transitions `phase` from celebrating -> reveal with a 2.5s server-side minimum-hold guard so a malicious client can't skip the overlay for the room). `app/api/party/rounds/[id]/vote/route.ts` (new — POST upserts into `party_round_votes` by (round_id, user_id), returns live tally + threshold state). `app/api/party/rounds/[id]/votes/route.ts` (new — GET, `?round_kind=sketch|bluff|pokerface` required, returns same shape as the POST response). `vercel.json` (modified — added a `crons` entry firing `/api/cron/reap-afk-presence` every minute; Vercel's auto-attached `Authorization: Bearer $CRON_SECRET` header is accepted by the route). `middleware.ts` (modified — two new rate-limit rules: `presence-heartbeat` 30/min/IP for `/api/presence/heartbeat`, `party-vote` 10/min/IP matching both `/vote` and `/votes` under `/api/party/rounds/[id]/`).

**Routes modified (JOIN/LEAVE wiring map):** `app/api/party/rooms/[code]/join/route.ts` (set_active_session on first-time join AND on rejoin AND on already-member refresh, role=host|player). `app/api/party/rooms/[code]/leave/route.ts` (clear_active_session, also on the already-ended-room fast path). `app/api/arena/queue/route.ts` (set_active_session for both players the moment the match row is created, after the queue rows are flipped to matched). `app/api/competitive/queue/route.ts` (set_active_session for every team_a + team_b participant inside `createMatch` after `seedRoundsForMatch`, roles `team_a` / `team_b`). `app/api/mastery/exams/[id]/sessions/route.ts` (set_active_session on both the resume + create-new paths, role=player). `app/api/mastery/sessions/[id]/complete/route.ts` (clear_active_session in both the active-close path and the already-closed idempotent return). `app/api/daily-drill/route.ts` (set_active_session on GET when we actually return questions — empty/completed states do NOT pin, since there's nothing to be active in). `app/api/daily-drill/complete/route.ts` (clear_active_session on both the fresh-completion and already-completed paths). `app/api/save-quiz-results/route.ts` (clear_active_session — quiz START is stateless and doesn't set a pin; the clear here catches any legacy/dangling pin from prior sessions as a safe no-op).

**Sketchy round-end DB phase persistence:** `app/api/party/sketch/rounds/[id]/complete/route.ts` modified — the SELECT now also pulls `phase / winner_user_id / celebrating_started_at` (so future idempotent re-fires can use them), the correct-guesses query orders by `guessed_at ASC` so the first row's `user_id` IS the round winner (NULL on timeout), and the round-end UPDATE now writes `phase: "celebrating"` + `winner_user_id` + `celebrating_started_at` alongside the legacy `ended_at` in ONE update. Frontend still reads the live broadcast for instant render — the persisted phase is for the reload-during-celebration case (a player who refreshes during the 2.5s overlay lands back on the celebration, sees the rest, instead of skipping to the reveal). The companion `/advance-phase` route transitions celebrating -> reveal after the 2.5s hold; server enforces the minimum-hold so a fast-fingered client can't shortcut the overlay for the room (returns 409 with `remainingMs`).

**Cron path picked:** Path A (Vercel cron) — `vercel.json` had no prior cron entry and no Supabase pg_cron setup, so Path A wins on "use what's already in the codebase." Caveat: Vercel cron's MINIMUM granularity is 1 minute, not 30s. With the migration's 60s presence TTL, a 1-minute reap cadence is still correct (a row at most 119s old can survive one cycle, still well under any user-perceived "they're gone" threshold). If sub-minute reaping turns out to matter, swap to Supabase Edge Function + pg_cron later — same RPC, no route changes.

**Vote routes auto-decide rule (server side):** `>=75%` of `total_eligible` (active room players, `left_at IS NULL`) for any vote_kind sets `threshold_reached: true` + `winner: <that kind>`. If everyone has voted but no kind hit 75%, `threshold_reached: true` + winner = majority with ties resolving to `play_again` (the optimistic default — keep playing rather than dump back to lobby). Host UI can act on `threshold_reached` to fire the next-round / back-to-lobby transition automatically.

**iOS bearing:** zero. Backend is platform-agnostic — iOS hits the same routes. The `lib/presence.ts` + `lib/party/round-votes.ts` helpers are server-side TypeScript and have no client counterpart. When iOS implements the post-round vote UI it'll call the same POST `/api/party/rounds/[id]/vote` route and read the same tally shape; the only consideration is that the iOS keyboard handling around the vote modal might want to debounce the upsert (vote-vote-vote rapid taps would otherwise burn the 10/min rate-limit faster than on web).

`npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No commits per CEO directive. Owner: `dev-backend`.

---

## 2026-06-04 — Session lifecycle Tier 1 frontend UX (web ships; iOS port should mirror)

Session lifecycle Tier 1 UX on web. iOS port should mirror: useActiveSession via TanStack Query or SWR-RN (reads profiles.active_session through Supabase RLS), useHeartbeat via AppState listener (React Native has native foreground/background events that map cleanly to web's visibilitychange — the 30s grace becomes the AppState background timer), ResumeBanner mounted in the root navigator (Expo Router's _layout) with the same gold-stripe + dismiss-per-session sessionStorage equivalent (`AsyncStorage` keyed by `${type}:${id}`), cross-game redirect via the same per-user realtime channel `user:<userId>` listening for `active_session_changed` broadcasts. iOS port should also wrap Supabase realtime subscribes with `subscribeResilient`-equivalent helper (exponential 1/2/4/8/16s backoff + single toast on give-up) — the helper lives at `lib/realtime-resilient.ts` on web and should move to `@lionade/core` if the iOS implementation is identical (almost certain).

**Files shipped on web:** `lib/active-session.ts` (new — `ActiveSession` type + `useActiveSession()` SWR hook with revalidateOnFocus + 30s refreshInterval + postgres_changes listener on profiles row; `urlForActiveSession()` switch maps each ActiveSessionType to its canonical URL; `labelForActiveSession()` gives banner copy). `lib/use-heartbeat.ts` (new — `useHeartbeat(type, id)` fires `/api/presence/heartbeat` every 10s while both args non-null, plus visibilitychange listener that keeps beating for 30s after the tab goes hidden then pauses, and immediately pings + resumes when visible again). `lib/realtime-resilient.ts` (new — `subscribeResilient(channel, opts)` wraps `.subscribe()` with exponential 1/2/4/8/16s backoff on CHANNEL_ERROR / TIMED_OUT / CLOSED; emits a single `toastError("Connection lost. Try refreshing.")` after MAX_ATTEMPTS=5; resets attempts counter on SUBSCRIBED; opt-in `silentOnGiveUp` for sibling channels that share a user-facing connectivity signal). `components/ResumeBanner.tsx` (new — fixed-position z-[55] above the Navbar, gold left-edge stripe via `boxShadow: "inset 4px 0 0 0 #FFD700"`, dismiss-per-session via sessionStorage keyed by `${type}:${id}`, hides when pathname already matches the active session's canonical URL, no JS motion library — CSS-only with `motion-reduce:transition-none` guard). `components/SessionLifecycle.tsx` (new — no-DOM component that subscribes to `user:<userId>` realtime channel for `active_session_changed` broadcasts; on event, mutates the SWR pointer + router.replace's the user to the new session's URL unless they're on a SAFE_LIST page like /login or are mid-question on a SOFT_CONFIRM page like /quiz/* / /learn/mastery/* / /compete/arena/* in which case it toasts with a "Join now" CTA instead of hard-redirecting; also skips redirect when the user has dismissed the banner for that specific session id). `app/layout.tsx` (modified — imports + mounts `<SessionLifecycle />` and `<ResumeBanner />` inside ToastProvider, both above the existing DemoModeBanner; ResumeBanner is fixed z-[55] so it visually sits above the Navbar's z-50; DemoModeBanner is inline-flow above Navbar; both can coexist if a demo user is mid-party-game — the resume banner is action-bearing so it sits visually first). `app/games/party/[code]/page.tsx` (modified — imports useHeartbeat + useActiveSession + useToast; `useHeartbeat("party_room", code)` near the top of the component; reconcile-on-mount effect using `reconcileFiredRef` toasts the user with a Resume CTA when their active_session pointer doesn't match the URL room code, soft-redirect via toast action rather than hard router.replace so they're not silently re-routed mid-flow). `app/learn/mastery/[examId]/page.tsx` (modified — imports useHeartbeat; calls it with `useHeartbeat(sessionId ? "mastery_session" : null, sessionId)` immediately after the existing `useActiveTime(sessionId)` call; the two hooks are intentionally separate concerns — useActiveTime posts elapsed-seconds deltas to the mastery session table, useHeartbeat posts presence pings to the universal `/api/presence/heartbeat`). `app/compete/arena/[mode]/[matchId]/page.tsx` (modified — imports useHeartbeat; `useHeartbeat("competitive_match", matchId)` fires the moment we have a matchId in the URL, no need to wait for the full match-load response). `components/party/SketchView.tsx` (modified — replaced the inline `ch.subscribe((status) => {...})` with `subscribeResilient(ch, { onSubscribed, onUnsubscribed, label: "sketch-room:${room.code}" })`; cleanup now calls `handle.cancel()` BEFORE `supabase.removeChannel(ch)` so the wrapper stops scheduling retries before the channel disappears under it). `components/party/SketchCanvas.tsx` (modified — same resilient wrapper, `silentOnGiveUp: true` so the stroke channel doesn't double-toast on top of the room channel's "Connection lost" toast). 

**Resilience strategy in detail:** the wrapper captures status transitions through a single `onStatus` callback passed to `ch.subscribe()`. On CHANNEL_ERROR / TIMED_OUT / CLOSED, it schedules a re-subscribe at delay BACKOFF_MS[attemptsAfterFailure] where BACKOFF_MS = [1000, 2000, 4000, 8000, 16000]ms. On SUBSCRIBED, the attempt counter resets so a 30-minute session with intermittent drops doesn't accumulate failures over the wall-clock. After MAX_ATTEMPTS=5 consecutive failures WITHOUT a SUBSCRIBED in between, the wrapper gives up — it emits `toastError("Connection lost. Try refreshing.")` ONCE (gated by `everSubscribed` so an initial-mount failure doesn't toast — that's the page's problem to surface), then stops. The caller's `cancel()` short-circuits all of this; we always check `cancelled` before scheduling or firing a retry, so a fast unmount races cleanly with an in-flight backoff.

**Subscribers migrated:** SketchView (room channel — sketch round_started/round_ended/guess), SketchCanvas (strokes channel — broadcast STROKE + CLEAR_CANVAS). Flagged for V1 follow-up (NOT migrated in this pass): BluffView (`components/party/BluffView.tsx` line 132, single `ch.subscribe()` with no status callback), PokerFaceView (`components/party/PokerFaceView.tsx` line 208, same pattern), and the room-state channel in `app/games/party/[code]/page.tsx` (line 149, also `ch.subscribe()` with no status callback). These three currently silently die on CHANNEL_ERROR and the user only learns when a broadcast goes missing. Should migrate in a follow-up — straightforward 4-line swap per call site.

**ResumeBanner ↔ DemoModeBanner interaction (precedence call):** both banners can coexist on screen (a demo user mid-party-game is a valid state). ResumeBanner is `fixed top-0 z-[55]` (above the Navbar's z-50); DemoModeBanner is `inline-flow` immediately above the Navbar in the layout tree. The fixed ResumeBanner sits visually first because the "resume" prompt is action-bearing (a missed click costs the user gameplay state), while the demo prompt is informational. The Navbar already has its own top padding tolerance so it doesn't crash into the fixed ResumeBanner. NO z-index war between the two — they sit in different stacking contexts. If the design team later wants the demo banner to stack BELOW the resume banner with both visible, the only change needed is to make DemoModeBanner also `fixed` with `top` set to ResumeBanner's height (currently inlined, so it sits below the resume banner naturally on most screens).

**In-session pages where heartbeat is wired:** party room (`app/games/party/[code]/page.tsx`), mastery session (`app/learn/mastery/[examId]/page.tsx`), competitive match (`app/compete/arena/[mode]/[matchId]/page.tsx`). **In-session pages flagged for follow-up wiring:** Daily Drill (under `app/learn/paths/`) — the drill surface is multi-page (subject pick → drill questions) and doesn't have a single "session active" handle the way mastery does; needs a backend-side decision on whether each drill question batch counts as one active_session or each subject-pick→submit cycle is its own session. Quiz pages (`app/quiz/*`) — quiz session IDs are minted server-side on first answer rather than on quiz-screen mount, so we'd need to either (a) pre-mint a session on mount, or (b) call useHeartbeat with the session id once the first answer fires; needs a small backend RPC change to enable (a) cleanly. Flagged as Phase 2 work.

**iOS bearing:** identical hooks shape, identical broadcast contract. Move `subscribeResilient` to `@lionade/core/realtime` so iOS doesn't reimplement the wrapper. Move ActiveSession types to `@lionade/core/session-lifecycle` so the JSONB column contract is one file across both clients.

`npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No commits per CEO directive. Owner: `dev-frontend`.

---

## 2026-06-04 — Session lifecycle schema V2 (cross-platform unified — one schema, two clients)

Session lifecycle schema on web. iOS port reads profiles.active_session for resume logic + writes presence via the same RPC. Cross-platform unified — one schema, two clients.

**Migration:** `supabase/migrations/20260604000000_session_lifecycle.sql` (not yet applied to remote — CEO runs `npx supabase db push` after review).

**Schema shipped:** `profiles.active_session jsonb` (GIN-indexed, UPDATE revoked from authenticated/anon — only SECURITY DEFINER RPCs can mutate) · `presence_heartbeats` table (user_id PK, last_ping_at, active_session_type/id mirror) · `sketch_rounds.phase` + `winner_user_id` + `celebrating_started_at` (promotes V1 broadcast phase to persisted DB column so reload-during-celebration works on V2) · `party_round_votes` (generic for sketch/bluff/pokerface; unique(round_id,user_id); SELECT gated by party_room_players membership join) · `mastery_session_state` (user+session PK, current_question_id + partial_answer + counts) · `daily_drill_progress` (user+drill_date PK, answered_question_ids uuid[] + partial_answer) · `quiz_session_state` (user+game_type PK, jsonb state for quiz/blitz/roardle/timeline/flashcards).

**RPCs shipped:** `ping_presence(user_id, type, id)` — SECURITY DEFINER, caller-id check, called every 10s during active session · `reap_afk_presence()` — service_role only, sweeps heartbeats older than 60s, clears profiles.active_session + leaves stale party_room_players, returns reaped count, called by 30s cron · `set_active_session(user_id, type, id, role?)` — caller-id check, sets pointer + writes initial heartbeat · `clear_active_session(user_id)` — caller-id check, clears pointer + deletes heartbeat.

**iOS port plan:** iOS uses the same Supabase project so the schema lands automatically on push. iOS clients should (1) read `profiles.active_session` on app launch + `useFocusEffect` to detect a resumable session and route to the right screen, (2) call `set_active_session` on join, (3) call `ping_presence` on a 10s interval while the screen is focused (clear the interval in `useFocusEffect`'s cleanup + on AppState background), (4) call `clear_active_session` on explicit leave. The reap_afk RPC needs no iOS work — it's a server cron. Mastery / Daily Drill / Quiz resumes on iOS use the same Tier 3 tables (same RLS owner-only policy works for both clients).

**iOS-side TODOs (when iOS ports this):** `ios-dev-data` writes a `useActiveSession` hook that wraps the 4 RPCs · `ios-platform-bridge` confirms heartbeats stop while AppState=background and resume on foreground · `ios-design-hig` decides whether to show a banner ("You have a Mastery session in progress — tap to resume") on app open vs auto-routing · `ios-parity-tracker` flips this row to "fully ported" when iOS lands the hook.

---

## 2026-06-04 — Sketchy round-end V1 (web ships; iOS port should mirror)

Sketchy round-end V1 on web. iOS port should mirror via Reanimated + Skia stamp + same server-pushed celebrating phase. Vote mechanic + reconnect-to-room + cross-game redirect queued for V2 on both platforms.

**Files shipped on web:** `components/party/RoundEndOverlay.tsx` (new — full-screen overlay component, State A winner avatar with gold ring + State B hourglass + "ROUND WON BY {NAME}" / "TIME'S UP" + word reveal + NEXT ROUND footer with shimmering ink dots; framer-motion enter/exit; role=status aria-live=polite; Esc dismiss; reduced-motion = fade only). `components/party/SketchView.tsx` (modified — added `celebrating` to phase union; `celebrating` state object `{ winner, word, started_at }`; `firstCorrectRef` captures the first correct guesser's identity live from the GUESS broadcast for winner attribution; `completeRound` now broadcasts ROUND_ENDED with BOTH a `celebrating` payload AND the legacy `reveal` payload; ROUND_ENDED handler enters celebrating then a separate effect transitions celebrating→reveal after CELEBRATING_HOLD_MS=2500 using server `started_at` so late joiners only see the remainder; canvas wrapper now renders centered GUESSED/TIME'S UP stamp + four green corner brackets during celebrating; AnimatePresence-mounted RoundEndOverlay at view root; host-only post-round controls (PLAY ANOTHER ROUND / BACK TO LOBBY); non-host post-round shows "Waiting for host to pick what's next" + ink-dot ambient + thumbs-up button that logs to console for V1). `components/party/SketchCanvas.tsx` (modified — new `disabled?: boolean` prop; pointer handlers (`onPointerDown` / `onPointerMove` / `onPointerUp`) early-return when `disabled === true`; wrapper div gets `pointer-events-none` class when disabled; cursor reverts to `default`. Internal stroke paint loop + strokesRef untouched per CEO directive). `app/globals.css` (modified — two new keyframe blocks: `pa-canvas-stamp` 0.55s var(--ease-out-quart) scale 1.45→1.05→0.97→1.0 with rotate(-8deg) preserved at all keyframes + opacity 0→1→0.95; `pa-canvas-corner` 0.75s var(--ease-out-quart) scale 0.6→1.15→1.0 + box-shadow glow bloom→steady. Both added to the existing prefers-reduced-motion guard at the bottom of the `pa-*` block). 

**Motion timings + easing:** Canvas stamp uses ease-out-quart (`cubic-bezier(0.25, 1, 0.5, 1)`) for the "slam down" character with a peak-overshoot-settle profile (1.45 → 1.05 → 0.97 → 1.0) over 0.55s. Each of the four green corner brackets uses pa-canvas-corner over 0.75s ease-out-quart, staggered 60ms apart (i*60ms via inline animationDelay) — the staggered bloom reads as ink spreading outward from a center rather than a chorus. RoundEndOverlay backdrop fades in over 0.22s ease-out-expo (`cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1)`); card scales 0.92→1.0 + lifts 12px over 0.42s ease-out-expo. Winner avatar scales 0.7→1.0 over 0.4s, 120ms after the card (matches the "lands slightly after" beat from the spec); hourglass uses a -180→0deg rotateZ enter for 0.55s with 80ms stagger. Headline + subtext slide-fade in with 8px / 6px y-offsets at 180ms / 260ms staggers behind the card. NEXT ROUND footer dots reuse existing `pa-ink-dot` 1.4s ease-in-out infinite. All motion is GPU-only (transform / opacity / box-shadow). prefers-reduced-motion freezes both new keyframes via the existing `pa-*` guard and the overlay degrades to fade-only via the `reduced` branch on every motion.div.

**Host vs non-host post-round UX:** HOST sees two big CTAs side-by-side: `PLAY ANOTHER ROUND` (gold btn-gold primary, calls `startRound` which fires a new round in the same room) + `BACK TO LOBBY` (outline secondary, calls `onReturnToLobby` which routes via the existing room-state machine to phase 'lobby' so any game can be picked next). NON-HOST sees a centered card: "Waiting for host to pick what's next" + three pulsing ink dots (reused `pa-ink-dot` infinite loop), plus a thumbs-up `ANOTHER ROUND` button styled in soft green (`bg-emerald-400/8 border-emerald-400/30 text-emerald-200`). The thumbs-up `onClick` calls `console.log("[Sketchy] thumbs-up: another round (V1 stub)")` — V2 will tally votes server-side and surface the result to the host.

**Server-pushed phase — design call:** The spec says "server emits `phase: \"celebrating\"`." I shipped this as a CLIENT-DERIVED celebrating state driven by an enriched ROUND_ENDED broadcast (payload now carries `{ celebrating: { winner, word, started_at }, reveal }`) rather than as a persisted DB phase column on `sketch_rounds`. The acceptance criteria say "the spec just requires that ALL clients agree on when the celebration is showing" and this implementation meets that: every client receives the same broadcast at the same time and reads the same `started_at` so the 2.5s hold elapses in lockstep regardless of when each client mounts the timeout (late joiners compute remaining = HOLD - elapsed-since-server-started_at, so the overlay self-shortens for them and everyone lands on reveal at the same wall-clock moment). The trade-off vs a true DB phase: a player who reloads DURING the 2.5s window doesn't see celebrating (they'd land on reveal because the broadcast already passed) — for V1 this is acceptable because reveal IS the natural next state. A DB-phase port would require a schema change (`sketch_rounds.phase TEXT` + `winner_user_id UUID` + `celebrating_started_at TIMESTAMPTZ`) plus a fetch on the existing round-state catch-up; iOS port can decide to upgrade to persisted phase if the reload case matters there. Existing iOS clients reading the same broadcast will get the celebrating payload for free once iOS Sketchy ships.

**Anti-cheat preserved:** `disabled` is in ADDITION to `readonly` — a drawer is still not readonly during celebrating (we want their previous strokes to keep painting), but `disabled === true` hard-blocks any new pointer events AND adds `pointer-events: none` on the canvas wrapper. The strokesRef + internal paint loop in SketchCanvas were not touched per CEO directive — only the input gates + a CSS class on the wrapper.

**Known V2 gaps (flagged, deliberate non-ship):** (1) voting mechanic — non-host thumbs-up is wired but does not POST anywhere yet, the host doesn't see the tally; V2 spec needs to define a `sketch_round_post_votes` table or a transient channel-broadcast vote pool. (2) reconnect-to-room — a player who closes the tab mid-round isn't auto-rejoined when they return; V2 needs a "last-active-room-code" cookie or DB column. (3) cross-game redirect — a player doing a quiz in the dashboard when the host starts a new game doesn't get pulled in; V2 needs a session-scoped "you have an active party room" floating dock.

**iOS bearing:** identical phase machine on iOS once Sketchy ports — same SKETCH_EVENTS.ROUND_ENDED payload shape, same `started_at`-driven hold. iOS-side equivalents: `RoundEndOverlay.tsx` → Reanimated 3 scaffold (BlurView backdrop + spring-config'd card scale + winner avatar with Skia gold-ring sweep); canvas stamp + green corners → Reanimated shared values + Skia `<Group>` overlay on the existing Sketch canvas (Skia is GPU-native so the stamp won't compete with stroke render); `disabled` prop → same boolean flag on the iOS SketchCanvas RN component, no-op the gesture handler when true. Reuse the same client-derived approach unless reload-during-celebration is deemed important enough to motivate a DB-phase upgrade.

`npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No commits per CEO directive. No migrations applied to remote. Owner: `dev-frontend`.

## 2026-06-03 — Shared demo account for tester onboarding (web ships; iOS port should mirror)

Demo account on web. iOS port should mirror: same `DEMO_USER_ID = d3500000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000` and the same server guards apply universally (the guards run on `/api/*` which both clients hit). iOS-side UI for "try the demo" can reuse the same auth flow — call `supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email: 'demo@getlionade.com', password: 'LionadeDemo2026!' })`. A persistent banner equivalent to web's `components/DemoModeBanner.tsx` should render at the top of every iOS screen when `user.id === DEMO_USER_ID` (subtle, dismissable for the session via `AsyncStorage`, "Create your own account" CTA routes to the Sign Up screen). Server filters for leaderboards + social search are platform-shared (both `lib/db.ts` and `app/api/social/search/route.ts` exclude the demo id), so iOS gets that for free. **Files shipped on web:** `supabase/migrations/20260603122412_demo_account.sql` (auth.users + profile + 1 language bank + 1 general bank + 8 vocab words + 2 notes + name_fx_rainbow equipped; idempotent ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING; not pushed to remote — Sam runs `npx supabase db push`); `lib/demo-guard.ts` (universal `DEMO_USER_ID` + `isDemoUser` predicate, safe to import from client bundles); `lib/demo-guard-server.ts` (server-only `demoBlockedResponse()` 403 helper, kept separate from the universal guard so `next/server` doesn't bleed into client bundles); `components/DemoModeBanner.tsx` (subtle one-line banner inside AuthProvider, just above Navbar in `app/layout.tsx`). **Endpoints guarded:** `/api/change-username` POST (username fixed to 'demo'); `/api/social/messages` POST (DM spam mitigation); `/api/social/friends` POST (friend-request spam mitigation); `/api/vocab/banks/[id]` PATCH when `is_public: true` (block public-publish of demo banks to Discover — private edits still allowed so the demo's own banks remain demo-able); `/api/stripe/checkout` POST (no subscription on shared Stripe customer); `/api/stripe/fang-purchase` POST (no IAP on shared customer). **Endpoints filtered (not blocked):** `lib/db.ts` `getLeaderboard` / `getEloLeaderboard` / `getLadderLeaderboard` all `.neq("id", DEMO_USER_ID)`; `/api/social/search` GET excludes demo via `.neq("id", DEMO_USER_ID)`; `/api/social/feed` GET filters demo from friend-id list as belt-and-suspenders (the friend-request guard already prevents real users from friending the demo). **Login page UI:** new section below the login form labelled "Want to try without signing up?" — a single button "Use the demo account" (auto-fill + auto-submit, decision rationale below) + a visible monospace credential strip so testers can copy manually if their browser autofill gets in the way + "Shared demo account. Don't store personal data here." disclosure. Login page also now honors `?signup=true` (used by the demo banner's "Create your own account" link) to pop the Sign Up tab on mount. **Endpoints intentionally NOT guarded:** `/api/shop/purchase` POST (the spec explicitly allowed Fang cosmetic purchases for the demo so testers can browse the shop with 5000 seed Fangs — IAP path is already routed to Stripe which IS blocked); `/api/auth/*` password change (Supabase handles password updates client-side via `supabase.auth.updateUser`, not via our API — flagged as a known gap, the demo password can be rotated by re-running the migration). **Profile edit (display name/avatar)** goes directly to the Supabase client from `app/profile/page.tsx` rather than through our API surface, so route-level guards do NOT apply; demo profile edits land in `profiles` directly. Mitigation flagged but not implemented in this pass — would require either an RLS policy that rejects writes when `auth.uid() = DEMO_USER_ID`, or routing profile edits through a new `/api/me/profile` endpoint. **Auto-submit vs highlight decision:** auto-submit (rather than just populating fields + highlighting Sign In). Friendlier for testers who click expecting to BE logged in, not to be one click closer. `handleLogin`'s existing double-submit guard prevents button-mash races. Manual paths still work — both credentials are printed as selectable monospace text. **iOS bearing summary:** identical UUID and guards apply universally; iOS port needs the equivalent `DemoModeBanner` and a login-screen affordance. No iOS-side schema work — the migration covers both platforms. Owner: `dev-backend`. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No commits per CEO directive.

## 2026-06-03 — Shop V2 UI: Identity & Status Pack (web-only, iOS needs Reanimated + Skia port)

Web-only frontend wave on top of the parallel Shop V2 catalog + schema + grant-wiring waves. Web ships the visible surface for the 18-SKU pack: (1) new reusable `components/AnimatedUsername.tsx` (props: `username`, `effect: 'none'|'rainbow'|'fire'|'holographic'|'gold'|'glitch'|'galaxy'`, `size: 'sm'|'md'|'lg'`); (2) ~140 lines of GPU-only CSS in `app/globals.css` under a clearly-marked "Shop V2 — Animated Usernames" block (background-position + transform only, all degrade to static colored variants under `prefers-reduced-motion`); (3) wired into 7 visibility surfaces — Navbar dropdown header, Dashboard "Welcome back" hero, Profile header (overview h1 + sidebar `@username`), Leaderboard (podium top-3 + every row), Social (friends list + pending requests), Party scoreboard tiles + Party lobby tiles. Mastery does NOT render the user's own username anywhere visible, so it's deliberately a no-wire (noted in `lib/use-username-effect.ts`). (4) Shop page extended: EXCLUSIVE Founder Badges section at top of Cosmetics tab (3 SKUs, cap countdown "247 of 1000 remaining", sold-out lock overlay when server reports cap closed); USERNAME EFFECTS section with LIVE PREVIEW of each effect on the user's actual username (try-before-you-buy); PREMIUM BANNERS section (5 Fang-purchasable animated banners with looping gradient preview tiles); PREMIUM REAL MONEY ONLY section (4 cash-only banners reusing PremiumCard); Inventory tab unioned with `/api/cosmetics/owned` and grouped under "Identity & Status" with source badges (Purchased / Earned / Founder). (5) Equip button on owned username effects PATCHes `/api/me/equip` body `{ slot: 'username_effect', cosmetic_id }`. (6) Read-side helper `lib/use-username-effect.ts` exposes `useEquippedUsernameEffect()` (SWR-cached, 60s dedupe, revalidate-on-focus, `shouldRetryOnError: false` so 404s during backend rollout fail silent) + `resolveRowUsernameEffect(value)` for list-API rows. **Backend gaps flagged for follow-up:** `/api/cosmetics/owned` is the only Shop V2 backend route already shipped by dev-backend in the parallel server wave above; `/api/shop/founder-caps` (cap countdown source) and `/api/me/equip` (equip writes) are NOT yet live and are called defensively — the UI falls back to "no effect" / static cap label on 404; equip shows an inline toast on failure. The `equipped_username_effect` column was added defensively as an OPTIONAL field on list-API row shapes (PartyPlayer, LbEntry, Friend, PendingRequest) so existing payloads remain valid; backend list endpoints need to start returning it for OTHER users' effects to render. Today, only the LOGGED-IN user's own equipped effect renders cross-surface (injected at each surface's "me" branch via the hook). **Hardest effect to nail visually:** `holographic` — the `::before` sparkle pseudo-element fights the `-webkit-background-clip: text` masking on the parent (because `background-clip: text` makes the element's background only visible THROUGH the glyphs); landed on a positioned-outside sparkle anchored to top-right of the inline span, which reads as a charm next to the name rather than a glow on the letters. **`galaxy` was the second-hardest** — true starfield-on-letters requires SVG noise + `mask-image`, which works on Chrome/Safari but is fragile; settled for three radial-gradient mask layers + the rainbow underlay, which gives a starfield FEEL without GPU-blowing repeat-render cost. **iOS bearing:** when the iOS app ports this, equivalents needed: (a) the 6 effects re-implemented via Reanimated 3 shared values driving Skia text gradients (CSS `background-clip: text` + `background-position` has no React Native equivalent — `react-native-linear-gradient` + a masked Text via `@shopify/react-native-skia` is the closest); (b) the live-preview tile pattern uses the same `<AnimatedUsername>` mounted in the SKU card, which translates 1:1 to RN; (c) founder badge cap countdown is plain `<Text>`; (d) prefers-reduced-motion = `AccessibilityInfo.isReduceMotionEnabled()` listener; (e) equip route is platform-shared. The effect string ids ("rainbow" etc.) should move to `@lionade/core/shop/username-effects.ts` on the port pass so both clients share the same enum + the `resolveUsernameEffect()` validator. **Awkward integration callout:** Profile page renders the user's hero `<h1>` inside the `OverviewSection` sub-component rather than the top-level `ProfilePage`, so `useEquippedUsernameEffect()` had to be CALLED TWICE (once in `ProfilePage` for the sidebar `@username`, once in `OverviewSection` for the h1) since props for that sub-component are typed as a fixed `SharedProps` interface and threading a new field through every sub-section (Edit / Avatar / Personalization / Privacy / Security / Activity / Notifications / About all take the same SharedProps) would have meant 8 unrelated changes — calling the hook locally keeps the diff small. SWR dedupes the underlying fetch, so the second call is free. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No commits per CEO directive. Owner: `dev-frontend`.

## 2026-06-03 — Shop V2 Identity & Status Pack catalog + auto-grant wiring (server, no-row)

Deliberate no-row decision. Server-only catalog + grant-wiring delivery on top of the parallel V2 schema wave. No client UI in this lane. **Catalog (`packages/lionade-core/src/constants/shop-catalog.ts`):** adds five new `ItemType` values (`username_effect`, `animated_banner`, `founder_badge`, `earned_medal`, `profile_flair`) and 18 SKUs across them. **Animated username effects (Fangs):** `name_fx_rainbow` 1500 / `name_fx_fire` 2000 / `name_fx_holographic` 3000 / `name_fx_gold` 2500 / `name_fx_glitch` 3500 / `name_fx_galaxy` 5000. **Premium cash variants** for the three top tiers in PREMIUM_ITEMS: `name_fx_holographic_premium` $1.99 / `name_fx_glitch_premium` $1.99 / `name_fx_galaxy_premium` $2.99 — render the full WebGL/particle treatment while the Fangs SKUs are the static-gradient version (renderer picks highest-fidelity variant the user owns). **Premium Fang banners:** `banner_interstellar` 3000 / `banner_aurora` 3500 / `banner_ink_splash` 4000 / `banner_honeycomb` 4500 / `banner_tidewave` 5000. **Cash-only banners in PREMIUM_ITEMS:** `banner_premium_aurora_borealis` $2.99 / `banner_premium_cosmic_drift` $3.99 / `banner_premium_liquid_gold` $2.99 / `banner_premium_lightning` $1.99. **Founder badges:** `badge_founding_scholar` cap 1000 priceUSD $14.99 purchasable Stripe-only; `badge_lionade_og` cap 500 autoGrant; `badge_beta_witness` autoGrant pre-deploy window. **Earned cosmetics (NOT for sale):** `emblem_streak_warrior_10/30/100/365` tiers, `badge_polyglot`, `badge_knowledge_sharer`, `medal_mastery_subject_` (dynamic prefix; actual id is `medal_mastery_subject_<exam_id>` minted by the RPC). New helpers: `getFounderBadge(id)`, `getEarnedCosmetic(id)` (exact + dynamic-prefix match), `isEarnedCosmeticId(id)`. **New file `lib/cosmetic-grants.ts`:** fire-and-forget RPC wrappers — `isFounderCapOpen(client, badgeId, cap)` returns boolean (defensive false on any error so we never over-grant), `grantPolyglotBadge`, `grantKnowledgeSharerBadge`, `grantStreakEmblem(userId, tier: 10|30|100|365)`, `grantMasteryMedal(userId, examId)`. All five use `supabaseAdmin`, all five log + swallow errors. **New endpoint `GET /api/cosmetics/owned`:** aggregates `user_inventory` + `founder_grants` + `earned_cosmetics` into one `{id, type, source: 'purchased'|'founder'|'earned', acquiredAt}` list via parallel Promise.all fetches and deterministic dedupe priority (purchased > founder > earned). Each source error is non-fatal — partial data beats a 500 here. Sorted newest-first by `acquiredAt` (null last). **Existing routes touched:** `app/api/shop/purchase/route.ts` early-rejects any earned-cosmetic id with 400 "This item can only be earned, not purchased" BEFORE any DB work, then branches `founder_badge` SKUs into new helper `handleFounderBadgePurchase` that runs `is_founder_cap_open` then inserts into `founder_grants` (NOT user_inventory) with race-safe 23505 handling (409 "sold out" on cap-full, 400 "Already owned" on uniqueness violation, also detects priceUSD-priced founder badges and routes them away from the Fangs flow). `app/api/vocab/banks/route.ts` POST — after successful `kind='language'` create, fires a void async block that COUNTs the user's language banks and calls `grant_polyglot_badge` RPC if >= 3 (the just-created bank is included so the threshold can trip on the third create). `app/api/vocab/banks/[id]/clone/route.ts` — after the clone RPC returns, fires a void async block that re-reads the source bank's `(user_id, clone_count)` and calls `grant_knowledge_sharer_badge(ownerId)` RPC if >= 10 (the cloner is NOT the badge recipient — the SOURCE bank owner is). `app/api/stripe/webhook/route.ts` — `customer.subscription.created` now passes `isCreate=true` into `handleSubscriptionUpsert(sub, isCreate)` and on success (either byCustomer-id happy path OR metadata.user_id fallback path) calls `tryGrantFoundingScholar(userId, sub.id)` which checks `is_founder_cap_open('badge_founding_scholar', 1000)` then inserts into `founder_grants` with `source='stripe_subscription'` + `reference_id=sub.id`. The grant is defensive: never throws, never blocks the subscription upsert — a missed grant can be backfilled by writing the row directly. **Wiring pending (flagged for follow-up specs):** `grantStreakEmblem` is implemented but NOT yet called from any route — needs to be wired into the streak-increment site (likely `app/api/clock-in/route.ts` or wherever `advance_streak` returns the new streak count) AFTER the streak lock-in. `grantMasteryMedal` likewise needs to be wired into the Mastery session-complete route AFTER verifying final score >= 95%. Neither requires a schema change — just one fire-and-forget call site each. **Founder-cap pattern for dev-frontend** (so "Only X/1000 left" UI can mirror it): server check is `await isFounderCapOpen(supabaseAdmin, badgeId, cap)` returning boolean; for the actual COUNT (display, not gating), the data lives at `SELECT count(*) FROM founder_grants WHERE badge_id = $1` and the cap comes from `getFounderBadge(id).cap` — a small read-only endpoint is the right shape but is out of scope here. **iOS bearing:** none — server catalog + grant wiring change. iOS picks up all 18 SKUs the moment it recompiles against `@lionade/core`. The auto-grants fire regardless of which client triggered the source action (creating a bank, cloning, subscribing). iOS Shop V2 UI port is queued. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on the backend surface; one pre-existing `usernameEffect` symbol-not-found error in `app/profile/page.tsx` belongs to dev-frontend's parallel in-flight wave, NOT this delivery. No commits per CEO directive. Owner: `dev-backend`.

## 2026-06-03 — Shop V2 schema (Identity & Status Pack): founder_grants + earned_cosmetics + 4 grant RPCs

Shop V2 schema on web. iOS reads cosmetics via existing user_inventory + new founder_grants/earned_cosmetics tables; auto-grants triggered server-side via RPCs (no iOS code change needed once they read the joined view). **Web ships:** `supabase/migrations/20260603154104_shop_v2_identity.sql` — two new tables (`founder_grants`, `earned_cosmetics`) for cohort markers + achievement-unlocked cosmetics, sitting alongside the existing `user_inventory` (which continues to own equip/unequip state of purchased SKUs). `founder_grants` has UNIQUE `(user_id, badge_id)` + indexes on `badge_id` (cap-count) and `user_id` (profile render); owner-only SELECT RLS, all writes service-role only via column-level revoke. `earned_cosmetics` mirrors that shape with a `metadata jsonb` column (Mastery medals carry `{exam_id, exam_name}`, streak emblems carry `{tier_days, streak_at_grant}`, polyglot carries `{bank_count_at_grant}`, knowledge_sharer carries `{triggering_bank_id, clone_count_at_grant}`) — UNIQUE `(user_id, cosmetic_id)` makes every grant path idempotent. Retroactive grants (single transaction): `badge_lionade_og` to the first 500 by `profiles.created_at ASC` (caps at whoever is here today; remaining slots fill via the Stripe-webhook-side cap check on new signups), `badge_beta_witness` to every user with `created_at < 2026-06-04 00:00 UTC` (frozen — no new grants after deploy day). `badge_founding_scholar` NOT granted in migration; Stripe webhook gates it via `is_founder_cap_open('badge_founding_scholar', 1000)` on `subscription.created`. Four SECURITY DEFINER RPCs with caller-identity gate (`auth.uid() = p_user_id OR service_role`): `grant_streak_emblem(p_user_id, p_streak_days)` picks the highest crossed tier (10/30/100/365), `grant_polyglot_badge(p_user_id)` grants when user has 3+ language-kind banks, `grant_knowledge_sharer_badge(p_user_id)` grants when any owned bank crosses 10 clone_count (note: caller passes the SOURCE bank's OWNER, not the cloner, so the badge goes to the author whose bank got cloned), `grant_mastery_medal(p_user_id, p_exam_id, p_exam_name)` mints `medal_mastery_subject_<exam_id>` on 95%+ Mastery sessions. All four return cosmetic_id on grant, NULL on no-op (via ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING) so the frontend can fire a "new emblem unlocked" toast off the non-null. `is_founder_cap_open(p_badge_id, p_cap)` helper is SECURITY DEFINER + service-role-execute-only — two layers prevent end-users from probing cap state (which would leak cohort size + enable rush-the-cap coordination): SECURITY DEFINER bypasses RLS so `count(*)` returns the true global count rather than the owner-filtered 0, AND execute is REVOKED from authenticated/anon so a user JWT can't invoke the function at all. Migration is fully additive (no DROPs, no profile mutations, no vocab/ninny touches), wrapped in BEGIN/COMMIT, idempotent on re-run via ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING. **iOS bearing:** schema is platform-neutral. iOS profile-render UI reads `founder_grants` + `earned_cosmetics` for the viewing user via the owner-only SELECT RLS (no new endpoints needed). All auto-grants fire server-side via the RPCs called from existing web routes (Stripe webhook for founder cap, streak-increment for emblems, vocab/banks POST for polyglot, clone route for knowledge-sharer, Mastery session-end for medals) — iOS gets the grants for free when iOS hits those same endpoints, which it already does for streaks and will when iOS Vocab + Mastery port. NO iOS-only RPC needed. Shop catalog SKU additions (18 new SKUs with `acquired_via: 'founder_grant' | 'earned' | 'purchase'` routing) belong to `dev-backend`'s parallel TypeScript-only change in `packages/lionade-core/src/constants/shop-catalog.ts` — schema deliberately does NOT constrain `cosmetic_id` format so the catalog can mint any id shape. Migration NOT pushed to remote (Sam runs `npx supabase db push`); NOT committed per CEO directive. Owner: `dev-database`.

## 2026-06-03 — Word Banks V3A: public banks + clone (web schema only, iOS port mirrors)

Public banks on web. iOS port should mirror the discover/clone surface when ported; same RLS lets iOS read public banks via the same endpoints. **Web ships:** `supabase/migrations/20260603152723_public_banks.sql` — adds `is_public boolean default false`, `published_at timestamptz`, `clone_count int default 0`, `parent_bank_id uuid` (self-FK, ON DELETE SET NULL), `parent_user_id uuid` (profiles FK, ON DELETE SET NULL) on `vocab_banks`. Partial index `(clone_count DESC, published_at DESC) WHERE is_public = true` for Discover sort; partial index on `parent_bank_id` for reverse-clone lookup. RLS: existing owner-only SELECT stays; ADDS a parallel SELECT policy allowing any authenticated user to read rows where `is_public = true`. `vocab_words` ADDS a parallel public-readable SELECT policy via EXISTS-join on `vocab_banks.is_public`. Column-level UPDATE revokes on `(is_public, clone_count, parent_bank_id, parent_user_id)` from authenticated/anon — only service-role routes + the new RPC can mutate. New CHECK: `clone_count >= 0`; new CHECK: `is_public = true` implies `published_at IS NOT NULL`. New `clone_bank(p_bank_id uuid, p_cloner_id uuid) RETURNS uuid` SECURITY DEFINER RPC: validates source is public, caller-identity gate (`auth.uid() = p_cloner_id` OR service_role), creates a new bank for cloner (name suffixed " (cloned)", truncated if needed to fit 80-char cap; copies kind/lang pair/color/icon; sets parent attribution; `is_public=false`), copies all words via single INSERT...SELECT (preserves translation/term_definition/user_definition/definition_source, resets SR state — review_count=0, correct_count=0, ease_factor=2.5, next_review_at=now(), last_reviewed_at=null), increments source's `clone_count`, returns new bank id. Self-clone allowed (no infinite loop — clones are flat copies, parent pointers don't iterate). Attribution chain is one hop (clone of a clone tracks immediate parent only). `ON DELETE SET NULL` on both parent FKs means cloners' progress survives original-author deletion (best-effort attribution; data is sacred). Migration is fully additive — zero data-loss risk, no DROPs, no column-type changes. Wrapped in BEGIN/COMMIT. **iOS bearing:** schema is platform-neutral. When iOS Vocab is ported, the Discover surface reads via the same `vocab_banks` SELECT policy (any authenticated user gets public rows), and the clone action calls the same `clone_bank` RPC via supabase-js. No iOS data work needed — the migration is web-applied but every public bank becomes visible to iOS reads the moment iOS Vocab ships. Server publish/unpublish/clone routes are dev-backend follow-up (not in this schema pass). Owner: `dev-database`.

## 2026-06-03 — Word Banks V2 backend (server-side API, no iOS row)

Deliberate no-row decision. Backend-only delivery: new `/api/vocab/banks` (POST + GET), `/api/vocab/banks/[id]` (DELETE + PATCH), new `/api/vocab/define` (Wikipedia → AI cascade), and bank-aware modifications to `/api/vocab/translate`, `/api/vocab/words` (POST + GET), `/api/vocab/streak`. New helpers: `lib/vocab-banks.ts` (kind/slug/term normalization, color/icon validators, language-pair check, definition-source allowlist). New middleware rule `vocab-define` at 20/min/IP. **Contract changes the frontend must handle:** (1) `/api/vocab/streak` response shape changed from per-language-pair (`{ langPair, count, … }`) to per-bank (`{ bankId, bankName, count, lastDay, maxStreak }`); (2) `/api/vocab/words` POST body diverges by bank kind — language banks send `{bank_id, word, translation, source_lang, target_lang, user_definition?}`, general banks send `{bank_id, term, term_definition, definition_source: 'wikipedia'|'ai'|'manual', user_definition?}`; (3) `bank_id` is now required on every vocab write and on `translate`/`define` calls; (4) `/api/vocab/words` GET filter renamed from `?lang=es-en` to `?bank_id=<uuid>`. **AI fallback prompt** (Sam-tunable, in `app/api/vocab/define/route.ts`): system = "You are a study assistant. Define this term in 1-2 clear sentences, suitable for flashcard learning. No prefixes like \"X is...\" or \"This term means...\" — just the definition itself. Keep it factual and concise." + user = `Term: ${stripSentinels(term)}`; gpt-4o-mini, max_tokens 80, temperature 0.2, 15s timeout. **Cost ceiling per IP per day** (worst case, all 20/min defines are unique-term AI hits): 20 calls/min × 60 min × 24 h × ~$0.00045/call ≈ $13/day/IP — that's the pessimistic ceiling before cache + Wikipedia free path is considered. Real-world steady state with cache hit rate >70% and Wikipedia covering most named entities: <$0.30/day/IP. **iOS bearing:** none yet. iOS vocab surface is queued post-web-stabilization; the same bank model + endpoints apply when ported. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on backend files (lib + app/api/vocab + middleware). Pre-existing tsc errors in `app/learn/vocab/page.tsx` and `components/Vocab/*` belong to dev-frontend's in-flight V2 UI port. No commits per CEO directive. Owner: `dev-backend`.

## 2026-06-03 — Word Banks V2 schema (web migration; iOS port reads bank_id)

Word Banks V2 schema on web. iOS port reads `bank_id` when listing words; create/manage banks via API. Migration backfills cleanly so no iOS-side data work needed. **Web ships:** new `supabase/migrations/20260603143154_word_banks.sql` introducing `vocab_banks` (parent table, kind ∈ {'language','general'}, source_lang/target_lang only set when kind='language' enforced by CHECK, `(user_id, lower(name))` unique, trigger-derived `slug` unique per-user, default color `#A855F7`, optional emoji `icon`, FORCE row level security with owner-only CRUD). `vocab_words` gains `bank_id` (FK CASCADE), `term_definition` (the canonical answer for general banks where there's no translation), `definition_source ∈ {'mymemory','wikipedia','ai','manual'}`, a composite `(user_id, bank_id, next_review_at)` index for the per-bank due-words query, and a new CHECK that at least one of `translation` / `term_definition` is set. `vocab_streaks` is re-keyed: `(user_id, source_lang, target_lang)` PK → `(user_id, bank_id)` PK, old lang columns dropped after backfill. Backfill creates ONE "Languages" bank per existing vocab user (kind='language', icon='🌍', color='#A855F7') using that user's MOST-USED `(source_lang, target_lang)` pair (mode, tie-broken by earliest `created_at`); all of that user's vocab_words get `bank_id` set and `definition_source = 'mymemory'`. After backfill, `vocab_words.bank_id` flipped to NOT NULL. Streak backfill matches on lang pair first, falls back to attaching unmatched streaks to the user's "Languages" bank regardless of pair (polyglot edge case — collapses to one bank-streak; documented in migration footer and accepted). `advance_vocab_streak(uuid, text, text)` is DROPPED and replaced with `advance_vocab_streak(uuid, uuid)` (bank-keyed); same SECURITY DEFINER + caller-identity gate + bank-ownership check (defense in depth even for service role). Whole migration runs in BEGIN/COMMIT so a half-failed backfill rolls back fully — no orphaned vocab_words, no half-migrated streaks. `vocab_words.bank_id` + `definition_source` have column-level UPDATE revokes so user JWTs can't reparent words or forge analytics fields via direct PostgREST. Bank deletion CASCADEs to vocab_words for V2 (mitigated UI-side via two-step confirm typing the bank name); soft-delete is flagged in the migration footer for a future opt-in if user feedback warrants. **iOS bearing:** schema is now bank-scoped so the iOS Vocab port (queued under `vp-ios` after web V2 stabilizes) MUST read `bank_id` when listing words and call the new 2-arg `advance_vocab_streak` (the 3-arg signature no longer exists on the server). When iOS adds "create bank" / "switch bank" UI it goes through the upcoming `/api/vocab/banks` endpoints — no direct PostgREST writes since `vocab_banks` will enforce RLS on the user JWT. The backfill makes iOS read-side compatible the moment the migration applies — every existing word already has a `bank_id`, so the iOS list query just needs the column added. **Constraints / migration safety:** migration is NOT pushed to remote — Sam runs `npx supabase db push` after review. Not committed (working tree only). Owner: `dev-database`.
