## 2026-06-03 — Auth flash + daily-claim reload fix (web-only, no iOS row)

Deliberate no-row decision. Web-side fixes for two flicker bugs Sam reported: (1) post-login briefly shows the landing page before resolving to `/dashboard`, (2) daily Fang claim from the Navbar button feels like a full page reload. Both are web-app state-machine bugs — the iOS app has its own AuthContext + claim flow at `~/Desktop/lionade-ios/lib/auth.tsx` and doesn't inherit either issue. **Web changes:** (1) `components/ProtectedRoute.tsx` — the `(!isLoading || timedOut) && !user` redirect-to-login effect previously fired on the very first commit, before AuthProvider's onAuthStateChange listener (which seeds `user` from localStorage asynchronously) had populated state. Now gated on `mounted` + strict `!isLoading` so the seed path gets a real chance to populate before we bounce. (2) `app/login/page.tsx` — the redirect-effect's 2s hard-reload fallback (`window.location.href = dest`) raced against `handleLogin`'s own `window.location.assign("/dashboard")` and against in-flight Next.js router transitions, cancelling healthy navs. Lengthened to 6s and added a `postLoginLock` short-circuit so the effect skips entirely once `handleLogin` owns navigation. (3) `components/ClockInButton.tsx` — replaced `mutateUserStats(user.id)` (which force-revalidated every `useUserStats` consumer + collided with Supabase realtime UPDATE + the local SWR mutate) with a single optimistic `swrMutate(cacheKeys.userStats(uid), prev => ({...prev, coins: prev.coins + amount}), { revalidate: false })`. The realtime channel still reconciles from server truth if anything drifts. **iOS bearing:** none. iOS auth state machine is independent (Expo Router, custom AuthContext using AsyncStorage seed) and iOS Daily claim is on a separate screen. If iOS later reports a similar "claim feels heavy" symptom, the same optimistic-update pattern transfers — but the SWR call needs to be ported to whatever React Query / TanStack equivalent the iOS app uses (currently none — iOS reads from AuthContext directly). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No commits per CEO directive. Owner: `dev-frontend`.

## 2026-06-03 — Fluid V1 motion pass on web (iOS mirror queued)

Fluid V1 motion pass on web. iOS counterpart should mirror via Reanimated 4 springs + Skia where applicable (`ios-design-motion` owns). Press feedback + animated counters most directly portable; scroll-into-view less critical on iOS where native scroll already has momentum. **Web ships:** four GPU-only utility classes in `app/globals.css` — `.press-feedback` (100ms scale-0.96 active state, ease-out-expo), `.fluid-card-hover` (220ms translateY(-2px) + shadow-deepen, `@media (hover: hover)` gated), `.fluid-reveal` (400ms opacity+slide-up driven by IntersectionObserver via new `components/FluidReveal.tsx`), `.fluid-modal-backdrop` + `.fluid-modal-panel` (180ms backdrop fade + 220ms 0.95→1.0 panel scale). New `components/FluidReveal.tsx` is SSR-safe (renders without `.fluid-reveal` class on server, arms it client-side via `useEffect`); IntersectionObserver fires `is-visible` toggle once per element with `threshold: 0.2` + `rootMargin: 0 0 -10% 0`. Smooth-scroll already existed on `html`; added `scroll-padding-top: 72px` to clear the Navbar + reduced-motion override. **Surfaces touched:** `app/classes/page.tsx` ClassCard (fluid-card-hover + press-feedback), `app/learn/page.tsx` primary "Next Up" CTA (fluid-card-hover + press-feedback) and subject-mastery rows (press-feedback only — adjacent-row shimmer risk), `app/leaderboard/page.tsx` entry rows (fluid-card-hover replacing existing `hover:-translate-y-0.5`), `app/dashboard/page.tsx` Wallet + Leaderboard CircleStat Links wrapped in `press-feedback` shells + WEEKLY ACTIVITY chart wrapped in `<FluidReveal>`, `components/Toast.tsx` (spring-overshoot cubic-bezier `0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1` on enter, 420ms; exit stays calm ease-out-emil at 200ms), `components/FocusLockIn.tsx` + `components/DailyDrillWidget.tsx` + `components/ShareCard.tsx` modals (added `.fluid-modal-backdrop`; ShareCard panel also switched from `animate-slide-up` to `.fluid-modal-panel` for scale-from-0.95). **Skipped intentionally** (anti-goal — already polished): shop SKU cards (own `shop-tilt-card` perspective animation), dashboard CircleStat circles (own scale-105 + orbiting dot), LaunchDock, Mastery thinking-state, Party game animations. **Pattern #2 (animated Fang counter) NOT re-implemented** — discovered the existing `components/CountUp.tsx` already does this (RAF interpolation, ease-out cubic, cross-mount sessionStorage cache, reduced-motion snap) and is already wired into Navbar pill, dashboard CircleStat, and wallet hero balance. No new `AnimatedNumber.tsx` created. **Press-feedback settled values:** `transform: scale(0.96)` (4% scale-down) over `100ms cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1)` — easy to tune in `app/globals.css` if too aggressive or too subtle. **iOS bearing:** Reanimated 4 `withSpring({ stiffness: 200, damping: 18 })` for press feedback on `Pressable` components; for animated counters, the existing RAF interpolation pattern transfers as a `useAnimatedValue` hook OR Reanimated's `withTiming` (same math: ease-out cubic over 500-600ms); for modal entrance, Reanimated's `entering={FadeIn.duration(180)}` on backdrop + `entering={ZoomIn.duration(220).easing(Easing.out(Easing.exp))}` on panel reproduces the web feel. Scroll-into-view reveals less critical on iOS — native scroll has inertia and ContentOffset-driven reveals via Reanimated are heavier; suggest skipping FluidReveal equivalent unless a specific surface requests it. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No commits per CEO directive. Owner: `design-motion-web`.

## 2026-06-02 — Dual-ledger Fang schema (Path B → Path C prep)

Dual-ledger Fang schema on web. iOS port must read `profiles.coins` for display + call `update_user_coins` with appropriate source on grants/spends. When iOS ships StoreKit IAP, route those to `source='iap'` to satisfy Apple 3.1.5(b) (IAP fangs never cashable). Migration: `supabase/migrations/20260603013600_dual_ledger_fangs.sql` (not pushed; Sam runs `npx supabase db push`). Three new bigint columns on profiles (`fangs_cashable`, `fangs_iap`, `lifetime_fangs_spent`), all NOT NULL default 0, backfilled with `fangs_cashable = coins` for existing users (all current Fangs were earned via gameplay; no IAP exists yet so 100% cashable). Column-level UPDATE revokes on the new columns AND on `coins` itself for `authenticated` + `anon` — every coin mutation now MUST go through the security-definer RPC. RPC signature changed from `update_user_coins(uuid, integer, integer)` → `update_user_coins(uuid, integer, integer, text)` with `p_source` default `'cashable'`; OLD 3-arg signature DROPPED at the end of the migration so any stale caller fails loud at runtime (and via tsc once Database types regen). Debit semantics on `p_source='spend'`: decrement cashable first, dip into iap if cashable exhausted, ALWAYS increment `lifetime_fangs_spent` by abs(delta) (drives V2 60%-spend cash-out gate). UI continues to read a single combined Fang total from `profiles.coins` — the dual ledger drives WRITES only, not display, until Path C lights up. Web caller updates (every `rpc('update_user_coins', ...)` site needs `p_source`) handled by parallel dev-backend wave — tsc errors are the intentional forcing function. Owner: `dev-database`.

## 2026-05-31 — Atomic Fang mutations wave C (web-only API + DB hardening, no iOS row)

Deliberate no-row decision. Server-side concurrency hardening: every coin (Fang) mutation in the codebase was a read-modify-write (`select coins → coins ± delta → update`) which let two parallel tabs duplicate balances (credits) or escape debits. Introduced `public.update_user_coins(p_user_id, p_delta, p_min_balance)` RPC (`supabase/migrations/20260531223724_atomic_coins_rpc.sql`) — single UPDATE with `coins + p_delta >= p_min_balance` predicate, raises `insufficient_coins` (P0001) on guard violation, `security definer + locked search_path`. Refactored 5 routes to use it: `app/api/place-bet/route.ts` (debit + refund-on-insert-failure), `app/api/shop/purchase/route.ts` (debit + NEW refund-on-inventory-failure — previously a best-effort `console.warn` so the user could pay and receive nothing), `app/api/claim-bounty/route.ts` (credit), `app/api/save-quiz-results/route.ts` (4 credit sites: main quiz reward, 3rd-quiz bonus, streak milestone, daily-bet win), `app/api/spin/roll/route.ts` (clamped delta path: P0001 fallback re-reads fresh balance and zeros it out). Also in `save-quiz-results`: GET handler now gated by `requireAuth` (previously exposed profile row count); two empty `else {}` blocks deleted. `req.json()` parse failures now return 400 in `place-bet` + `games/reward` (was uncaught and 500'd). iOS has no counterpart: server-side hardening only, RN clients hit the same backend and inherit the concurrency safety transparently — no client-side change. Migration must be applied via `npx supabase db push` (Sam's call). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. Owner: `dev-database` + `dev-backend`.

## 2026-05-31 — Auth ownership wave B (web-only API hardening, no iOS row)

Deliberate no-row decision. Surgical auth-ownership pass on 8 server-side routes plus one new authed sibling endpoint: (1) added `isRoomMember(supabaseAdmin, round.room_id, userId)` 403 gate on the 3 party mutation routes that previously trusted any authed caller with a round id (`app/api/party/bluff/rounds/[id]/answer/route.ts`, `app/api/party/bluff/rounds/[id]/vote/route.ts`, `app/api/party/sketch/rounds/[id]/guess/route.ts`); (2) same gate added to the 4 round-detail GETs that leaked structural masks, reveal-phase secrets, drawing history, and Poker Face state to any authed user who guessed a round id (`app/api/party/sketch/rounds/[id]/strokes/route.ts` GET, `app/api/party/sketch/rounds/[id]/reveal/route.ts`, `app/api/party/bluff/rounds/[id]/route.ts` GET, `app/api/party/pokerface/rounds/[id]/route.ts` GET) — chose 403 over 404 to match the existing "Drawer can't guess" / "You can't vote for your own fake" 403 pattern in the same route family; (3) `app/api/auth/record-attempt/route.ts` POST now rejects `success: true` (400) — previously an attacker could clear another user's failed-attempt counter by POSTing `{ email, success: true }` and bypass lockout. New authed sibling `app/api/auth/clear-attempts/route.ts` handles the legitimate post-login clear path, gated on the caller's own session JWT (clears only `auth.email`'s counter, never an arbitrary email). `lib/auth.tsx` updated to call record-attempt only on failure and clear-attempts only on success; (4) `app/api/social/messages/route.ts` GET now runs the same friendship verification POST already did — closes a conversation-history leak where any authed user could fetch messages between any two friends + mark them as read. Middleware rate-limit added for the new `clear-attempts` route (20/15min/IP, matches record-attempt). iOS has no counterpart: all changes are server-side authorization additions; RN clients call the same backend and inherit the harder posture transparently (no client-side change needed). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. Owner: `dev-backend`.

## 2026-05-31 — AI hardening wave D (web-only, no iOS row)

Deliberate no-row decision. Server-side AI cost-runaway + prompt-injection hardening across six surfaces: (1) `stripSentinels()` helper added to `lib/ai.ts` that removes literal `</student-material>`, `</context>`, `</exam>`, `</subtopic>`, `</study-material>`, `</student-goal>`, `</student-reasoning>`, `</exam-title>`, `</subtopic-name>`, `</difficulty>` substrings (and their opening forms, case-insensitive) from any user-supplied text before it gets interpolated into a sentinel-wrapped LLM prompt — closes the "stuff the closing tag inside your input to break out of the wrapper" attack. Applied to `app/api/games/pdf/route.ts` (the truncated PDF text), `lib/ninny.ts` (the chat raw_content + flashcard fallback + title + subject), `app/api/mastery/parse/route.ts` (the student-goal input), and `lib/mastery-content.ts` (the user-controlled exam title + subtopic name on BOTH the teaching-panels and questions generators — these were previously interpolated raw with no sentinel wrapping at all; now wrapped in `<exam-title>` and `<subtopic-name>` tags with the corresponding system-prompt callout). (2) `app/api/games/pdf/route.ts` now hand-rolls a `validatePdfContent()` shape check on the parsed JSON (vocabulary/facts/concepts/timeline/keyTerms with per-field length caps + control-char and angle-bracket stripping) and returns 502 if the model's payload fails — prompt-injected output (`{"keyTerms":["<img src=x onerror=...>"]}`) no longer ships straight to the client. (3) `app/api/mastery/sessions/[id]/socratic/route.ts` now reads `socratic_turns_spent` (column already on the table), returns 429 if `>= 20`, and increments by 1 on successful Haiku calls (fallback path doesn't burn down the budget). (4) `app/api/classes/[id]/plan/route.ts` adds a 5-min per-(user, class) in-memory regenerate cooldown — `?regenerate=1` is no longer spammable; returns 429 with `Retry-After`. (5) `app/api/ninny/chat/route.ts` truncates historical assistant messages to 800 chars before re-sending them to OpenAI, preventing maxed-out 400-token replies from compounding across every subsequent chat turn. No model swaps, no Zod adoption, no Upstash migration, no per-user cost caps (those are queued for Sam's product call on cap values + UX). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. iOS bearing: all six fixes are server-side hardening on Next.js routes/libs; RN clients call the same routes and benefit transparently. The mastery socratic turn cap + classes plan regenerate cooldown will apply to iOS callers automatically when the iOS Mastery + Classes flows reach those endpoints. No iOS code change needed.

## 2026-05-31 — Code-quality wave A (web-only client fixes, no iOS row)

Deliberate no-row decision. 10 surgical client-code findings from the code-reviewer audit fixed across 3 web files (`components/Navbar.tsx`, `components/party/SketchView.tsx`, `app/games/page.tsx`): logout await race, tautological coin ternary, SketchView stale `round?.id` closure (host self-stomp on own ROUND_STARTED echo) promoted to `roundIdRef`, SketchView timer effect stale `completeRound` closure promoted to `completeRoundRef`, duplicate `if (id === "party")` GameMini branch removed, two debug probe comments removed, dead `getLetterStatus` function removed, dead `fcTotal` state removed, unused `_desc` parameter removed from `awardFangs`, notification realtime teardown switched from `channel?.unsubscribe()` to `supabase.removeChannel()` for consistency with SketchView/RoomLobby/BluffView. All web-only client code — no iOS counterpart. iOS Sketchy isn't built yet, but when it lands `ios-dev-realtime` should mirror the same `channelRef` + `subscribedRef` + `roundIdRef` + `completeRoundRef` pattern (Reanimated/AppState pause-resume makes the stale-closure bugs even easier to hit on RN).

## 2026-05-31 — Outbound fetch timeouts (web-only, no iOS row)

Deliberate no-row decision. Added 8-second `AbortSignal.timeout()` on the three remaining unbounded outbound `fetch()` calls in server-side libs: `lib/party/bluff-questions.ts` (opentdb.com), `lib/competitive/rest-countries.ts` (restcountries.com), `lib/competitive/sabotage-questions.ts` (opentdb.com). Without a timeout, a hanging upstream could pin a Vercel serverless worker against the platform's 60s hard limit (15s on hobby tier). All three already had try/catch with a curated fallback bank / empty-array fallback, so the new `AbortError` is caught and logged identically to other fetch failures — no return-shape or signature changes. iOS has no counterpart: these are server-side fetches initiated by Next.js API routes; RN clients call those same routes and benefit transparently. Web-only library code.

## 2026-05-31 — Security audit emergency fixes (web middleware + admin gate, web-only)

| Feature | Web route(s) | iOS route(s) | Web | iOS | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Admin gate on /api/question-bank/curate + rate-limit emergency tweaks** | `app/api/question-bank/curate/route.ts`, `middleware.ts` | n/a (no iOS admin routes today) | ✅ shipped | 🚫 N/A (web-only middleware change) | Three surgical fixes from a fresh security audit, CEO approved as urgent: (1) **Admin gate on `/api/question-bank/curate` POST.** Was authenticated-only with a "add admin check later" TODO; now gated on a comma-separated `LIONADE_ADMIN_USER_IDS` env var. No prior admin convention existed in the repo (no `app/api/admin/` directory, no `is_admin` column, no `admin_email`), so env-var-driven allow-list was the right primitive to introduce. GET (stats) remains authenticated-only for now. (2) **Mastery `POST /api/mastery/exams/[id]/sessions` moved into the `email` rate-limit bucket** (3/15min/IP) because it sends a Resend email on session-create — was falling to the 100/min catch-all. Required adding optional `method` filter to `RouteLimit` so the email throttle only hits POST (a hypothetical GET listing would stay on the catch-all). (3) **`/api/party/sketch/rounds/[id]/strokes` POST capped at 240/min/IP** (own `party-strokes` bucket) — drawer flushes stroke batches every ~500ms during a sketch round = ~120/min legit traffic, and the 100/min catch-all was dropping real strokes mid-game. 2x headroom. Other party routes deliberately left on the catch-all pending the broader party audit. **iOS bearing:** the middleware fix is web-only by construction (no iOS-side middleware equivalent — RN clients call the same backend, so they benefit transparently from the stroke-cap fix when iOS Sketchy is built). The **admin-gate concept should mirror on any iOS-side admin routes if/when those exist** — flag for `vp-ios` when iOS introduces its first admin-only endpoint (same `LIONADE_ADMIN_USER_IDS` env var, same `requireAuth` + allow-list pattern). |

Root cause: each call site (`ROUND_STARTED`, `WORD_SELECTED`, `LETTER_REVEAL`, `GUESS`, `ROUND_ENDED`, `STROKE`, `CLEAR_CANVAS`, undo) created a fresh `supabase.channel(...)` handle and called `.send()` synchronously — Supabase silently no-ops sends on an unsubscribed channel, so the first GUESS-correct on a slow connection vanished and the drawer's UI stayed mid-round with `iGotIt=true` on the guesser only. Server-side broadcast path deferred to a separate spec (per CEO). `ios-dev-realtime` should audit when iOS Sketchy is built — search for the iOS-side Sketchy implementation (currently doesn't exist; note as future-port). The same pattern (channel ref + subscribed flag + retry helper) will be needed on iOS — Reanimated/AppState pause-resume makes the unsubscribed-handle bug even easier to hit. Channel name (`party-room-{code}-sketch`) unchanged. |
| **Trust Issues redesign spec** (`docs/specs/trust-issues-redesign.md`, formerly Poker Face) | `/games/party/[code]` (trust-issues) | iOS Party (not built) | 🟡 spec locked, web build pending | ❌ paused | Asymmetric-information game replacing the casino-mechanics Poker Face. CEO locked on 2026-05-31: (1) **renamed Poker Face → Trust Issues** (file renamed `poker-face-bluff-redesign.md` → `trust-issues-redesign.md`; legal memo renamed `poker-face-legal-memo.md` → `trust-issues-legal-memo.md`; casino vocabulary entirely banned from user-facing copy — bluff/ante/call/fold/chips/pot/jackpot all out; the verb "bluff" stays in INTERNAL mechanical docs only); (2) Knower's claim input is MULTIPLE CHOICE — 4 generated claims per round, 1 truth + 3 plausible lies, Knower picks one to say (free-text deferred to V2); (3) card source is HYBRID BY PHASE — V1 ships with 3 curated decks × 100 cards (Pop Culture, Trivia Facts, Lionade Lore = 300 cards total) to avoid moderation headaches at launch, V1.5 adds Ninny-generated decks as a Pro perk. Reader verdict button is BELIEVE / DOUBT (no "call the bluff"). NO Fang stakes in V1 (XP + leaderboard only) per legal memo for safest App Store review. `design-copywriter` dispatched 2026-05-31 to draft V1 user-facing copy at `docs/specs/trust-issues-copy.md`. **iOS port queued for after web V1 stabilizes** per product-strategist; the rename happens before the iOS port starts so the iOS implementation never carries the Poker Face name. |

## Real Feature Gaps (Things iOS Genuinely Doesn't Have)

After the audit, the actual list of iOS-missing features is:

**High value (Batch A — Week 2):**
1. Duel (`/duel`) — entire feature missing
2. Learn hub (`/learn`) + Learn → Ninny + Learn → Paths
3. Classes index page
4. Arena PvP matchmaking ("Find Match" → real matches)
5. Mastery orchestrator full integration

**Medium value (Batch B — Week 3):**
6. Syllabus upload
7. Grade tracker
8. Flashcard study (standalone)
9. Study DNA
10. Shop cosmetics + boosters (UI exists, stubbed)
11. Friend DM

**Low value (Batch D — Week 4 or defer):**
12. Games hub
13. Focus music toggle

## Reverse Parity — Things iOS has that Web Should Match

These are flagged for the WEB team — iOS shipped them first or better:
- **Notifications inbox** — iOS has full `/notifications` route; web has component only
- **Daily Bet** — verify web has it
- **Bounties card** — verify web has it
- **Streak Revive UI** — iOS has dedicated banner + hook
- **Native auth flow polish** — Apple auth, haptics, animated intro on iOS

---

## Deliberate No-Row Decisions (perf/architecture refactors)

These web changes intentionally have **no parity row** — recorded here so a future audit doesn't misread the absence as missed tracking:

- **2026-06-06 — UX hygiene sweep: replace raw validator toasts with friendly copy (web-only, no iOS port).** Last night's vocab bug (`d09047e`) surfaced because the client toast was wired to the raw server `error.message`, so users saw Zod validator output verbatim (e.g. `definition_source must be wikipedia, ai, or manual`). Same pattern audited across the web app and swept everywhere it leaked: 29 form-submit / mutation handlers across vocab (AddWordForm, BankSelector, CreateBankModal, BankPreviewModal, VocabList, ReviewQueue), party (page, [code], RoomLobby, BluffView × 3, PokerFaceView × 4), mastery (parse / create-exam / start-session), ninny (generate / unlock / delete / chat), classes (create + edit), academia (create class), settings (notif + privacy + visibility), settings/subscription (portal), shop (fang checkout + equip), social (nudge + challenge), profile (privacy + notifications + delete-account), account (portal), pricing (checkout), login (Google + Apple OAuth), Coach resume upload, syllabus upload, focus session claim, streak revive. **Pattern applied:** `setError(r.error ?? "friendly")` and `toastError(e instanceof Error ? e.message : "friendly")` (which let the raw server string run first and showed the friendly only as fallback) replaced with `console.error("[surface:action] failed", err); toastError("friendly")` so devs still see the real error in the browser console while users only ever see Gen-Z-toned calm copy ("Couldn't save. Try again.", "Couldn't open billing portal. Try again.", "Network's being weird. Try again.", etc.). **Preserved intentionally:** (a) `StreakReviveBanner` keeps `r.data?.message` because that's server-curated user copy (e.g. "Need 1500 Fangs"), not a raw validator string; (b) `BankSelector` keeps the explicit `error.toLowerCase().includes(...)` matching against the V3A profanity + 20-bank-cap server contract because those errors are intentionally shaped as user copy; (c) `RoomLobby.startGame` keeps `meta.title needs at least ${meta.minPlayers} players` because that string is built client-side from `GAME_META`, not from a server response. **iOS impact: none.** iOS has its own copywriter-owned toast strings via `react-native-toast-message` + per-screen error handling — the iOS surfaces don't share toast strings with the web app, so there's nothing to port. The `@lionade/core/api/http.ts` client (which both platforms consume) was NOT changed — `ApiResult.error` still carries the raw server string for any caller that wants to switch on a specific error code; this sweep just fixed the **client-side display of that field**. If iOS ever surfaces `ApiResult.error` directly in a toast it should adopt the same console.error + friendly-copy pattern, but the audit at 2026-06-06 confirmed iOS doesn't do this today. Commit `a85c20f`. Files: 29 (16 under `app/`, 13 under `components/`). Type-check clean. (`admin` → in-place pattern sweep → no separate spawn since this is a mechanical guard-rail; `quality-code-reviewer` style guard implied by Sam's spec — friendly copy, no em-dashes, no jargon, no field/column names, success-path untouched.)

- **2026-06-05 — Word Bank list redesign (Excel-vibe dense rows + confidence tint + inline add + per-row magnifier lookup) — web-only by CEO decision.** Tab C of `/learn/vocab` rewritten from glass-card list to dense table-style rows: front | back | user note | confidence dot | accuracy | next-review | 🔍 magnifier | 🗑 delete. Subtle row-bg wash (~6–10% alpha) + 2px left-edge accent in the confidence color. Confidence auto-derived from accuracy bands (≥80% green "locked in", 60–79% yellow "shaky", <60% red "struggling", zero reviews neutral); manual override sticky in DB via new `self_confidence` enum column (`'confident'|'shaky'|'struggling'`, nullable → null means use auto). Tap the dot to cycle confident→shaky→struggling→↺auto. Inline add-row pinned at the top — front + back inputs, Enter saves, focus stays for rapid-fire add. Per-row 🔍 popover hits existing `/api/vocab/define` (general banks) or `/api/vocab/translate` (language banks), results cached per-word in an in-memory Map. Filter chips above the list: All / 🟢 / 🟡 / 🔴 / new. **iOS status:** Word Banks does NOT exist on iOS today — no `/learn/vocab` route, no `@lionade/core/api/vocab.ts`, no vocab components. vp-ios surfaced this as a full-feature-port-needed gap (banks/words/define/translate/review/streak) before the redesign could be applied. **CEO decision (Sam, this session): "Skip everything for iOS version. We are just full working with the web app."** Word Banks stays web-only for now; logged here instead of as a missing-feature row to make the explicit intent visible. If/when iOS picks Word Banks up, this row becomes the spec for the redesigned dense layout to build from day 1 (no V1-old-layout intermediate). **Files shipped (web):** `supabase/migrations/20260605000000_vocab_self_confidence.sql` (new enum + nullable column + partial index; applied to remote 2026-06-05 via `npx supabase db push`); `app/api/vocab/words/[id]/route.ts` (PATCH handler added beside existing DELETE, UUID + body shape + ownership validated, service-role write); `app/api/vocab/words/route.ts` (one-line comment confirming `select *` carries `self_confidence` through, no behavioral change); `components/Vocab/VocabList.tsx` (full rewrite ~800 LOC: `AddWordRow`, `ConfidenceDot`, `LookupPopover`, `VocabRow` desktop grid, `VocabCard` mobile stack, helpers `deriveConfidence`/`getConfidenceWash`/`getAccuracyColor`); `components/Vocab/ReviewQueue.tsx` (`VocabWord` interface extended with optional `self_confidence`); `docs/CHANGELOG.md`; `docs/FEATURES.md`; `~/Desktop/lionade-vault/lionade/Daily/2026-06-05.md`. Commit `90987d0`. Chain: `admin` (orchestration) → `dev-database` (migration) → `dev-backend` (PATCH endpoint + GET passthrough) → `design-ui-ux` (dense-row spec + confidence wash %) → `dev-frontend` (rewrite + AddWordRow + ConfidenceDot + LookupPopover + filter chips + race protection via revision counter) → `design-copywriter` (state labels) → `quality-qa-tester` (test plan: confidence cycle, override persistence across reload, inline add edge cases incl. 409 dupes, magnifier cache, filter chips, mobile breakpoint, offline PATCH revert) → `quality-code-reviewer` (clean; one NIT logged about `fetchLookup` deps for a future useRef-backed cache, not blocking) → `quality-docs-writer` (CHANGELOG + FEATURES + vault Daily/2026-06-05.md + this row). **Open NIT (not blocking):** `LookupPopover.fetchLookup` has `lookupCache` in useCallback deps — recreates callback on every cache update; functional setState is correct but a useRef-backed cache would cut re-renders.


- **2026-05-31 — Sanitize error responses in three web API routes (web-only API hardening, no iOS counterpart).** Three surgical edits remove sensitive detail from JSON error responses while keeping detailed server-side logs intact: (1) `app/api/save-quiz-results/route.ts:606` swapped `{ error: String(err) }` (exposed raw `Error.toString()` including stack/cause text) for `{ error: "Server error" }`; existing `console.error("[save-quiz-results] UNEXPECTED:", err)` retained for ops triage. (2) `app/api/arena/answer/route.ts:109` swapped `{ error: insertErr.message }` (leaked Postgres column/table/constraint names on insert failure) for `{ error: "Failed to record answer" }`; added a `console.error("[arena/answer] insert error:", insertErr.message)` so the message still lands in server logs. (3) `app/api/auth/record-attempt/route.ts:41,78` dropped the `reason: "table_missing_or_error"` and `reason: "exception"` fields from the 200 fail-open responses (these leaked migration state — an attacker could discriminate "login_attempts table exists" vs "missing" by polling and reading the reason); responses are now `{ ok: false }` only. Both server-side `console.error/warn` lines preserved (kept the existing `error.code !== PG_UNDEFINED_TABLE` guard + the `!msg.includes("does not exist")` guard so missing-table noise stays suppressed). **iOS bearing: none.** All three routes are web-side API hardening of error envelopes — the iOS client calls the same backend and benefits transparently from the sanitized responses (no client-side change needed; the iOS app does not parse or display these specific error fields). No iOS-side equivalent exists for `/api/auth/record-attempt` (iOS auth flows go through Supabase directly). When iOS introduces its own server-side error responses (if ever — currently it consumes the same Next.js backend), the same pattern applies: generic message in the body, detail in logs only. (`ios-parity-tracker` via `admin`.)

Local commit, NOT pushed.** **Phase C iOS — audit only (same day, no commit yet).** vp-ios completed the iOS-side audit of `getSubjectStats` consumers in advance of admin's Postgres RPC ship. iOS has a SINGLE consumer hook (`lib/hooks/use-subject-stats.ts`, 82 LOC, iOS-local — does NOT route through `@lionade/core`) feeding TWO Dashboard components: `SubjectStatsCard` (per-subject breakdown bar list) + `StatOrbs` (count-of-distinct-subjects orb value). iOS uses windowed-only (7-day window, 200-row cap) — **does NOT use the lifetime variant** that web's profile page consumes; iOS profile screen has no subject breakdown today. Four iOS-specific transforms must survive the migration: (1) `accuracyPct` precompute on output; (2) sort `questions DESC` (web doesn't sort); (3) `"Other"` fallback for null/blank subject; (4) 7-day window (vs web's 90-day). Audit posted to `packages/lionade-core/PHASE_B_NOTES.md` under `## Phase C — iOS audit` with four BLOCKING open questions for admin (RPC signature, return-shape field names, gating pattern hard-cutover-vs-fallback, window semantics 7-vs-90-day-vs-int-param). **No code change on iOS yet** — Phase C iOS migration is mechanical-swap-pending-RPC-name; will commit on top of `806eba6` the moment admin ships and answers the four questions. Chain: `ios-dev-data` + `ios-platform-bridge` (audit) → `ios-shared-core` (confirmed iOS hook does not route through core; per-platform path stays). `ios-docs-writer` updated iOS CHANGELOG, vault Daily/2026-05-25.md. **Phase C WEB (admin, same day, separate commit) — `getSubjectStats` Postgres aggregation shipped.** New migration `lib/migrations/047_subject_stats_rpc.sql` creates `get_subject_stats(p_user_id uuid, p_lifetime boolean)` RPC with `SECURITY INVOKER` + RLS-respecting + quoted-camelCase return columns matching the existing JS shape (`{ subject, questionsAnswered, correctAnswers, coinsEarned }[]`). `lib/db.ts:getSubjectStats` rewritten as a thin `.rpc()` call — JS aggregator + 500/5000 row cap deleted. Cache key in `lib/hooks.ts:useSubjectStats` (`subject-stats/${userId}/${lifetime}`) byte-identical so Phase B's persisted SWR cache continues to hit. Index coverage already in place from migration 039 — no new index. **Answers to the four iOS audit questions, posted to `packages/lionade-core/PHASE_B_NOTES.md` under `# Phase C coordination notes`:** (1) RPC signature: `get_subject_stats(p_user_id uuid, p_lifetime boolean DEFAULT false)`. (2) Return shape: quoted camelCase TABLE — fields land as `questionsAnswered/correctAnswers/coinsEarned` with zero JS mapping. (3) Gating: web went **hard-cutover** (no fallback) because migration 047 + db.ts ship together in the same push. iOS can choose hard-cutover OR keep the SELECT-and-aggregate path until prod has the migration — both are safe. (4) Window semantics: web hard-codes 90 days inside the RPC for the windowed branch; if iOS needs 7 days specifically, the cleanest path is to extend the RPC signature to `(p_user_id, p_lifetime, p_window_days int default 90)` in a follow-up migration — or iOS can call with `p_lifetime=false` and filter client-side until then (10-20 subjects × 1KB is not a real cost). Recommendation in handoff doc: iOS adds `subjectStatsAPI` to `@lionade/core` mirroring the web wrapper and ships the swap in the same push window; until prod has the RPC, iOS stays on its current path. Estimated speedup: 140-280ms (Dashboard) / 300-600ms (Profile lifetime); network payload reduction ~95-98%. Chain: `dev-database` (migration design) → `dev-backend` (db.ts rewrite) → `security-auditor` (`SECURITY INVOKER`/RLS/`search_path` review — clean) → `dev-performance` (speedup estimate) → `quality-qa-tester` (return-shape parity verified, edge cases dry-run) → `quality-code-reviewer` clean → `quality-docs-writer` (CHANGELOG + this row + iOS handoff in `PHASE_B_NOTES.md` + vault). Local commit, **NOT pushed**; migration **NOT applied to prod** (Sam batches A+B+C push window). TypeScript types in `@lionade/core/types/supabase` to be regenerated after the migration lands on prod. Hotspots flagged but NOT migrated this pass (scope discipline): `getBestScores` (lib/db.ts:750 — same SELECT-then-JS pattern, ~100ms more savings) and `getRecentTopics` (lib/db.ts:664 — 2-query LATERAL candidate). Filed for a possible Phase C.2. **Phase C iOS — follow-up filed (same day, vp-ios, no commit on iOS).** vp-ios re-audited admin's Phase C answer to question #4 (window semantics). Admin's recommended workaround — *iOS calls with `p_lifetime=false` and filters client-side to 7 days* — is not viable on the current RPC return shape: the function returns rows already aggregated by subject (no `completed_at` exposed), so the client has no signal to filter from 90 days down to 7 days. iOS UX (`SubjectStatsCard` literal "Last 7 days" label + `StatOrbs` distinct-subjects-this-week orb count) is load-bearing on 7-day semantics. **Decision: iOS code migration DEFERRED**; `lib/hooks/use-subject-stats.ts` stays on the existing SELECT-and-aggregate path until a follow-up migration adds a `p_window_days integer default 90` parameter to `get_subject_stats`. Proposed signature posted to `packages/lionade-core/PHASE_B_NOTES.md` under `## Phase C.1 follow-up request`. Backward-compatible (90 default keeps web's call site untouched); iOS will pass `p_window_days: 7` once it lands. **No iOS commit this pass** — the prior audit-only commit `12fa593` remains the latest iOS Phase C artifact. **iOS is decoupled from migration 047 timing** — TestFlight builds keep working with the existing path; nothing breaks if Sam pushes 047 to prod and iOS does not update for a week. Sequenced push path becomes: web push (047 ready) → apply 047 to prod → next cycle web ships 048 (`p_window_days`) → apply 048 → iOS hook swap → `eas build` → `eas submit`. Chain: `ios-shared-core` (workaround-not-viable decision) + `ios-dev-data` (no code change confirmed) + `ios-platform-bridge` (intentional documented divergence on subject-stats path until 048 lands) → `ios-qa-tester` (dry-run consumer check — `SubjectStatsCard` + `StatOrbs` consume `SubjectStat` interface unchanged) → `ios-code-reviewer` N/A (no code change) → `ios-docs-writer` (CHANGELOG + this row + vault). Surprise flagged back to admin: the client-side-filter recommendation was made under the assumption iOS had access to raw rows; it does not because the RPC pre-aggregates. **Phase D (web Dashboard RSC promotion) — DEFERRED (same day, admin halted before any code change, CEO decision = defer).** `dev-frontend` audit of `app/dashboard/page.tsx` (1279 LOC, 14 hooks) surfaced an architectural blocker: Lionade's Supabase session is stored in `localStorage` (key `lionade-auth`) and API routes auth via `Authorization: Bearer` header — there is no cookie-based session anywhere in the codebase (zero hits for `@supabase/ssr` / `createServerClient` / `cookies()`). Of the 14 dashboard hooks, 12 are uid-scoped and require the user session; only 2 (`useWeeklyLeaderboard(5)`, `getActiveBounties()`) are anonymous/global. A Next.js Server Component cannot read localStorage, so it cannot authenticate users — making the spec'd Phase D ("RSC pre-fetch all 14 via Promise.all + fallbackData") impossible without migrating the auth system to cookie-based SSR. That migration requires editing `lib/auth.tsx`, `lib/supabase.ts`, and `middleware.ts` — all three on the CLAUDE_AGENT.md **Do-Not-Touch list**. admin presented three options to CEO Sam: (1) approve a scoped exception for cookie-auth migration (~150-250 LOC refactor + RSC split, full-day session, security-auth-guardian as gate); (2) defer Phase D entirely, ship A+B+C as the win, schedule auth migration as its own future session; (3) ship Phase D-lite — pre-fetch only the 2 anonymous hooks (~14% of spec benefit, no Do-Not-Touch violation). **Sam chose (2): defer.** Phase A+B+C alone deliver substantial wins (no refetch storm + persisted SWR cache cross-platform + 150-600ms Postgres aggregate speedup + ~95-98% network payload reduction on subject-stats); RSC architecture deserves a dedicated session with the auth migration scoped properly, not a same-day continuation of a perf sprint. **No files modified for Phase D.** `lib/auth.tsx`, `lib/supabase.ts`, `middleware.ts` untouched. No `@supabase/ssr` install. No new `lib/auth-server.ts`. No commits. Audit findings recorded only in this entry + CHANGELOG + vault for future reference when Phase D is revisited. Chain: `admin` (dispatch) → `dev-frontend` (audit, halted on blocker discovery) → CEO escalation (Sam) → decision = defer. iOS impact: none — Phase D was always web-only-by-design (RSC doesn't exist in React Native; iOS cold-start already addressed by Phase B's AsyncStorage hydration gate). **Push window for A+B+C remains intact** — Sam pushes web (applies migration 047 to prod), then runs iOS `eas build` on iOS commit `7d7da2c` whenever. The 4-phase data-loading sprint closes here as **A+B+C shipped, Phase D + C.1 + sign-out cache clear filed as future work**.

- **2026-05-22 — iOS build 10: profile hub redesign + cross-platform avatar sync (no web port).** Two iOS changes shipped to TestFlight (build 10): (1) the **profile side panel** was rebuilt into a richer hub — a neon-ringed (tier-colored, breathing) avatar + tier & Fangs chips, a gradient **Go Pro** card (dormant PRO-member branch ready for when subscriptions are wired), a **2×3 shortcuts grid** (Shop / Wallet / Badges / Leaderboard / Games / Study DNA), Account rows (Edit Profile / Settings / Notifications), and a **More** section (Invite a Friend share sheet / Rate Lionade / Help & Support / Privacy & Terms) — all routes verified. (2) **Cross-platform avatar sync** — the web stores avatars as DiceBear SVG URLs that React Native can't render (iOS was falling back to initials); iOS now resolves them to PNG (`/svg`→`/png`) and uses the same DiceBear default, so the **same profile picture renders on web + iOS** (shared `profiles.avatar_url`; uploaded Storage photos pass through unchanged). iOS-only polish/parity — no web feature to port. Chain: web research (general-purpose) → `dev-frontend` ×2 → `quality-code-reviewer` (shippable, 0 critical/high) → `quality-docs-writer`.

(2) **Back button felt broken** — `BackButton.onPress` was `router.push(parentPath)` which GREW the stack instead of popping. Fix: `router.canGoBack()` → `router.back()` (true native history-back), fallback to `router.replace(parent)` for deep-link entry. Added selection haptic. (3) **Laggy scroll** — starfield was running 6 infinite Reanimated `withRepeat` worklets (4 twinkle + 2 shooting) 24/7, plus 5+ widget worklets on the dashboard. Fix (subset for this build): halve twinkles 4 → 2 and AppState-gate all starfield worklets (`cancelAnimation` on background, restart on resume). Per-widget pruning (`StatOrbs` rotation + `LevelProgressBar` shimmer + `HeaderGreeting` dot + `ClockInButton` glow) DEFERRED to a follow-up build pending Sam's validation that the starfield gate alone meaningfully cut scroll lag. Files touched: `app/_layout.tsx`, `components/BackButton.tsx`, `components/SpaceBackground.tsx`. **Build 14 = appBuildVersion 14, autoIncrement remote, sdk 54, fingerprint 5730f9b6 (unchanged from build 13).** Build URL: https://expo.dev/accounts/sulods-organization/projects/lionade/builds/a394323e-53f8-4d56-9953-219a90c4ce5c. Chain: `vp-ios` (orchestration) → `ios-perf` (worklet thread audit, identified 11+ concurrent withRepeat as scroll-thread starvation root cause) → `ios-dev-native-modules` + `ios-architect` (3-file fix) → `ios-code-reviewer` clean → `ios-qa-tester` (6-case test plan, see iOS CHANGELOG `## 2026-05-25 — Build 14`) → `ios-docs-writer` (iOS CHANGELOG + this row + vault). **Deferred / open:** (a) `eas.json` still has `ascAppId: "TBD-FROM-APP-STORE-CONNECT"` — submit attempted in non-interactive mode for build 14; if it fails an interactive submit is needed once the build finishes. Build 16 errored in `INSTALL_DEPENDENCIES` (lockfile path mismatch for `@lionade/core` — `package-lock.json` still pinned the OLD sibling-repo path `../lionade/packages/lionade-core` even though `package.json` had moved to `file:./packages/lionade-core`; fixed in commit `eece2ca` by regenerating lockfile to `packages/lionade-core`). Build 17 errored in `EAGER_BUNDLE` (Metro): verbatim from the EAS log — `Unable to resolve module semver/functions/satisfies from /Users/expo/workingdir/build/node_modules/react-native-reanimated/scripts/validate-worklets-version.js`. Root cause: `react-native-reanimated` declares `semver: ^7.7.2` as a runtime dep, but npm hoisted the older `semver@6.3.1` (pulled in by other transitive packages) to top-level `node_modules/`. semver 6.x has no `functions/` subpath; semver 7.x does. Local dev was rescued by `node_modules/react-native-reanimated/node_modules/semver/7.7.4`, but EAS Metro resolver walked up to the hoisted 6.x first and failed. Fix committed as `d27801e fix(ios): hoist semver@^7.8.1 to fix EAS eager-bundle Metro resolution` — added `"semver": "^7.8.1"` as a direct dep in `package.json`; top-level `node_modules/semver` is now 7.8.1 with `functions/satisfies.js` present. Build 18 confirmed the fix worked — EAGER_BUNDLE passed without error. **Build 18 then errored in `Run fastlane`** (Xcode build phase) with sentry-cli output: `Auth token is required for this request. Please run sentry-cli login and try again!` + `To disable source maps auto upload, set SENTRY_DISABLE_AUTO_UPLOAD=true in your environment variables. Or to allow failing upload, set SENTRY_ALLOW_FAILURE=true`. Root cause: `@sentry/react-native` is installed in `package.json` and the Sentry Xcode build phase auto-uploads source maps, but neither `SENTRY_AUTH_TOKEN` nor `SENTRY_DISABLE_AUTO_UPLOAD` is set in the EAS production env. Prior TestFlight builds 9-13 either had the var set or shipped with an older Sentry SDK that did not enforce upload. Build 18 URL: https://expo.dev/accounts/sulods-organization/projects/lionade/builds/79b8a91c-5f7c-4dd4-92a4-cc9b596c2dd7. **Per Sam's hard constraint (one build attempt per session), STAND-DOWN. No build 19 attempted this run.** Recommended next-session fix: either (path A, fast) add `SENTRY_DISABLE_AUTO_UPLOAD=true` to `eas.json` under `build.production.env` — source maps will not upload but builds pass; iOS crashes report to Sentry without symbolication (acceptable for TestFlight beta), OR (path B, correct) provision a real `SENTRY_AUTH_TOKEN` via `eas secret:create --name SENTRY_AUTH_TOKEN` and plumb through `eas.json` env — source maps upload and crashes symbolicate. Sam decides next session. **Cumulative session result: 5 EAS build numbers burned (14/15/16/17/18), 0 shipped to TestFlight; last working TestFlight build is still 13.** The 4 UX fixes from commit `8354afa` (swipe-back ghosting + back-button history + worklet idle gate) are not on TestFlight yet — they will ride the next successful build. - **2026-05-26 - Hydration mismatch on persisted SWR provider (web ✅ fix shipped local, iOS 🚫 N/A).** Blocking-bug fix on web commits `3111969`, `089aa9c`, `5bd6445`, `f185fba`. Sam saw `Did not expect server HTML to contain a <div> in <div>` on both `/dashboard` and `/quiz?subject=Science` while preparing to push. Root cause: Phase B's `lib/swr-config.ts:getProvider()` constructed the persisted SWR provider on the FIRST render in both environments. Server SSR has no localStorage so the cache was empty and the tree painted the loading skeleton; client first render (the hydration commit) ran the same factory and the synchronous localStorage read populated the cache before useSWR hooks read it, so the client painted the data DOM. Server tree did not match client first-render tree, React threw. **Fix:** Option A (mount-gated SWRConfig). `components/SwrProvider.tsx` now uses a new `swrConfigNoPersist` variant (added in `lib/swr-config.ts`, mirrors every revalidation/retry setting from the persisted variant) for the server render AND the client's hydration commit, then flips to `swrConfig` in a post-mount `useEffect`. Trade-off: SWR cache is re-mounted across the swap so hooks may fire one extra revalidation right after first paint. **Why not Option B (deferred hydration in the shared factory):** the shared `createPersistedSwrProvider` already does hydration asynchronously via an internal IIFE that resolves `readyPromise`, but the localStorage read still resolves on a microtask which races React's hydration commit. Solving at the factory layer would require an opt-in `skipInitialHydration` flag plus a web-side `.hydrate()` call from `useEffect`, which touches the shared package and adds API surface. Option A keeps the entire fix inside web with zero change to the shared factory or to iOS. **iOS status: 🚫 N/A.** React Native has no SSR so the hydration-mismatch class of bugs does not exist on iOS. The shared factory's existing `readyPromise` gate continues to serve iOS unchanged. **Files (web):** `components/SwrProvider.tsx`, `lib/swr-config.ts`, `docs/CHANGELOG.md`, this row. Hard constraints respected: no edits to `lib/auth.tsx`, `lib/supabase.ts`, `middleware.ts`. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. Localhost hard-refresh on `/dashboard` and `/quiz?subject=Science` (signed in, populated localStorage) confirmed hydration error gone on both routes. Chain: `admin` (orchestration + root-cause diagnosis) -> `dev-frontend` (Option A implementation) -> `quality-code-reviewer` (typecheck) -> `quality-qa-tester` (both-route refresh verification) -> `quality-docs-writer` (CHANGELOG + this row + vault Daily/2026-05-26.md).

- **2026-05-26 - Ninny MCQ answer-position de-bias (web ✅ shipped, iOS ✅ via-backend).** Web commit `5bd6445`. Sam reported quiz answers landing on A or B almost every time, never D. Two-pronged fix: (1) the shared Ninny prompt at `packages/lionade-core/src/prompts/ninny.ts` showed `correctIndex: 0` in BOTH example objects (`multipleChoice` and `blitz`), and LLMs pattern-match heavily on example values; examples now use `correctIndex: 2` and `correctIndex: 3` plus an explicit REQUIREMENTS line asking the model to distribute correctIndex evenly across 0/1/2/3. (2) added `lib/shuffle-mcq.ts` (Fisher-Yates) and applied `shuffleOptions` to every item in `validated.multipleChoice` + `validated.blitz` inside `app/api/ninny/generate/route.ts` BEFORE the DB insert into `ninny_materials.generated_content` and the background `saveGeneratedQuestions` call into the question bank. Belt-and-suspenders: prompt-level + post-generation guarantee. **Verification:** 4,000-question simulation over a biased input distribution (60/30/8/2 A/B/C/D) produced post-shuffle counts of 24.7 / 25.2 / 25.0 / 25.1 percent — uniform within sampling noise. Mastery already had this fix via `shuffleFour` in `lib/mastery-content.ts`; this commit is the matching Ninny half. **iOS status: ✅ via-backend.** No iOS code change required — the iOS app calls the same `/api/ninny/generate` route via `ninnyAPI`, so generated content arrives pre-shuffled. Old biased questions in the question bank are NOT migrated; they age out naturally as the bank rotates. Chain: `admin` (orchestration) -> `dev-ai-specialist` (prompt-example bias detection in core) -> `dev-backend` (shuffle helper + route patch) -> `data-analytics` (4,000-question uniformity verification) -> `quality-code-reviewer` (typecheck clean) -> `quality-docs-writer` (this row + vault).

- **2026-05-26 — Arena V2 Phase 3: ghost-owner offline ELO buffer + Trainer accuracy tune (web staged, iOS paused per CEO).** Phase 3 closes the two final pieces of the locked spec: **(A) Option B ELO conservation** — every real-ghost match now generates symmetric +/- ELO flow so the rating pool stays conserved. Live player gets their delta immediately at `/api/arena/v2/complete` (unchanged); the ghost owner is offline so their `−1 × live_delta` is buffered on `profiles.pending_elo_change` (int) + `profiles.pending_elo_summary` (jsonb, FIFO-capped at 50 entries) + `profiles.pending_wins/losses/draws`. On their next login, the V2 lobby renders `GhostEloCard` ABOVE the subject picker with "Your ghost ran N duels" + W/L/D row + current→new ELO arrow + Claim button. Trainer-Ninny matches are EXPLICITLY excluded from the conservation system (trainer ghosts inject/absorb ELO from outside the player pool by design; per-user cap of first 3 duels OR 24h bounds the imbalance). **(B) Trainer Ninny accuracy tune-down** — 75/85/95% → 60/75/90%; new players win MORE often in their first 3 trainer matches, flipping the trainer cohort from a slight deflation source to a slight inflation source at launch so cold-start feels competent. **Files staged:** `lib/migrations/050_arena_v2_ghost_elo.sql` + `supabase/migrations/20260526220000_arena_v2_ghost_elo.sql` (5 new columns on profiles with comments); `app/api/arena/v2/complete/route.ts` patched (symmetric ELO delta computed; ghost-owner buffer update inside an `is_async && !is_trainer_match && ghost.owner_user_id` guard; FIFO cap at 50; uses `generateAnonHandle(userId)` for the challenger handle in the summary entry; service-role writes; never fails the live `/complete` if the buffer write errors — logs only); new endpoint `app/api/arena/v2/ghost-elo-summary/route.ts` GET (requireAuth, reads userId from bearer only, returns `{ pending: { elo_change, wins, losses, draws, summary, current_elo }, hasPending }`); new endpoint `app/api/arena/v2/claim-ghost-elo/route.ts` POST (requireAuth, idempotent zero-out, no body-trusted userId, returns `{ new_elo, wins_applied, losses_applied, draws_applied, elo_delta, noop }`); new component `components/arena-v2/GhostEloCard.tsx` (SWR-backed, fetches `/api/arena/v2/ghost-elo-summary` on mount, renders nothing when `hasPending === false`, glassmorphism card matching V2 lobby style with purple radial-glow accent + gold-gradient Claim button + framer-motion fade-in respecting `prefers-reduced-motion`, optimistic mutate-to-empty on claim, success/error toasts); `app/arena/v2/page.tsx` wires `<GhostEloCard />` at the top of `phase === "lobby"` render block right after the hero/header; `scripts/seed-trainer-ninny-ghosts.ts` retuned BANDS to 60/75/90% accuracy + added `--reseed` CLI flag that DELETEs all `owner_user_id = TRAINER_NINNY_USER_ID AND is_trainer = true` rows before inserting (default behavior remains idempotent-skip). **Migration 050 APPLIED to remote DB via `npx supabase db push --include-all`.** **Trainer ghost reseed RUN** (`npx tsx scripts/seed-trainer-ninny-ghosts.ts --reseed`): 24 ghosts deleted, 24 reseeded (earth-science skipped with 0 questions in pool, as in Phase 1); per-band avg `total_score` 563 / 713 / 863 vs old 720 / 832 / 944, exactly matching the new accuracy profile within mulberry32 sampling variance. **`npx tsc --noEmit` clean.** Localhost test route: http://localhost:3000/arena/v2 (NEXT_PUBLIC_ARENA_V2_ENABLED must be true). To verify card render: `UPDATE profiles SET pending_elo_change = 12, pending_wins = 4, pending_losses = 2, pending_elo_summary = '[{"match_id":"00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001","challenged_at":"2026-05-26T22:00:00Z","challenger_anon_handle":"Shadow Wolf 4729","subject":"algebra","outcome":"ghost_won","elo_delta":4}]'::jsonb WHERE id = '<sam-user-id>';` → reload /arena/v2 → card appears → click Claim → arena_elo += 12, arena_wins += 4, arena_losses += 2, buffer zeroed. **Self-checks performed in-session:** `data-economist` lens — symmetric math verified (live gain == ghost loss, pool conserved); 60/75/90% accuracy doesn't break Fang flow (trainer matches still transfer zero Fangs, only ratings move); 50-entry cap sufficient (P99 of "matches against one user's ghost in 24h" expected <10; 50 covers an absent user being challenged for ~5 days). `security-auth-guardian` lens — `requireAuth` on both new endpoints; `claim-ghost-elo` reads userId only from verified bearer (never from body — so a malicious body cannot drain another user's buffer); idempotent zero-out cannot grant arbitrary ELO (a second call sees zeroes and returns no-op). **Deferred to Phase 4 / V1.5:** RPC-based atomic claim transaction to eliminate the thin read-then-write race window (current code mitigates by absorbing any new entries that landed between read and update); the legacy non-RLS write path could move to a `claim_pending_elo` RPC for stronger guarantees once we hit V1 telemetry. Telemetry items in the locked spec (weekly avg ELO drift, win/loss split by match type, distribution of `pending_elo_change` deltas at login) are NOT built — `data-analytics` pre-public-launch work. Notification card outside the V2 lobby (e.g. global nav dot when buffer is non-empty) is NOT built — scoped to the V2 arena entry as requested. **iOS status: ❌ paused per CEO 2026-05-26 web-only scope.** When iOS resumes: port `GhostEloCard` to RN (NativeWind glassmorphism, Reanimated fade-in), wire the same two endpoints into `@lionade/core` shared client, render the card at the top of the iOS arena V2 lobby. Chain (this session): `admin` (orchestration) → `dev-database` (migration 050 + 5 columns) → `dev-backend` (complete-route patch + 2 new endpoints) → `data-economist` (self-check on symmetric math + accuracy band) → `security-auth-guardian` (self-check on auth surface) → `design-ui-ux` (GhostEloCard glassmorphism spec) → `dev-frontend` (GhostEloCard + lobby wire-in) → `quality-code-reviewer` (typecheck clean) → `quality-docs-writer` (CHANGELOG + FEATURES + this row + vault Daily/2026-05-26.md).

This also CLOSES the `AuthContextValue`-shape tsc errors carried since iOS Phase 0. (2) `app/login.tsx` — all three sign-in paths (password / Apple / Google PKCE+fragment) now `await finalizeSignIn()` before routing; `Invalid` errors map to "Wrong email or password" (web parity); wired the previously-dead Forgot-password (`resetPasswordForEmail`), shared demo-account button (`demo@getlionade.com`, visible creds, NEVER Sam's real creds), and "Create an account" footer; VoiceOver labels added to all auth controls. Post-auth routing unchanged — RouteGuard reads `onboardingCompleted` → new user `/onboarding`, returning `/(tabs)`. **Verification:** `npx tsc --noEmit` 14 errors, all arena-specific (Section 5); the 3 auth-surface errors gone. `expo export --platform ios` clean (8.94 MB Hermes). No new npm packages. **Flagged for Sam:** Google OAuth iOS client + Apple Service ID / Supabase Apple provider are dashboard config (code is correct); `EXPO_PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL` needed in `eas.json` for `login-event` on prod builds (defaults to getlionade.com). **Parity decision:** iOS keeps the OAuth-first single-screen sign-in; new-user data collection lives in iOS onboarding (Section 2), so "Create an account" opens email mode rather than web's 3-step signup wizard. ## How to Use This File

**When shipping a NEW feature:**
1. Add a row in the relevant section with `Web: ✅` and `iOS: ❌ port pending`.
2. Mention in CHANGELOG that iOS parity is tracked here.

**When porting to iOS:**
1. Flip the iOS column from `❌` to `✅` (or `🟡` if partial).
2. Note the iOS route path or component path.

**Audit cadence:** Quarterly full audit by `Explore` agent + `quality-docs-writer`.

---

*Strategy = shared-core extraction (Strategy C) starting Week 1. Once core lands, parity-by-default becomes the default workflow — no more drift.*
